## AFF-01 法兰西特快 / The French Express

**？？？**：就不能麻利点吗，阿黛拉？堵车，罢工……我受够了！\
**???**: Must we really sit here, Adèle? I have had quite enough—strikes and traffic everywhere!

**阿黛拉**：玛莱区的街道是有些窄，这没办法。至少我们已经到了地方……\
**Adèle**: Oh, well, yes, this isn't Versailles, madame. The streets in Le Marais are always a tight squeeze. Besides, we're almost there.

**阿黛拉**：那间沙龙应该就在楼上。还好孚日广场附近人不多。\
**Adèle**: I believe the salon should be right above us, in one of these buildings. The traffic might thin once we're near Place des Vosges.

**？？？**：当然，亲爱的司机小姐，你宝贵的车只有德佩区的宽阔大道才配得上——我的东西呢？\
**???**: These streets were never the problem, my dear. Perhaps you'd prefer a client that lets you drive on the boulevards of Saint-Germain-des-Prés instead. Now, did you bring what I asked?

金属碰撞声和细碎的摩擦声证明了司机的努力。\
The faint clinking of metal reveals the driver's effort.

**阿黛拉**：——在这儿！我找到了，完美无损！\
**Adèle**: Voilà! It survived all the bumps!

**阿黛拉**：我不得不再次提出那个老问题，费利西安小姐。\
**Adèle**: I know what you'll say, Madame Félicienne, but I must ask again.

**阿黛拉**：咱们一定得带着这种易碎的甜点到处跑吗？\
**Adèle**: Do we really need to carry these pastries around with us?

**费利西安**：你稍作努力，让拉杜丽开遍全巴黎，自然就不必这样麻烦。\
**Félicienne**: Not at all. Provided you ensure there's always a Ladurée around the corner.

**阿黛拉**：您真是高看我了——喔，我们还提前了十分钟，可以慢慢走上楼。\
**Adèle**: If only that were in my power, madame. Oh look, we're here, and with time to spare. Great, no need to rush.

这段时间以来，她已经习惯了这位小姐的脾气，也熟练掌握了让对方消气的技巧。\
By now, she's used to her employer's temperament and knows exactly how to calm her down.

**阿黛拉**：全怪我考虑得不够周到。明天我来接您之前，先去一趟香榭丽舍大街……\
**Adèle**: I'll be sure to make some adjustments before tomorrow. Maybe stop by the Champs-Élysées and get those macarons you like before picking you up.

**费利西安**：你知道就好。走吧，今天你选的这条近道还不错，总算没有迟到。\
**Félicienne**: That will do nicely. Now, shall we go in? You worked hard to find that shortcut. Let's not squander our timeliness.

这句话多少给疲惫的司机提供了几分动力。

她关上车门，张开双臂转了个得意的圈儿。\
The remark gives the weary driver just enough motivation. She closes the door and spins around with a proud flourish.

**阿黛拉**：看吧，我接下您的单子时可没胡说。\
**Adèle**: See? Just like I said from the start—

**阿黛拉**：“整个巴黎的一切，全都在我脑袋里头！”\
**Adèle**: "I know Paris like the back of my hand!"

**？？？**：吾等本为虚无。永远的国度、权柄与荣耀，皆归于祢——\
**???**: Thou art the Kingdom and the Power and the Glory.

（ATAH MAKUTH VE-GEBURAH VE-GEDULAH)

**？？？**：永世无尽，阿门。\
**???**: Forever. Amen.

(LE-OLAHM AMEN)

香棒在静室中燃烧，乳香、没药与鸢尾根的气味漫散开来，所有人都屏息注视着位于中央的女子。\
Soft smoke fills the chamber, tinged with frankincense, myrrh, and iris root. Gathered onlookers hold their breath in silence, all eyes fixed on the woman in the center.

她神情肃穆，口中念念有词。在用一根一半白色、一半黑色的朴素术杖分别向四个方向画出五芒星的图案后，她向两侧伸出双臂。\
She murmurs under her breath as she produces a simple wand, half white and half black, tracing pentagrams in each cardinal direction as she throws open her arms.

**雷曼女士**：拉斐尔，在我面前现身。加百列，在我身后现身。米迦勒，在我右手侧现身。乌列尔，在我左手侧现身——\
**Madame Raymond**: Before me, Raphael. Behind me, Gabriel. At my right hand, Michael. At my left hand, Auriel.

**雷曼女士**：五芒星在此熊熊燃烧，六芒星于光柱中闪耀！\
**Madame Raymond**: Before me flames the pentagram. Behind me shines the six-rayed star!

随着她顿挫的声音落下，熏香燃烧着的火焰忽地明亮了一瞬。\
Her deep voice trails off, and the burning incense flares bright like a guiding star in the dim room.

**雷曼女士**：我看见了……我看见了那自北方出现的旋风、巨云，以及向内侧熊熊燃烧的火焰……\
**Madame Raymond**: Shown to me ... This, I see ... The whirlwind in the north, the giant cloud, and the blazing flames ...

**雷曼女士**：那万丈光辉，正是祂之智慧在地上的显现。\
**Madame Raymond**: Through the stifling cloud comes light, a piercing flame, a manifestation of divine wisdom.

**妇人**：怎么样，雷曼女士？您是否……\
**Lady Visitor**: And what, madame? What do you see? Do you ...

**雷曼女士**：我已自星界请来了四位大天使在此投下他们的化身，他们将借予我力量，令我可以一窥那意象宝库中的秘密。\
**Madame Raymond**: Four angels have answered and four aids given so that I may glimpse the secrets of the Archive of Imagery.

**雷曼女士**：您的丈夫不知踪迹，但他的影子仍在家中徘徊。\
**Madame Raymond**: Your husband is nowhere to be seen. Yet his shadow lingers still in the house.

**妇人**：——！\
**Lady Visitor**: ...!

**妇人**：是的……是的！您说得对！\
**Lady Visitor**: Yes. Yes! How did you know that?

**妇人**：我总能感觉到……有时还能看见他的身影！就穿着那件土黄的大衣……\
**Lady Visitor**: Sometimes I feel his presence. I ... I see him in that khaki coat.

妇人急切地凑上前去，紧紧扒住占卜桌的边沿。\
The woman rushes forward, gripping tightly at the edge of the divination table.

**妇人**：我请求您，女士！请告诉我他究竟遇到了什么？要怎样才能让他回来？\
**Lady Visitor**: Madame, please! What's happened to him? How do I bring him home?

妇人的话让阿黛拉皱起眉头。她压低声音，让自己的话混入台下的议论声中。\
Adèle frowns. She lowers her voice into a whisper that blends into the other murmurs in the room.

**阿黛拉**：她说的是最近的失踪案。有不少人都想找大人物们要一个解释。\
**Adèle**: Poor woman. Sounds like her husband's gone missing. Just one of who knows how many others that have lost someone lately.

**阿黛拉**：但解释可没那么好找，我的警察朋友忙活了半天也没见有结果。你觉得这位占卜师会怎么说？\
**Adèle**: You know, my friend in the police told me there hasn't been any progress on these cases. If only it were as easy as all this. What do you think she'll tell her?

**费利西安**：大概是诅咒或者恶魔附体一类的。总是这些。\
**Félicienne**: That it's a curse, a demonic possession, or some such nonsense. That's the usual prattle anyway.

占卜师朝满眼恳切的妇人点了点头，转身面向台下众人。\
The diviner gives a small nod to the pleading woman and turns to face her audience.

**雷曼女士**：这位可怜女子的丈夫遭到了诅咒——一头野兽的诅咒！\
**Madame Raymond**: He is bound by a curse—held fast in the claws of a monstrosity!

**雷曼女士**：它未能诞生自温暖的血肉之中，而是由笼罩这座城市的黑暗孵化而生。\
**Madame Raymond**: A beast born of no mortal womb, a foul creature of darkness, nurtured by the shadows that cloak this city!

**雷曼女士**：旧的秩序崩坏已久，新的乐园却迟迟没能得到兑现。魔鬼从未走远，它们在我们的近旁虎视眈眈，蛊惑每一个摇摆的灵魂……\
**Madame Raymond**: The old order has been shattered, yet there has been nothing to take its place. We are without shelter, and the beasts are circling, sniffing, coveting our troubled souls.

**雷曼女士**：于是它才自百年的沉睡中苏醒，现身于这个时代，将苦痛施加于众人！\
**Madame Raymond**: They have awakened from their centuries-long slumber, bringing torment upon us! We have called them forth. We have set loose this horror: the Beasts of Gévaudan!

是我们唤醒了它——那热沃当的野兽！

那个不祥的名字令屋内瞬间安静下来。\
An ominous pall falls over the room at the sound of its name, like a taboo has been broken. The murmurs stop. Breath stops. The pause holds tension like a breaking dam until gasps pierce through one by one.

人们屏住呼吸，半晌后掺着恐惧的惊呼声才小心翼翼地响起。

**参会者Ⅰ**：怪不得总有隆隆怪响……是那些黑影回来了！\
**Participant I**: So that's what those rumblings were. The shadows have returned!

**参会者Ⅱ**：难道我铺子里那些不来干活的家伙，也是——\
**Participant II**: Maybe that's what happened to my missing workers.

**阿黛拉**：好吧，你猜对了。又是老一套，“诅咒”。\
**Adèle**: Ah, bravo, madame. "It's a curse," just as you said! The same old rubbish.

**阿黛拉**：要是这种东西真的存在，我的家族根本就传不到我这一代。\
**Adèle**: If curses were half as powerful as people think, my family and I would've been snuffed out long ago.

**费利西安**：少说我不爱听的。你死了谁来给我开车？\
**Félicienne**: Spare me the morbid talk, would you? How would I ever get around without my driver?

她抛下这句话，转过头盯着台上的占卜师，不再理会不懂事的司机。\
She throws out the remark, then turns a sharp glance to the diviner on stage.

**雷曼女士**：我无法消灭那只野兽，它实在过于强大。\
**Madame Raymond**: I cannot expel the beast. It is beyond my power.

**雷曼女士**：但我可以限制那诅咒的效力，削弱它的影响。\
**Madame Raymond**: But I do have some means to sap its strength.

等在一旁的学徒适时地为她捧上许多小物件。\
Her apprentice steps up at once, holding out several small items.

一块刻有奇妙符号的水晶，以及墨水、白蜡烛与黑色丝绸。\
A crystal etched with a strange symbol, ink, white candles, and a strip of black silk.

**雷曼女士**：天上如此，地下亦然。一切存在都彼此相连，万物在这条永恒的巨链中均有自己的位置。\
**Madame Raymond**: Our world mirrors the one above, bound in its reflection. All things find their place in the Great Chain of Being.

**雷曼女士**：有时，我们能够自那些更加完美的存在处借来些许力量。\
**Madame Raymond**: Sometimes, powers may be drawn from those higher along the Chain.

**雷曼女士**：我将借助来自土星的智性，为你制作一块能够限制诅咒的灵摆。佩戴它一段时日，你的丈夫将会归来。\
**Madame Raymond**: From Saturn, I ask for knowledge and insight. And with its power, I offer you this pendulum. Keep it close, and your husband will find his way home.

**妇人**：好的，好的！太感谢您了！\
**Lady Visitor**: Thank you! Thank you, madame! There are no words!

费利西安的耐心只够坚持到听完这段话。\
Félicienne's patience lasts only long enough to hear that much.

她悄无声息地起身，阿黛拉也紧跟着迈出步子。\
She rises silently, and Adèle follows close behind.

**费利西安**：我还以为能在这里听到些新鲜的神秘学理论，或者有意思的八卦……没想到是无聊套话而已。\
**Félicienne**: I was hoping to hear some insights on arcane study or at least some decent gossip. Had I known it was just some poseur selling tired old charms, I wouldn't have bothered.

**阿黛拉**：所以我才说，巴黎好玩的地方多的是，想逛街有老佛爷百货公司，各种小玩意都在圣图安市场，没必要特地赶过来看这种……好吧，演出。\
**Adèle**: There are still plenty of places in Paris worth a visit! If you're in the mood for fashion, there's the Galeries Lafayette Haussmann. Or for antiques and curiosities, we might try le Marché aux Puces de Saint-Ouen. Something to take your mind off this, erm, "performance."

人群已经涌向前去，争着向占卜师寻求解答。只有少数人像她们一样打算退场。\
The crowd surges forward, eager for answers. Though a few, like them, slip quietly out from the scene.

尽管没人会在意，阿黛拉还是压低了声音。\
Though it seems unlikely anyone would notice, Adèle still lowers her voice.

**阿黛拉**：下次就考虑我的建议……\
**Adèle**: Perhaps next time, we could go with my—

**费利西安**：我已经买下了你的时间，你的工作就是陪同我去城里任何一个我想去的地方。\
**Félicienne**: Your hours are paid for. You'll take me wherever I like.

**阿黛拉**：好吧。我投降。一切都按您的意见办。\
**Adèle**: Fine. As you say, madame. I shouldn't overstep.

阿黛拉总结出的应对技巧并不会每次都起效。\
Her usual approach is anything but foolproof. Félicienne stops mid-step, giving her a half-smile.

费利西安停下脚步，似笑非笑地望向她。

**费利西安**：观赏闹剧也算是一种消遣。再说……\
**Félicienne**: These cheap stunts are just a harmless little diversion. Besides ...

**费利西安**：你对这类“占卜”也并不是全无兴趣。比如，《高等魔法的教义与仪式》？\
**Félicienne**: I believe I'm not the only one who's taken an interest. How have you been finding Dogme et rituel de la haute magie?

**阿黛拉**：呃！那些书都是看着玩……而且你怎么知道的？\
**Adèle**: Ah! How did you know about that? I'm just reading it for fun.

**费利西安**：“看着玩”。对，在每一个“家族诅咒”词条下面画上红色波浪线，你就喜欢玩这个。\
**Félicienne**: Fun, is it? And what about those red squiggles you circled around every entry about generational curses?

**阿黛拉**：你看到过？嘿，你究竟怎么知道的？快告诉我！\
**Adèle**: Ah. How on—Did you go through my things? Oh, come on. Tell me!

对于占卜沙龙的主办者来说，这番喧闹的景象或许过于显眼了。\
Their small commotion draws just enough attention to catch the diviner's eye.

**雷曼女士**：这位小姐，请暂留脚步。\
**Madame Raymond**: Madame, please stay just a moment longer.

**雷曼女士**：迷途的乌云和执妄的枷锁正笼罩着你……你已灾厄缠身，而我能拨开你的迷雾。\
**Madame Raymond**: I see ... clouds and chains around you ... the bonds of one led astray, shackled by fixation ... I might offer some clarity.

**雷曼女士**：请靠近些，让我能看得更清楚。\
**Madame Raymond**: Come closer so that I may see you better.

直到所有目光都汇聚过来，阿黛拉才明白占卜师指的正是她们中的一个。\
Only as every eye in the room turns their way does Adèle realize she is talking to one of them.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安，她让你……\
**Adèle**: Félicienne, I think she's talking to you.

**雷曼女士**：是的，这位正四处张望的小姐。我希望您能上前来。\
**Madame Raymond**: I'm speaking to you, madame. No need to look about. Please, come forward.

**阿黛拉**：我？\
**Adèle**: Me?

阿黛拉看向费利西安，后者像是突然提起了兴趣，轻轻推了她一把。\
She looks at Félicienne, who, now quite suddenly intrigued by the scene, nudges her driver forward.

**费利西安**：就是你了，别傻站着。既然她自己找上门，那就让她见识见识你的本事。\
**Félicienne**: Yes, you, Adèle. Well, don't just stand there. Go on! Show her what's what.

**阿黛拉**：……好吧。\
**Adèle**: *sigh* Okay.

在众人的注视下，她站到了占卜师对面，将手伸向桌上的灵摆。\
Feeling the weight of the gawking crowd, she stands across from the diviner and reaches for the pendulum on the table.

**阿黛拉**：说实话，女士，我对您的占卜不感兴趣，您这些小伎俩也唬不到我……\
**Adèle**: Forgive me, madame, but I have no interest in divination. And I didn't come here for any advice, either.

**阿黛拉**：但我可不希望被您当做打响名号的幌子。\
**Adèle**: Frankly, I find it difficult to watch you take advantage of all these people.

她拿起水晶，对着一旁的烛火照了照。\
She lifts the crystal and holds it up to the candlelight.

**阿黛拉**：通透纯净、手感温和……本来是枚不错的水晶。\
**Adèle**: Excellent clarity, smooth to the touch. Hmph. A fine crystal at first glance.

**阿黛拉**：——可惜它的颜色太过均匀，一点包裹体和裂隙都没有，显然有人动过手脚。\
**Adèle**: But there's something else—the evenness of its hue and that flawless sheen. Nothing is ever this perfect.

**妇人**：什么？可是……可是……\
**Lady Visitor**: Whatever do you mean? But ...

**阿黛拉**：很快您就会知道它的真假。\
**Adèle**: Let's put it through a little test, shall we?

一条小龙在眨眼间从她的袖口探出头。\
A small dragon pokes its head out from her sleeve as if on cue.

**阿黛拉**：唯以真知炼化虚妄。\
**Adèle**: By fire, what is false is purged.

火光一闪，近旁的妇人并未感受到任何高温，而原本美丽的宝石已经变回了丑陋破碎的残次品。\
Flames flicker, yet the woman feels no heat. Though the once-beautiful crystal has been rendered into dull, broken shards.

小龙灵巧地攀到阿黛拉肩膀上，得到了赞许的抚摸。\
The little dragon climbs nimbly onto Adèle's shoulder and tilts its head to receive a gentle pat of approval.

**阿黛拉**：干得好，小家伙。\
**Adèle**: Bravo, Feufeu.

围观的人群骚动起来，阿黛拉满意地捕捉到几句惊叹。\
The crowd stirs, and Adèle catches a few gasps of awe with satisfaction.

**妇人**：您把它——\
**Lady Visitor**: What have you done to my crystal?

**阿黛拉**：不必慌张，夫人。我是阿黛拉·塔沃尼尔——就是那个盛产宝石猎人的塔沃尼尔家。也许您曾听过我先祖的名号。\
**Adèle**: Please, allow me to explain. My name is Adèle Tavernier. Have you heard of us before? Les Taverniers? Famed jewel hunters?

**阿黛拉**：他们曾为路易十四寻回过法兰西之蓝和无数珍宝，那时他们所用的也是和我一样的神秘术。\
**Adèle**: The arcane skill I just used has been performed by my family for generations. We've recovered and examined all manner of treasures, including the Bourbons' own French Blue.

**阿黛拉**：火焰将揭示所触之物的本质，破除迷障，辨明真实与虚假。\
**Adèle**: Fire holds a certain power to reveal the true nature of what it touches. Through fire, we discern falsehood from truth.

**阿黛拉**：很遗憾，女士，这枚水晶并未通过鉴定——我想它并没有什么来自土星的智性，也没能在“存在的巨链”中占到什么好位置。\
**Adèle**: Sadly, madame, your crystal failed the test. It holds no wisdom of Saturn, nor any power from the so-called Chain of Being.

**阿黛拉**：但好在您也不必掏出腰包来支付它的巨额价码了，不是吗？\
**Adèle**: But luckily, we exposed it before the coin left your hand, didn't we?

**妇人**：这……您说……\
**Lady Visitor**: I ... This ...

妇人的目光在占卜师与阿黛拉之间来回扫了几趟，最终，她急匆匆地跑下了台。\
The lady's gaze darts between the diviner and Adèle before she bolts off the stage.

接下来，轮到了这场骗局的始作俑者。阿黛拉转过身面向沉默的占卜师。\
Adèle turns toward the dumbfounded diviner.

**阿黛拉**：好了，我也得对您说声抱歉，女士。\
**Adèle**: And you, madame, have given a lovely performance, I have to say. It's almost a shame to bring it to an end.

**阿黛拉**：倘若您的水晶货真价实，我就能帮您炒热气氛了。而现在——唉。\
**Adèle**: Ah, if only you hadn't tried to deceive your client with that fake crystal. Things might have gone quite differently, no? My arcane skill would've spoken volumes about your integrity.

发生这种事，我也很遗憾。

她朝着台下的观众耸了耸肩，遗憾的是无人开口回应。\
She shrugs toward the audience, each face in the crowd falling somewhere on a spectrum between starstruck and stupefied.

但一两秒后，掌声突兀地响起。费利西安全然不顾周围疑惑的目光，兴致勃勃地为精彩的戏码拍着手。\
Until at last, applause bursts out. Félicienne claps eagerly along with them.

阿黛拉朝她比了个“一切顺利”的手势，露出笑容。费利西安立刻把脑袋别开了。\
Adèle gives her an "all good" gesture and smiles. Félicienne replies with a brisk turn of her head.

**雷曼女士**：很近了，你身上的影子……我马上就能看清。\
**Madame Raymond**: This is close enough, close enough for me to clearly see the shadow upon you.

**阿黛拉**：什么？\
**Adèle**: Pardon?

她立刻望向占卜师，恰巧对上那双直勾勾盯住她的眼睛。\
She looks toward the diviner and meets those unblinking eyes staring straight at her.

**雷曼女士**：塔沃尼尔家的小姑娘……最年轻的那位，最崭新、最生动的那个……\
**Madame Raymond**: A Tavernier girl ... The youngest and brightest, brimming with vitality.

占卜师向前探身，她们之间的距离被压缩得过近了。阿黛拉的脊背窜起一阵寒意。\
The diviner leans forward. The space between them closes too fast. A chill runs down Adèle's spine.

**雷曼女士**：命定之人刚刚踏上了旅途，没有回头的余地，两次碰撞，先下而后上，你将践行……践行你的命运！\
**Madame Raymond**: The fated one has stepped onto her path. Twice will she collide with destiny—once risen, once descended. For a fate left vacant now shall be fulfilled!

**阿黛拉**：你——\
**Adèle**: You—

**雷曼女士**：你注定逃不过宿命的感召！怀有私心的贤者将玩弄你的命运，死亡的深渊正等待你坠入……\
**Madame Raymond**: The call must be answered! Walk with the wise, but beware their words. Beware the gaping abyss of death.

**雷曼女士**：而那地之上的，终将等同那天之下的……你所有的终将消失，死亡亦将引导你最终的升华……\
**Madame Raymond**: What lies below shall reflect what lies above—one shall ascend, but all must be paid.

**雷曼女士**：直到一切都回归！回归那——\
**Madame Raymond**: All must return! All must restore—

**雷曼女士**：——！\
**Madame Raymond**: ...!

**雷曼女士**：是——野兽——\
**Madame Raymond**: Monster! ... B-Beast!

**雷曼女士**：呃、呃……！\
**Madame Raymond**: Urh—Ugh!

**阿黛拉**：快叫人来！这里有没有医生？你怎么了？！\
**Adèle**: She needs help! Someone fetch-fetch a doctor! Madame, can you hear me?

**参会者Ⅰ**：她看起来不能呼吸了！\
**Participant I**: Why can't she breathe?

**参会者Ⅱ**：发生了什么？！\
**Participant II**: What's going on? Are we in danger?

**阿黛拉**：等等——\
**Adèle**: Wait ...

**阿黛拉**：她……在笑？\
**Adèle**: Is she smiling?

## AFF-02 友好证人 / Innocent Bystanders

**警员**：各位女士各位先生，请大家跟着那位警员到外面登记信息，不要停留在这里。\
**Police Officer**: Please, follow the officer outside and leave your contact details before you go.

占卜沙龙的众人像围栏中的绵羊一样陆续走出，议论声却仍不绝于耳。\
The shocked crowd file out like penned sheep, bleating and chattering with each step.

**参会者Ⅰ**：真是太可怕了，她临死前的样子……我今晚一定会做噩梦……\
**Participant I**: I doubt I'll get any sleep tonight after that sight.

**参会者Ⅱ**：我早和你说不该来！什么占卜……做这种事是会招来厄运的！\
**Participant II**: I told you we shouldn't have come! Nothing good ever comes of fortune-telling!

**参会者Ⅲ**：会不会是突发的疾病？比如癔症……\
**Participant III**: What could explain all that? Hysteria? A disease, perhaps?

**参会者Ⅰ**：噢，我知道那个，法比奥和弗朗格前几天还提到过！他们的邻居自称自己是黎塞留的轻骑兵，骑着扫帚从窗户跳了出去，现在还在医院里。\
**Participant I**: It's possible. You know, Fabio and Franco told me their neighbor started ranting about fighting alongside Cardinal Richelieu. Next thing you know, the man's leapt out the window riding a broom. Still in the hospital, I hear.

**参会者Ⅱ**：或者——你们忘了她说过的话？也许这些真的都是因为……\
**Participant II**: But remember what she said earlier? Maybe what she saw was her own killer.

**参会者Ⅰ**：——“热沃当的野兽”？\
**Participant I**: You mean the Beasts of Gévaudan?

恐惧和一丝隐秘的兴奋爬上每位来客的脸，那个百年前的传说再一次投下骇人的阴影。\
Fear, and a trace of hidden excitement, creeps onto every guest's face. The century-old legend casts its terrifying shadow once again.

**警员**：女士们，先生们！\
**Police Officer**: Ladies and gentlemen!

**警员**：巴黎警方一定会优先侦办此案，请各位不要传播流言，不要散播恐慌！我们会保护市民的安全！\
**Police Officer**: We will begin our investigation immediately. In the meantime, we ask that you not spread any rumors. There's no cause for panic as of now.

人们停止了谈论，但从他们的表情来看，恐怕不能指望这番话起到多大的作用。\
The murmurs fade but the officer's words have done little to calm them.

填满房间的众人散去，只留下了几位关键的“证人”。\
The crowd disperses, leaving behind a few key witnesses.

**阿黛拉**：这事可不要算在我头上，我根本没有碰到过她！\
**Adèle**: This isn't going to get pinned on me, is it? I didn't even touch her! You'll testify for me, won't you, Félicienne?

费利西安，你要为我作证……

**阿黛拉**：费利西安？\
**Adèle**: Félicienne?

阿黛拉回过头，发现自己的雇主正专注地绕着地上的尸体漫步，眼中闪动着兴味盎然的光彩。\
Adèle turns back to find her employer pacing around the corpse, eyes gleaming with curiosity.

**费利西安**：没想到还有这样精彩的余兴节目……\
**Félicienne**: Our so-called prophet failed to see her own demise. Well, if this isn't an interesting twist ...

**阿黛拉**：嘿，别离得太近！你这样搞不好会破坏现场的。\
**Adèle**: What are you doing? Get over here before they scold you for disturbing a crime scene!

她不免再次为雇主的随心所欲头疼，所幸一旁的警员并没有关注到这边。\
She sighs inwardly at her employer's whims, relieved the nearby officer isn't paying attention.

**警员**：唉，又来了，“热沃当的野兽”……\
**Police Officer**: Ah, not these Beasts of Gévaudan again.

**阿黛拉**：……又？为什么这么说，本杰明警官？\
**Adèle**: Again? What do you mean, Benjamin?

阿黛拉疑惑地看向熟识的警员。\
She's fortunate to have found a familiar face among the arriving officers.

**警员**：一个不知道从哪儿出现的流言，根本是无中生有，却传遍了全巴黎！\
**Police Officer**: *sigh* It's just a rumor and a wild one at that. Yet somehow, it's spread to every corner of Paris!

**警员**：总有人报警说碰到了什么“热沃当的野兽”，我们过去一看，连一颗面包渣都没有！不知道他们的脑子出了什么问题！\
**Police Officer**: There have been a number of sightings of these so-called "beasts," but by the time we arrive at the scene, there isn't so much as a trace left of them—not even a hair!

**警员**：街上乱了起来，不少混球也开始不安分，上次喊你帮忙鉴定证物的那个案子也是这样……\
**Police Officer**: The whole world's gone mad. Street crime is on the rise, and the last case we asked you for help with identification on? Well, that was completely ... *sigh*

他捂着额角叹出一口气。\
He presses his hand to his temple, giving it a soft rub.

**警员**：本来最近就忙！将近半个城的工人都在搞罢工，在工厂里大办舞会……警察的工作已经够多了！\
**Police Officer**: As if we don't have enough to deal with! Half the city's on strike, and every day there's some new trouble, whether from the factories or out on the streets!

**警员**：有时候我真羡慕你，阿黛拉。每天开开出租车，陪外地人四处转转就行了。\
**Police Officer**: I envy you, Adèle. How simple it must be to sit behind a wheel all day and show visitors around.

**阿黛拉**：哈哈……还行吧，大家都有自己的烦恼嘛。\
**Adèle**: Oh, well, it comes with its own set of problems.

阿黛拉向费利西安的方向瞥了一眼——她似乎已经对那具死尸失去了兴趣，正若有所思地盯着角落的一张空椅子。\
Adèle glances toward Félicienne. She seems to have lost interest in the corpse and is now intent on examining a chair in the corner.

**警员**：哈，就知道你会这么说。\
**Police Officer**: Heh. Knew you'd say that.

警员摸出了本子与笔。待他再抬起头时，脸上那份面对熟人时的亲昵态度已经收起了大半。\
The officer pulls out a notebook and pen. When he looks up again, he adopts his best attempt at a professional tone.

**警员**：好了，那我们开始吧。有几个问题需要你配合回答一下。\
**Police Officer**: Let's get on with it. There are some questions we need you to answer. You know how these things go.

**警员**：虽然咱们也是老朋友了，但公事公办，毕竟你是当时离她最近的人。\
**Police Officer**: I trust you know this is strictly procedure. You were the person closest to the victim at the time of death. So please, Adèle, answer with care.

**阿黛拉**：当然，我明白，警官。\
**Adèle**: Go ahead. Ask away, officer.

证物已经被尽数撤走，法医正在查看地上的遗体，占卜师的死状狰狞可怖。\
The evidence has been cleared away. The coroner examines the body with visible concern. The diviner's death is gruesome indeed.

**警员**：口唇发绀，瞳孔放大，手指紧缩，脊柱强直……虽然只是初步鉴定，但这一切都符合惊吓过度致死的表现。\
**Police Officer**: Blue lips, dilated pupils, clenched fists, and a stiffened spine ... The coroner will have his say, I'm sure, but it looks like extreme shock to me.

**阿黛拉**：惊吓过度致死？这……\
**Adèle**: Extreme shock? But ...

**警员**：现场当时有没有发生什么特殊的事？\
**Police Officer**: What were the circumstances of the event? Anything unusual?

**阿黛拉**：她正在为我占卜。从中途起她的举动就很奇怪，突然死死盯住我，说了一长串听不明白的话。\
**Adèle**: The madame offered to read my fate, but halfway through, she started acting strange, staring at me and mumbling things.

**阿黛拉**：丢下那堆“预言”之后，她提到了“野兽”，接着就倒在地上……\
**Adèle**: She said something about a beast and then collapsed to the floor.

**警员**：照这么说，她通过占卜，从你身上看到了“热沃当的野兽”，然后……就吓死了？\
**Police Officer**: So, she was reading your fortune, saw a Beast of Gévaudan, and it what? Scared her to death?

**阿黛拉**：我知道你不信，但看起来确实是这样。\
**Adèle**: It sounds ridiculous, I know, Benjamin, but it's what I saw.

二人面面相觑了片刻。\
They exchange a glance.

警员拿笔的手迟迟未动——显然他也在评估这番疯话的实际价值。\
The officer's pen hesitates, weighing how much of the madness is worth writing down.

最后，他合上了本子，露出了相当无奈的表情。\
Finally, he closes the notebook with a resigned look.

**警员**：好了，感谢你，阿黛拉。看来我们得考虑把它和城中沸沸扬扬的传言合并调查了。\
**Police Officer**: Okay. Thanks for your help, Adèle. I suppose it's about time we tied all these cases concerning the beasts together.

**警员**：说到底，“热沃当的野兽”已经是一百多年前的传说了，怎么会现在又莫名其妙地流行起来？\
**Police Officer**: But it's strange, no? How could creatures from a folktale more than a century old be doing all this here and now?

**警员**：我看这里面有不少问题。现在不止巴黎，全法国都让这些事弄得无法安宁，而混乱总是和谣言相伴而生。\
**Police Officer**: This has to be more than a passing fad. Paris—hell, the entire country—has been gripped by all sorts of rumors. The streets are growing more volatile by the day.

**阿黛拉**：是，很多人都想借着这个传说做点什么。\
**Adèle**: You're right. There are always people who will try to take advantage of these situations.

**阿黛拉**：比如这位留下“预言”的占卜师，不知道从哪儿听说了我家的事，趁机拿毫不相干的东西糊弄我。\
**Adèle**: Like this poor fortune-teller. I bet she heard some tales about my family and thought she could scam me with a sensational prophecy about my not-so-rosy fate.

**警员**：那个说你们一家人都会为了寻宝而遭遇不测的诅咒？\
**Police Officer**: "Doomed to die on a quest for hidden jewels." Seems the madame didn't know that you're the furthest thing from a treasure hunter.

**警员**：只要肯稍微花点工夫打听塔沃尼尔家，这的确也不是什么秘密。\
**Police Officer**: It's hardly a secret that the Taverniers have a habit of meeting an unfortunate end.

**阿黛拉**：没错，我不打算太相信她的话。说到底，“诅咒”的说法无非是来自我那几个最为人所知的祖辈。\
**Adèle**: Far from it. Which is why I didn't believe her for a moment. The Tavernier Curse? Please, it's just a story made up to dramatize the legends of my ancestors.

**阿黛拉**：比如我那位曾曾曾曾曾曾祖父，从印度带回了著名的“法兰西之蓝”，结果不久就死于非命。\
**Adèle**: From my great-great-great-great-great-great-grandfather, who died after bringing the French Blue from India,

**阿黛拉**：又比如我那个曾祖父，为了寻找大革命期间流失到国外的珍宝，因为一场风暴死在了海上……\
**Adèle**: down to my great-grandfather, who died chasing jewelry stolen from France during the Revolution.

**阿黛拉**：说是真有某种神秘的力量也好，说是巧合也成。没必要放在心上。\
**Adèle**: Call it a curse, if you like—a mystical power, fate, coincidence—whatever the words, the plain and dull truth is that hunting jewels is a dangerous line of work, no?

**警员**：也对……我记得你说过，你父母也是宝石猎人。那他们还好吗？\
**Police Officer**: That it is. While we're on the topic, how are your parents doing? I recall you said they were still in the family business.

**阿黛拉**：还在国外满世界跑呢，我们三个很久没见面了。\
**Adèle**: Out on some quest again. I couldn't even hazard a guess as to where they are now; they move around so often.

**阿黛拉**：不过偶尔会有些信寄回家里，看样子他们应该过得不错。\
**Adèle**: But they have sent letters. Living life to the fullest, as far as I can tell.

警员如释重负地呼出一口气。\
The officer exhales in relief.

**警员**：那就好！寻找宝石，周游世界……听着真是不错！肯定比像我这样整天窝在同一个地方，几十年如一日地过日子要有意思多了。\
**Police Officer**: *relieved sigh* Glad to hear it. Maybe I should envy them instead. Traveling the world like that ... Much better than being stuck in a police station.

**警员**：你呢？你打算什么时候追随父母的脚步，也做个宝石猎人？\
**Police Officer**: And you? Don't you ever think of joining them on the hunt?

**阿黛拉**：他们是他们，我对那些闪闪发光的东西可没那么大兴趣。\
**Adèle**: My parents and I are different, to say the least. I don't share their obsession with shiny stones.

**阿黛拉**：我只想过普普通通的日子，赚的钱够花就行，重要的是要舒服、自在。\
**Adèle**: A simple, comfortable life—that's all I want. No glittering ambitions, no fancy things, just a job that pays the bills, fills my belly, and lets me get a good night's sleep at the end of the day. Why anyone would want to think so hard every day is beyond me.

最好工作不要太忙，每天能睡到自然醒，也不需要费太多脑筋……

**阿黛拉**：当时我和朋友随便在招聘册上翻了一页，第一个出现的词就是“出租车司机”。不得不说，它挺合我心意。\
**Adèle**: In fact, this job was the first thing I saw when I opened the advertisements page. "Why not?" I thought. "Suits me better than treasure-seeking ever will."

**警员**：哈哈！的确是你的风格。\
**Police Officer**: Hahaha. I would expect nothing less.

警员点了点头，将拿在手里的笔记本收回口袋。\
He nods and slips the notebook back into his pocket.

**警员**：行了，情况我都大致明白了。\
**Police Officer**: Good! I believe we have all we need from you.

**警员**：不用太担心，你没有动机，也没有手段……目前这事看起来和你没什么关系。\
**Police Officer**: Please, don't worry, Adèle. I see neither motive nor means for you to do her harm. You're all clear.

**警员**：如果之后还需要你进一步配合调查，我们会联系你。\
**Police Officer**: But we'll get in touch if we need anything else. Oh, forgive me—another question. Was there anything else that seemed suspicious? Anything that stood out to you?

还有什么要补充的吗？

**阿黛拉**：多谢，本杰明警官。我没有什么要补充的了——\
**Adèle**: No, nothing really.

**阿黛拉**：不对！等一下……\
**Adèle**: Oh, wait!

**阿黛拉**：还有一件事，不确定帮不帮得上你——我看到过一个可疑的女人。\
**Adèle**: There was a woman. I don't know if she's involved, but there was something odd about her.

**阿黛拉**：事情发生得很突然，几乎所有人都被吓住了。只有她还无动于衷地坐在座位上……甚至在笑。\
**Adèle**: It happened so fast, but still, while everyone else was too stunned to do anything, she sat there and smiled.

**警员**：嗯？你还记得那个人的特征吗？\
**Police Officer**: She smiled? Do you recall what this woman looked like?

阿黛拉快速描述了记忆中的画面。在听完后，原本如临大敌的警员却放松了神情。\
Adèle recounts the events as they happened. After hearing her out, the officer's professional demeanor cracks a little.

**警员**：哦！你提到的应该是贝丽尔·布翁尼女士，和平街一家水晶工房的主人，一位占卜师。\
**Police Officer**: Hah, that's Madame Beryl Bouanich. Couldn't be anyone else! Owns a crystal parlor on Rue de la Paix. She's a diviner, too.

**警员**：她是这起案子的报案人，我们已经和她聊过了。\
**Police Officer**: She's the one who reported the case to us. Our officers have already spoken with her.

**阿黛拉**：她是……报案人？\
**Adèle**: She reported the case?

## AFF-03 会面礼 / Encounter Etiquette

成功点火后，引擎微颤着发出规律的响声，黑色的出租车向前方驶去。\
The engine starts, churning into a rhythmic patter as the black taxi moves forward. A chime sways in the taxi—a gift from her parents.

来自父母的纪念风铃在窗前轻轻摇晃着。

**阿黛拉**：所以就是这样了，没想到又是一个占卜师。\
**Adèle**: Well, I suppose that's that. No mysterious murderer, just another diviner.

**阿黛拉**：不过本杰明警官说，已经调查过那位布翁尼女士的嫌疑了，她是清白的。\
**Adèle**: Benjamin said they spoke to her already and cleared her of any suspicion.

**费利西安**：清白？那可不一定。\
**Félicienne**: Cleared? I wouldn't be so quick to believe that.

**费利西安**：贝丽尔·布翁尼——她的心思可不是普通人能轻易看透的。\
**Félicienne**: Beryl Bouanich—she hides herself well, that one.

副驾驶席上的乘客将甜点丢入口中嚼碎，颇有几分咬牙切齿的意思。\
The passenger pops a pastry into her mouth, chewing with a mix of irritation and thought.

**阿黛拉**：怎么，你认识她？\
**Adèle**: Hm? Do you know her, madame?

阿黛拉投去错愕的一瞥。她从未见过费利西安露出过这样不悦的表情。\
Adèle glances over in surprise. She's never seen Félicienne look so displeased.

**费利西安**：刚才的就是最后一枚了。\
**Félicienne**: This box is empty. Was that the last macaron?

**阿黛拉**：……我怎么敢怠慢了您呢？这里还有，您请用。\
**Adèle**: Of course not! I got another box just for you.

职业精神让阿黛拉并未对话题的转移表示异议，她从座位旁拿出包装精致的小盒。\
She maintains an absolute sense of professionalism while taking out a neatly wrapped box from beside her seat.

**费利西安**：算你机灵。\
**Félicienne**: Ah, it seems my expectations have been surpassed, low as they were.

**费利西安**：没错……就是这个味道。\
**Félicienne**: Mmm. So delicious!

**阿黛拉**：你还真是喜欢甜食。\
**Adèle**: Hah, I must say, you seem to really have a sweet tooth.

费利西安咬下甜点的声音让她有些说不出的紧张。阿黛拉握紧方向盘，努力让精神集中在眼前的道路上。\
The soft crunch of Félicienne biting into a pastry makes Adèle strangely tense. She grips the wheel, forcing herself to focus on the road ahead.

**费利西安**：那个警察说贝丽尔·布翁尼人在哪里？\
**Félicienne**: So, Beryl Bouanich—where is she now? Did your little policeman say anything?

**阿黛拉**：和平街，布翁尼女士在那里有一家水晶工房。\
**Adèle**: He said she's running a crystal parlor on Rue de la Paix.

**费利西安**：掉头，我们现在就去。\
**Félicienne**: Turn around. I should like to pay her a visit.

熟悉的命令式语句从副驾驶席上飞来，所幸阿黛拉已经熟练掌握了应对之法。\
A familiar commanding tone comes from the passenger seat. Fortunately, by now, Adèle has learned how to handle it.

**阿黛拉**：抱歉，费利西安，现在不行。\
**Adèle**: Now? I don't know, Félicienne. It's nearly the end of the day.

**阿黛拉**：我和你说过，今天晚上我和朋友有约了。\
**Adèle**: I'm meeting a friend tonight. I told you that.

**费利西安**：那就让她去和平街等你。\
**Félicienne**: Then you can tell your friend to meet you at Rue de la Paix.

眼刀立刻剐了过来。\
A sharp glare follows the words, audible without even looking at her.

**费利西安**：你的报酬翻倍，就现在，掉头——我是说，随便转向哪个该死的方向。\
**Félicienne**: I'll double your pay for the evening. Turn us around. Take whichever route you like.

**阿黛拉**：可是……\
**Adèle**: But ...

**费利西安**：三倍——不，十倍。\
**Félicienne**: Ah, fine. Triple? No? Ten times, then.

**阿黛拉**：十……？！\
**Adèle**: Ten times?!

阿黛拉不想承认她确实动摇了一下，哪怕最近她有读那本写着“不要被报酬收买，工人需要休息时间”的宣传册。\
Adèle struggles against the temptation but weighs it against what she read in the pamphlets the strikers have been passing around. "Don't be swayed by money alone; workers need rest!"

**阿黛拉**：不……咳，不行！真的不行。西莉亚难得有空。\
**Adèle**: Ah ... No, Félicienne, I really can't. Célia's always busy these days; I barely get to see her.

**阿黛拉**：她之前一直忙着写论文和搞叫什么……“超心理学”的研究，我们好久没见面了。\
**Adèle**: She's all wrapped up in this parapsychology thing. I haven't seen her in so long. I don't want to cancel on her.

我不想放她的鸽子。

**阿黛拉**：明天我一定陪你过去，随叫随到。\
**Adèle**: We'll go to Rue de la Paix tomorrow. I promise.

**费利西安**：真没劲。\
**Félicienne**: You live a terribly tedious life, Adèle Tavernier.

费利西安不悦地眯起了眼睛——下一句话还没出口，她忽然猛地从副驾驶席上探身。\
Félicienne narrows her eyes with acute displeasure, but before she can speak, she jerks forward from the passenger seat.

**费利西安**：——等等！就在那里，是她！\
**Félicienne**: Wait. Look! That's her!

**阿黛拉**：什么？谁？\
**Adèle**: What? Who?

**费利西安**：贝丽尔·布翁尼，她就在那里！快回去！\
**Félicienne**: Beryl Bouanich! Just there! Turn, now!

**阿黛拉**：等一下，别乱动！这样很危——\
**Adèle**: Let go! I can turn the wheel my—Rgh!

吱——！！\
*screech*

阿黛拉的车在划出一道长长的弧线后勉强停住，而相对驶来的另一辆车则结结实实地撞在了路灯上。\
Adèle's car skids in a long arc before finally stopping, while the oncoming vehicle veers into a streetlight.

**情绪高亢的司机**：拜托！是谁开的车，这是在搞什么鬼？\
**Agitated Driver**: Damn it! Have you lost your mind?

勉强爬出驾驶室的司机愤怒地指向阿黛拉，咆哮的声音让车窗一阵震颤。\
The driver climbs out, furious, pointing at Adèle as his shouting makes the windows rattle.

**情绪高亢的司机**：喂！喂！你给我下来！\
**Agitated Driver**: Ah! I'm speaking to you! Out of the car! Now!

**费利西安**：……\
**Félicienne**: ...

**阿黛拉**：…………\
**Adèle**: ...

**费利西安**：看我干什么？你没听见吗，外面有人找你。\
**Félicienne**: What are you staring at? You heard the man. Get out.

**阿黛拉**：……我回来再和你算账！\
**Adèle**: We'll settle this later!

推开车门，阿黛拉庆幸自己反应还算快，事故后果不至于太严重。\
Pushing open the door, Adèle silently praises her own quick reflexes. The crash isn't too severe.

街边也并没有任何像贝丽尔·布翁尼的人，整件事都像是下班路上的祸不单行。\
There's no sign of anyone like Beryl Bouanich on the street. The whole thing just feels like another stroke of bad luck on the drive home.

**阿黛拉**：再怎么着急，抢方向盘也太危险了！唉……我的零事故记录就这样终结了。\
**Adèle**: What was she thinking? Urgh, ah, grabbing the wheel like that! Never imagined my first crash would be like this.

她揉了揉额头，硬着头皮向一旁火冒三丈的年轻男子走去。\
She rubs her forehead and steels herself to face the fuming young man nearby.

**阿黛拉**：抱歉，先生，刚才我有些分神……\
**Adèle**: I'm terribly sorry, sir. I was distracted—

**情绪高亢的司机**：抱歉？\
**Agitated Driver**: Sorry? Aha! Do you even have the slightest clue what sort of damage you've caused?

抱歉就足够了吗？你知不知道自己做了什么？

**情绪高亢的司机**：现在正是国家存亡的关键时刻，一刻都不能够耽搁！\
**Agitated Driver**: We can't afford to lose time here! The nation is calling to us!

他愤怒地给了自己的车子一拳，原本就轻微变形的后车盖发出凄惨而空洞的哀嚎，围观的人越来越多。\
He slams his fist against his own car. The already-dented trunk lets out a hollow, miserable groan as the crowd thickens.

**阿黛拉**：国家……存亡？\
**Adèle**: Ah? The nation?

**阿黛拉**：呃，您是想说您正有特别重要的事要做吗？\
**Adèle**: Is that a strike slogan? Or do you mean you have urgent business to tend to?

还是说……这是新的罢工口号？

**情绪高亢的司机**：帝国的真正主人已经回来了，拿破仑皇帝已经在儒安港登陆！他会再次为我们带来胜利与荣耀！\
**Agitated Driver**: Our one true leader has returned! The Emperor has landed at Golfe-Juan! He will bring glory to France once more!

**情绪高亢的司机**：现在他正向巴黎赶来，但身边只有寥寥数百的士兵……我们必须立刻集结，前往他的身边！\
**Agitated Driver**: He's riding to Paris with only a few hundred soldiers at his side. Our Emperor is too distant from his people. We must go to him!

**阿黛拉**：帝国？儒安港？您到底在说什么呢？\
**Adèle**: The Emperor? Golfe-Juan? What on earth are you talking about?

男子表情严肃，实在不像是在开一个蹩脚的玩笑。阿黛拉错愕地看着他，一时间不知道该如何接话。\
The man's stern face makes it clear he isn't joking. Adèle stares at him, at a loss for words.

但她的反应似乎被理解为了另一种意思。\
But her silence seems to be taken another way.

**情绪高亢的司机**：我明白了……你是波旁王朝和路易十八的走狗，是不是？\
**Agitated Driver**: I see. You've sided with the Bourbons, haven't you? You're another one of the king's stooges!

**情绪高亢的司机**：奥斯特里茨的太阳在呼喊着我，我绝不会让你阻止我！\
**Agitated Driver**: The Sun of Austerlitz calls to me. I will not be stopped!

**情绪高亢的司机**：放开我！我必须去……去我们的皇帝的身边！\
**Agitated Driver**: Let me be! I must go to the Emperor!

**阿黛拉**：先生，您冷静点！谁能来帮我一把？\
**Adèle**: Sir, calm yourself! Someone help me, please!

在周围人的帮助下，阿黛拉成功地将司机从车顶拽了下来，但骚动也令围观者越聚越多。\
With help from the bystanders, Adèle manages to pull the driver down from the roof, though the commotion draws even more onlookers.

**围观群众Ⅰ**：看样子又是一个被癔症害了的可怜家伙。\
**Curious Passerby I**: Ay, ay, ay! Another poor fellow lost in delusion.

**围观群众Ⅱ**：我看也是。离远点，他净说些疯话……百日王朝可是在一个世纪前就没了！\
**Curious Passerby II**: Careful! Don't get too close. He's talking gibberish. The Hundred Days ended over a hundred years ago.

**阿黛拉**：嘿，谁能帮忙叫救护车吗？\
**Adèle**: Please, someone, get him to the hospital. He needs help!

**阿黛拉**：有没有认识这位先生的人？我没时间在这里等太久——\
**Adèle**: Does anyone know this man? I really need to go. I have to see someone.

她看了看自己挂了彩的爱车和里面坐着的漠不关心小姐，感到一阵为难。\
She looks at her scratched-up car and the indifferent lady inside, feeling a twinge of helplessness.

就在此时，层层人群被挤出一道缝隙，几名学者装扮的人努力地靠近了现场。\
Just then, the crowd parts as several men in scholarly attire push their way forward.

**？？？**：真是太抱歉了，小姐！我的学生给您添麻烦了，您的一切损失我来赔偿。\
**???**: Vincent, my God! I'm terribly sorry for all the trouble he's caused, miss! He's my student. Please, allow me to cover the damages.

**？？？**：您留下联系方式就行，我来处理之后的事……\
**???**: Would you mind leaving me your address? I'll take care of the rest.

一名四十岁上下的男人终于穿过了人群，他掏出手绢擦去额头的汗水，带着书卷气的脸上满是歉意。\
A man in his forties finally makes it through, wiping sweat from his brow with a handkerchief. His face full of apology.

几名学生模样的年轻人跟在他身后，为首的女孩有着阿黛拉再熟悉不过的面容。\
Several young people follow behind him—students, led by a girl Adèle immediately recognizes.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚？！\
**Adèle**: Célia!

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉？天哪，还好你们没受伤！\
**Célia**: Adèle? Goodness, are you hurt?

女孩焦急地跑了过来。仔细确认了阿黛拉和那位司机的安全后，她才稍微退开几步，为身后的人简单做起介绍。\
She rushes over, checking that Adèle and the driver are safe before stepping back and introducing the others.

**西莉亚**：这是罗西教授，我和你提起过——罗西教授，这是我的朋友阿黛拉。\
**Célia**: This is Professor Roseau—the one I told you about. Professor, this is my friend, Adèle.

**西莉亚**：就是那个和我约好了今天一起吃晚饭的朋友。\
**Célia**: She's who I was going to see this evening.

西莉亚飞快说完，如释重负地拍了拍好友的肩膀。\
Célia finishes her introductions, patting her friend's shoulder in relief.

**西莉亚**：还好你拦下了文森特，阿黛拉！否则我们不一定来得及追上他……\
**Célia**: Thank goodness you stopped him, Adèle! Who knows what might have happened otherwise.

**罗西教授**：对，多亏您反应快，阿黛拉小姐。\
**Professor Roseau**: Yes, yes. You acted both quickly and rightly, miss.

面对意料外的感谢，阿黛拉只能挠挠头，试图把话题抛回仍在胡言乱语的司机身上。\
Faced with unexpected thanks, Adèle scratches her head, trying to shift the topic back to the still-babbling driver.

**阿黛拉**：他这是怎么了？\
**Adèle**: Uh ... What's wrong with him?

**西莉亚**：说来话长……最近几个星期，文森特的精神状况一直都不太好。\
**Célia**: It's a long story. He's been acting strange for weeks.

**西莉亚**：他今天迟迟没有露面，我们就去了他的公寓找他。门没锁，推门进去，到处都是一片狼藉……\
**Célia**: So when he didn't turn up this morning, we went to his home to check on him. The door was open, and it was a total mess.

**罗西教授**：唉，可怜的孩子。说到底，都是我的错，也许是我给了他太大压力。\
**Professor Roseau**: Poor boy. Such potential. But then perhaps I pushed him too hard.

男子抢过西莉亚的话，摇了摇头，一脸自责。\
The man cuts Célia off, shaking his head, guilt written all over his face.

**罗西教授**：不该再耽误大家的时间了。西莉亚，你和这位小姐去吃饭吧。我会处理好文森特的事。\
**Professor Roseau**: I shan't keep you, ladies. Célia, go with your friend. I'll deal with all this.

**西莉亚**：这……\
**Célia**: But ...

**罗西教授**：去吧，别忘了明天的调研要准时到场。\
**Professor Roseau**: Please, Célia. Put this behind you and enjoy your evening. But be sure to join me for tomorrow's fieldwork.

年轻的女学生看了看一旁的阿黛拉，最终选择接受老师的好意。\
She glances at Adèle, then accepts her teacher's offer.

一行人将那位可怜的年轻人搀扶走后，围观的人群渐渐散去，夜色正恰如其分地到来。\
After helping the poor man away, the crowd gradually disperses as night falls over the street.

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉，你的车还好吗？罗西教授会承担赔偿的，别太担心。\
**Célia**: How's your car? I know the professor said he'd cover it.

**阿黛拉**：车没事，也就前面剐蹭了些。只是把我们吓着了——\
**Adèle**: Not bad, just a dent on the bumper. It was a bit of a fright, but I'm fine now.

**阿黛拉**：啊，西莉亚，稍等！\
**Adèle**: Ah, wait! Sorry, Célia, I need to—

刚才的一连串事情搅得阿黛拉脑袋发晕。她终于回过神，跑向停在不远处的标致201。\
The whirlwind of events leaves Adèle dizzy. She finally regains her senses and runs toward her Peugeot 201 parked nearby.

**阿黛拉**：我都忘了，费利西安还在车上！我得先把她送回酒店。\
**Adèle**: Félicienne's still in the car! I'll have to take her back to the hotel.

**阿黛拉**：等了这么久，这下她又要生气了……\
**Adèle**: Urh. She's not going to be happy after I left her like that.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安小姐，费利——咦？\
**Adèle**: Félicienne! Fé—huh?

车里空空如也，副驾驶上的乘客不见踪影，取而代之的是车窗上多出的一行鲜红文字。\
The passenger seat is vacant, replaced by a line of bright red words scrawled across the window.

先走了，明天和平街见。\
Tomorrow, Rue de la Paix.

**阿黛拉**：……这不会是用口红写的吧！\
**Adèle**: Oh, no. Is that lipstick?!

阿黛拉掏出手帕试图清理车窗上的留言，遗憾的是效果并不明显。\
Adèle pulls out a handkerchief to wipe the writing from the glass, but despite her scrubbing, it barely fades.

**阿黛拉**：和抢方向盘的事一起算上，明天我一定要向她要清理费！\
**Adèle**: First she grabs the wheel, crashing my car, might I add. And then, she has the cheek to scribble on the window! Ugh! She's paying for a full clean, I swear it!

**西莉亚**：怎么了，阿黛拉？\
**Célia**: Are you certain you're alright?

好友也走了过来，站在车窗边，好奇地探头向里张望。\
Her friend walks over, peeking curiously through the window.

阿黛拉摆摆手，不想让这小小的插曲影响期待已久的晚餐。\
Adèle waves it off, refusing to let this small incident ruin their long-awaited dinner.

**阿黛拉**：没什么，我们走吧！去老地方，塞纳河边的那家餐厅？还是你想换换新口味？\
**Adèle**: Ugh! I'm fine. *exhale* So, shall we eat at that spot near the Seine again, or are you feeling adventurous tonight?

**阿黛拉**：你不是总和我说学校那边的餐馆早都吃腻了吗，难得见面，这顿饭听你的。\
**Adèle**: You said you couldn't stand the campus cafés anymore. So, tonight, my darling, you choose the food.

**西莉亚**：听我的？那……干脆回家简单做点菜好啦。\
**Célia**: Really? I suppose if I could have anything ... You know, what I'm really missing is some good home cooking.

她愉快地掰着手指，报出一连串菜单。\
She starts counting on her fingers, reciting a whole list of dishes.

**西莉亚**：洋葱汤、奶酪锅和焗土豆——还有我刚买的苹果酒，怎么样？\
**Célia**: Onion soup, gratin dauphinois, maybe a bit of cheese for a small fondue. Oh, and I just bought a bottle of cider. What do you think?

**西莉亚**：前几天我回家取资料，本来想顺带着找你帮忙收拾收拾的。但你不在，我只有一个人把整个屋子整理好了，连露台都打扫干净了。\
**Célia**: You simply have to come over and see my place now. I cleaned the whole thing. Balcony, too! I came over to ask you for help, but you weren't home.

**阿黛拉**：那不是正好吗？上车！\
**Adèle**: Home cooking it is! Hop in!

二人一拍即合，默契地绕到了标致201的两侧，几乎是同时拉开了车门。\
In perfect sync, the two circle to opposite sides of the Peugeot 201 and open the doors at once.

**阿黛拉**：——坐稳，我们出发！\
**Adèle**: Buckle up, to home!

## AFF-04 潜意识猎手 / Unconscious Hunting

**执夜人**：塔沃尼尔家的人都会不可避免地追逐宝藏，并在冒险的途中遭遇不幸。身边亲近之人或接手宝藏的人也会沾染这样的厄运。\
**Vigil Officer**: The Tavernier curse—every member of your family is destined to hunt endlessly for treasure until they meet their end. Passed through blood relation, usually to the relative closest to them.

**执夜人**：但你并不相信这个预言，对吗？——阿黛拉·塔沃尼尔，或者“灰调蓝”小姐？\
**Vigil Officer**: You don't believe in this so-called curse, do you, Ms. Tavernier? Or should I call you Brume?

僻静的谈话室中，除了摄像机运作的少许杂音外，四周再听不见其他多余动静。\
The interview room is coldly silent except the faint whir of the recording camera.

年轻女子的证言一字不落地被收音设备捕捉，化作磁性材料上记录的冰冷信号。\
Every word of the young woman's statement is captured by the microphone, preserved as cold signals on magnetic tape.

**灰调蓝**：事到如今，倒也不是完全不信。\
**Brume**: Given how things have turned out, it isn't as easy as a yes or no, don't you think?

她无奈地笑了笑，低头看着自己的手掌。\
She gives a helpless smile, looking down at her palms.

**灰调蓝**：可就算它真的会在某一天应验，那又如何呢？\
**Brume**: But say it is true, then what of it? We're all going to die, no? One day I'll die searching for treasure, but before then, I'll live as I see fit.

所有人都知道人终有一死，但大家仍然在好好生活。

**灰调蓝**：在某个命运的分歧点真正来临之前，我并不打算每天战战兢兢地活着。\
**Brume**: I don't plan on wasting away my days in fear.

她稍作停顿。\
She pauses briefly.

**灰调蓝**：或者说，即使结局无可更改，我也不希望按预设的剧本生活。\
**Brume**: The ending may be written, but that doesn't mean I want to follow the story word for word.

**灰调蓝**：那天，我载着西莉亚前往她家……我也这么回答了她。回过头想，也许从那时起一切就改变了。\
**Brume**: That's what I told Cici as we were driving to her place. And now, looking back ... Maybe that's when it all began.

**阿黛拉**：嗯——好吃！\
**Adèle**: Mmm, so good! This gratin is the best. How'd you get so much flavor out of a simple potato?

我一直不明白，土豆怎么也可以做得这么美味！

**西莉亚**：其实和学校食堂一个水平。你自己不怎么做饭，当然觉得格外好吃。\
**Célia**: You like it, then? It's just ordinary home cooking, really. Maybe it's finally time you started doing it yourself.

**阿黛拉**：是啊，毕竟小时候我那倒霉老爸只会端出各种野营罐头，然后说“在丛林里有这个吃就谢天谢地吧”。\
**Adèle**: Well, Papa didn't exactly teach me much in the art. He'd just pop open a tin can and say, "Be grateful. When you're in the jungle, this is a luxury."

**阿黛拉**：可我现在都还没离开过巴黎半步！\
**Adèle**: But he never took me to the jungle. He never even let me leave Paris. I still haven't been anywhere.

西莉亚笑着摇了摇头，接过空盘，为好友又盛上了一份土豆泥。\
Célia smiles and shakes her head. She grabs the empty plate to scoop her friend another serving of potatoes.

**西莉亚**：是你自己选的，说什么绝对不会成为宝石猎人。\
**Célia**: You can only blame yourself, Adèle. You were the one adamant about not becoming a hunter.

**阿黛拉**：我绝不要按规定好的剧本生活——而且这事也有你的一份，别忘了当时翻开那套印着招聘广告的报纸时，可是你挑的页数！\
**Adèle**: Of course! Because I don't want my life planned out like a stage play! A-And don't pretend you didn't have a part in this. You're the one who picked the page number in the advertisements.

西莉亚说不过她，往土豆泥上又浇了两勺炖菜，垒起一座小山，推到阿黛拉面前。\
Célia can't argue, so she pours two more spoonfuls of stew over the mash, stacking it high into a little mountain and sliding it in front of Adèle.

**西莉亚**：算了，瞧你这副能说会道的样子——我们的司机女士最近有没有遇见什么趣事？\
**Célia**: Sharp as ever. Since we're on the subject, how is work going? Any interesting fares lately?

**阿黛拉**：还真有一个。只是与其说是“趣事”，不如说是“怪事”。\
**Adèle**: Hmm. There was one thing. Not sure if I would call it interesting, though. Peculiar, perhaps?

她咬着勺子努力回忆不久前的情景，占卜师的表情在脑海中仍然清晰。\
She bites down on her spoon, trying to recall the scene from earlier. The diviner's expression is still vivid in her mind.

**阿黛拉**：我去了玛莱区的一家占卜沙龙。里头的占卜师是个招摇撞骗的家伙，甚至骗到了我头上！\
**Adèle**: I was at a diviner's salon, and the host ... I don't know; I think she was trying to scam me.

**阿黛拉**：她对我说了一些奇怪的预言，听起来和“塔沃尼尔的诅咒”很像……然后她突然倒下，就这么……死了。\
**Adèle**: She started rambling about all these strange things that would happen, things that sounded a lot like the Tavernier Curse. And then, she, well, she died.

**西莉亚**：……死了？\
**Célia**: Died?

西莉亚睁大眼睛，手里的叉子不自觉地磕碰着餐盘。\
Célia's eyes widen, her fork clinking unconsciously against the plate.

**阿黛拉**：反正警察已经在处理了。别太担心。至于那些预言，你也知道我向来不信，对吧？\
**Adèle**: Then the police came, and I suppose the case is still under investigation. Anyway, you know what I think of those diviners. They're not exactly people you should take seriously.

**西莉亚**：那你怎么突然想着跑去占卜沙龙？\
**Célia**: Then why were you there?

**阿黛拉**：我？可不是我想去，是我的老主顾费利西安大小姐一时兴起。\
**Adèle**: Not by choice, that's for certain. One of my clients was interested. Madame Félicienne.

**阿黛拉**：今天的撞车也是……算了，不聊工作了。你呢，有没有碰见值得说说的事？\
**Adèle**: She always gets these sudden whims and insists on having everything done just as she pleases. I wouldn't have crashed my car if she hadn't—Bah, forget it. How's university life?

西莉亚没有顺着阿黛拉的提问说下去。她敏锐地抓住了这段话中的几个词。\
Célia doesn't answer Adèle's question. Instead, she catches on to her words.

**西莉亚**：老主顾？没听你提起过她，是我住在学校太久了吗？\
**Célia**: She is a long-term client, then? Can't say you've mentioned her before. Or maybe I've been spending too much time on campus, haven't I?

**阿黛拉**：拜托，这里就不要用疑问句了吧！\
**Adèle**: What do you think? I swear, this little one might forget you completely if you spend any more time hidden away in your books!

你再多消失几个月，小家伙搞不好就要忘记你的气味了。

**“小家伙”**：吼……！\
**Feufeu**: Rarr!

阿黛拉肩膀上的小生物闻言发出了疑似抗议的叫声，西莉亚隔空拍了拍它的脑袋。\
The tiny creature on Adèle's shoulder lets out something like a protest, prompting Célia to playfully pat its head.

**西莉亚**：“小家伙”不是你的家传神秘术呼唤出来的守护神吗？按理说，只要你还记得我这号人，它就也永远不会忘记。\
**Célia**: Oh, heheh. I know better than that. This sweet little thing was summoned by your family's incantation. As long as you remember, he remembers.

**西莉亚**：它的记忆就是你的记忆，它甚至能读到你自己无法察觉的潜意识。\
**Célia**: Such a fascinating creature, the Tutelary. He sees every corner of your psyche, memory, and sensation, even your unconscious thoughts.

**阿黛拉**：我可听不懂，也记不住这些复杂的理论……这是你现在的研究课题吗？\
**Adèle**: Hah, here comes Cici with another one of her academic lectures. Is this what you're studying these days?

**西莉亚**：是的。\
**Célia**: Yes.

**西莉亚**：罗西教授从一位瑞士心理学家处获得了很多启发，现在正带着整个课题组快速突破，我们的研究已经初有成效了。\
**Célia**: Professor Roseau has found new inspiration in a Swiss psychologist's theories. He's pushing for some new breakthrough; the whole research team's working on it. We've already seen some early progress.

**阿黛拉**：又是那个什么……可收集意识？\
**Adèle**: That ... "collecting brain" thing?

**西莉亚**：是集体潜意识！\
**Célia**: Collective unconscious!

高材生严肃地推了推眼镜，打开手边的笔记本。差生意识到问题不妙。\
She adjusts her glasses with academic rigor and opens her notebook. Her poor student senses trouble.

**阿黛拉**：行，我记住了！我保证——\
**Adèle**: Okay, okay. I won't forget it again.

**西莉亚**：潜意识领域可比你想的要复杂多了，阿黛拉。其中可能还有着能够改变巴黎的关键。\
**Célia**: Says the one who invents a new name for it every time. But it's even more complex than you think, Adèle, and very important. It may even help us make Paris a better city.

**西莉亚**：我们每个人就像是一座座湖中的小岛，有意识的记忆就是岛。\
**Célia**: Imagine the minds of people like islands, each floating on their own,

**西莉亚**：而储存意识不到的记忆的，则是连接我们所有人的这片湖。\
**Célia**: and the collective unconscious as the water that links them all.

**西莉亚**：这就是荣格认为的集体潜意识，它被所有人共享。\
**Célia**: This is Jung's idea of the collective unconscious—a psychic space shared by all of humanity.

**西莉亚**：而战争，贫富差距，神秘学家与人类之间不曾停止的斗争……\
**Célia**: Human aggression—whether it be war, class conflict, or tensions between humans and arcanists—has always been a constant.

**西莉亚**：这些就像是岛上的树木，你砍掉它们后，只要根系还在，就会再次长出。\
**Célia**: It's like the tides affecting the shared ocean between us. We build on our islands, but inevitably the tide will reclaim them.

兴致勃勃的学者合上笔记，用征询的目光抓住了阿黛拉，等待着她的反应。\
The eager scholar closes her notes, fixing Adèle with an expectant look, waiting for her response.

**阿黛拉**：现在大家的日子都不好过，这是事实……可这和我们的潜意识有什么关系呢？难道是我们自己想要这些纷争吗？\
**Adèle**: Maybe this guy's onto something. We're all fighting for our place in these troubled times. But I don't understand what's unconscious about it. Are you saying that, deep down, we're all war-hungry maniacs?

**西莉亚**：当然不是！可它的确是我们集体潜意识的一部分，会在历史中反复上演。\
**Célia**: Certainly not! But we are all under the influence of this collective mind. That's why the same conflicts happen again and again, in all times, in all places, and to all people.

**西莉亚**：想要消除这些代表纷争的树木，就要将它连根拔起。这几乎是不可能的。\
**Célia**: We can't force back the tide, but what if we found a new way to change the ocean itself—fill it with a new nature? One of peace and equality.

但如果我们能够影响到下方的湖，将和平与平等的水流注入湖中呢？

**西莉亚**：哪怕是一股微小的水流，也可能会被树根吸收，进而改变一棵树。\
**Célia**: Even one tiny drop of new thought could make a world of difference.

**西莉亚**：我们的研究就是，如何更加科学且直观地去影响集体潜意识，进而改变大众。\
**Célia**: What we're trying to do is find some way to practically influence the collective unconscious—to create real and lasting change for everyone.

**西莉亚**：这可比任何改革法案都要有效！\
**Célia**: I believe, truly, I believe it could do more to save us than any law or reform ever could!

阿黛拉挠了挠脑袋，她没有这么远大的志向，也无意去改变谁。\
Adèle scratches her head. She has no such lofty ambitions, nor any intention of changing anyone.

**阿黛拉**：所以你们的研究就是……如何控制每一个人的思想？\
**Adèle**: So, you want to control everyone's minds?

**西莉亚**：当然不！个体的思想仍然会得到保留，我们只是留下了那么一个点子。\
**Célia**: What? No! We still want people to think for themselves. We just want to change how they think.

**西莉亚**：把一个美好的愿景留在集体潜意识中，即便短期内不会有成果，但可能性已经存在。\
**Célia**: If we can plant a more hopeful vision into the collective unconscious, we could sow the seeds for a better future for all.

**西莉亚**：雨果想象不到那美好的一天要如何到来，但他还是把梦想都写成了书，并传达给了每个法国人。\
**Célia**: Like how Victor Hugo wrote his dreams into his books, and they reached every reader in France.

**西莉亚**：我们也是如此，不过不依赖于文学创作这类不可控的方式，而是更加科学的手段。\
**Célia**: Only we're doing it in a more controlled, systematic way than simply telling stories.

**阿黛拉**：那文森特呢？他看起来可是个拿破仑狂热分子。\
**Adèle**: What about Vincent? He seems the furthest thing from controlled. Eh, loyalty to "the Emperor" aside.

**阿黛拉**：你们的研究不会有什么风险吗？\
**Adèle**: Are you sure this research is safe?

**西莉亚**：……我不会说“肯定没有”。\
**Célia**: Truthfully, I wouldn't say it's entirely without risk.

**西莉亚**：集体潜意识中有着文明的原始意象，那些在人群中共通的艺术、传说与梦，越是有普遍性，在集体潜意识中就越有影响力。\
**Célia**: The collective unconscious is a sea of primordial images formed into cultural motifs and symbols. The more popular that symbol is—or, the more often a theme occurs across cultures—the more powerful it's said to be in our collective unconscious.

**西莉亚**：文森特应该是“拿破仑”感染了……该说不说，他以前就有这方面的嗜好。\
**Célia**: Take Napoleon, our "conquering hero-king" and cultural symbol. Vincent ... Well, he's always admired him, so perhaps that made him more susceptible.

**西莉亚**：毕竟，改变人的认知总是伴随着精神错乱的风险。在找到安全的研究方法之前，文森特不会是最后一个意外……\
**Célia**: We're working in the mind, so it's understandable that there might be some unforeseen effects. I fear Vincent may not be the last to suffer like this until we find a safer way to proceed.

**阿黛拉**：普遍性……共通的传说……精神错乱……\
**Adèle**: Popular symbols ... Recurring themes ... Mental distress ...

阿黛拉忽然心中一动。\
Adèle pauses as a thought strikes her.

**雷曼女士**：于是它才自百年的沉睡中苏醒，现身于这个时代，将诅咒施加于众人！\
**Madame Raymond**: They have awakened from their centuries-long slumber, bringing torment upon us! We have called them forth. We have set loose this horror ...

是我们唤醒了它——

**阿黛拉**：比如“热沃当的野兽”？\
**Adèle**: Like the Beasts of Gévaudan?

阿黛拉念出了那个在占卜沙龙上听到的名字。\
She repeats what she heard back at the divination salon.

**西莉亚**：你是说最近在城里传得沸沸扬扬的那个？\
**Célia**: That old legend? But why would the Beasts of Gévaudan be ...

但历史上其实根本不存在什么“热沃当的野兽”……

**西莉亚**：等等，也许这说得通。\
**Célia**: Wait, you might actually be onto something.

**西莉亚**：恐惧“热沃当的野兽”的种子通过传言汇入集体潜意识中，接着被个体吸收，然后发芽……\
**Célia**: As the rumors about the beasts have spread, it has gained a new identity in our collective unconsciousness, planting the seeds of terror inside just about everyone.

**西莉亚**：这说得通！\
**Célia**: Formidable!

好友从餐桌上跳起，直扑自己放在一旁的笔记本，开始在上面写写画画了起来。\
Her friend leaps up from the table, dives for her notebook, and starts scribbling frantically.

**西莉亚**：谢谢你，阿黛拉，你总是能够给我提供全新的灵感！我得再去研究一下那幅死亡之舞壁画了——这一切也许都是关联的！\
**Célia**: Thank you, Adèle! You truly are my very own academic muse! I must take another visit to the Dance of Death mural. It may play a part in all of this.

**西莉亚**：等我的研究结果出版，我一定会用稿费给你买一条最漂亮的好运项链！\
**Célia**: I'll buy you one of those good-luck necklaces when I publish my paper!

**阿黛拉**：那你得好好选，我可会每天都戴着它出门的。\
**Adèle**: Then you'd better make sure it's chic. I'll want to wear it every day.

在涉及到自己的研究时，好友往往会展现百倍于平时的热情，阿黛拉对此已见怪不怪。\
When it comes to her research, her friend's enthusiasm is irrepressible. Adèle has long since grown used to it.

**阿黛拉**：你打算去干什么特别的事吗？\
**Adèle**: So, what comes next?

**西莉亚**：没错，不过具体是什么暂且保密，等到我确定了后一定会第一个分享给你的。\
**Célia**: It's only a thought for now—one I must keep to myself. But you'll be the first to know when it's confirmed.

**西莉亚**：我保证你……不，说不定全世界都会为这个发现而震惊。\
**Célia**: I swear, you and indeed the whole world will be shocked!

**西莉亚**：说起来你可别笑我。有时我会觉得自己也是一名城市里的冒险家……用我手中的纸与笔，发掘着埋在厚重历史中的宝藏。\
**Célia**: You know—and please don't laugh—sometimes, I feel like an adventurer too. Hunting for hidden treasures with my pen and paper.

**西莉亚**：某种意义上——就像你的父母一样。\
**Célia**: I suppose what I do isn't all too different from your parents after all.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

**西莉亚**：抱歉，我太激动了……我说得有点多了。\
**Célia**: Forgive me, Adèle. That-that was inconsiderate of me. I got carried away.

**阿黛拉**：他们可算不上什么负责的人，西莉亚。\
**Adèle**: You can find better role models than my parents, Célia.

**阿黛拉**：我最近又收到了他们的来信。里头还是一个劲地在提发现了值钱的矿产，见到了古老壁画之类的。\
**Adèle**: I got another letter from them the other day. It's always the same: a mine sure to bring amazing profits and something about a mural.

**西莉亚**：噢，你已经读了吗？听起来很不错！我是说——真的，我很喜欢这些冒险故事……\
**Célia**: So you do read their letters! They sound exciting, don't you think? You know how much I love adventure stories.

好友骤然积极的态度让阿黛拉哭笑不得。\
Her friend's sudden burst of energy makes Adèle both amused and helpless.

**阿黛拉**：我有时候觉得你才更像塔沃尼尔家的一员。\
**Adèle**: That you do. Sometimes, I think you're more of a Tavernier than I'll ever be.

**西莉亚**：哈哈……是这样就好啦。你明天打算和那位老主顾去哪儿？\
**Célia**: Haha. I suppose I have always thought of you as a sister. Anyway, enough about that. Where are you taking your client tomorrow?

**阿黛拉**：和平街的水晶工房。我有些想确认的事。\
**Adèle**: To Rue de la Paix. There's a crystal parlor we're going to visit.

**西莉亚**：你是不是在想那个占卜师的预言？可别被你的潜意识奴役，阿黛拉……\
**Célia**: Because of what that diviner told you? You must be the master of your own will, Adèle. Don't let your subconscious make all the decisions.

**阿黛拉**：又到了你的专业领域是吗？\
**Adèle**: Whatever you say, Madame Professor.

**西莉亚**：我说了，绝大多数问题的根源都在人们的脑海深处……\
**Célia**: I mean it! So many things in life are stirred up from the depths of our minds.

阔别许久的好友间总有说不尽的话，也不知过了多久，星星占据了整片天空，在夜幕中闪耀。\
There's never an end to the things old friends have to say. They talk until the stars have claimed the night sky.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚，你说，世上真的有命运吗？\
**Adèle**: Cici, tell me, do you really think there's such a thing as fate?

**阿黛拉**：嗯？西莉亚？\
**Adèle**: Cici? Célia?

友人已进入了梦乡，奔赴了某个尚未和阿黛拉在“集体潜意识的海洋”中连通的梦境。\
Her friend drifts off to sleep, wandering into some dream not yet connected to Adèle's in that sea of collective unconscious.

**阿黛拉**：好吧，晚安……祝我俩明天都一路平安。\
**Adèle**: Well then. Good night, dear friend. May tomorrow bring good luck to both of us.

**执夜人**：于是第二天，你前往了贝丽尔·布翁尼的水晶工房。\
**Vigil Officer**: And it was on the following day that you paid a visit to Beryl Bouanich's Parlor of Crystals?

**灰调蓝**：是的。\
**Brume**: Correct.

**执夜人**：你说你在那里接受了一场“奇异的占卜”。\
**Vigil Officer**: And there, you had another, ah, what did you call it? Unusual divination?

**灰调蓝**：贝丽尔·布翁尼……她早就预见了我的造访。\
**Brume**: Beryl Bouanich had foreseen my visit long before I arrived.

**灰调蓝**：正如她早就预见了在那之后发生的一切。\
**Brume**: Just as she had foreseen all that came afterward.

## AFF-05 所有映照万物的光 / Light That Illuminates All

旺多姆广场上的人越来越多，从四面八方的街巷里汇集的人流积聚于此。\
A dizzying crowd has filled Place Vendôme, flowing in from every direction.

年轻的司机靠在车门边，边打量着过路人群，边踢动脚下的小石子。\
The young driver leans against her car door, kicking at a small stone while watching the passersby.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安说是今天在这里见面，也不留个时间……我不会得等到晚上吧！\
**Adèle**: "Tomorrow ..." She never said the time. She's not planning to keep me waiting until the evening, is she?

**阿黛拉**：难道她已经进去了？\
**Adèle**: Or has she already gone in?

她转过头，水晶工房那扇漂亮的雕花木门和两三个小时前一样紧闭着。\
She turns her head. The ornate carved door of the Parlor of Crystals is shut and shuttered, just as it was a few hours ago.

**阿黛拉**：再试一次，这个时间了，店里总该有人在……\
**Adèle**: Should I knock again? Someone must be in at this hour.

**阿黛拉**：您好——\
**Adèle**: Hello?

这次没费多大力气，木门刚被叩响，就顺势朝两侧敞开。\
This time, the door opens the very moment she knocks.

一条灯光昏暗的长廊等待着她。\
But once it does, all she can see is the dim corridor ahead.

**阿黛拉**：嗯？终于开门了。是我之前敲门的方式不对？\
**Adèle**: Ah, finally. Perhaps they didn't hear me knocking before?

**阿黛拉**：也没看到有店员在附近。算了，先进去问问。\
**Adèle**: Er, hello? Right, I suppose I'll just let myself in.

她踏入走廊。脚步落下的瞬间，那一点儿仅有的光线也熄灭了。\
She steps inside. But the very instant her foot touches the floor, the last trace of light vanishes.

幼龙的火焰勉强映亮了周围，它没精打采地甩动尾巴。\
The tiny dragon's flame barely lights the way, its tail swishing weakly.

**阿黛拉**：我说，至少给新顾客留下些照明吧！\
**Adèle**: They could at least leave a light on for the customers.

**阿黛拉**：你们好——有谁见到了一位趾高气昂的小姐吗？\
**Adèle**: Hello? Anyone here? I think my "friend" arrived before me. She's about this tall—just enough to always be looking down her nose at you?

阿黛拉伸手摸索着墙壁，凭借刚才的记忆前进。\
Adèle reaches out along the wall, feeling her way forward from memory.

**“小家伙”**：——嗷！\
**Feufeu**: Grrrh!

**阿黛拉**：有新发现吗？\
**Adèle**: What is it, Feufeu?

循着幼龙仰起的脑袋望过去，前方闪动着几个尖耳朵的透明身影。\
Following the dragon's upward gaze, she spots a few faint, translucent figures with pointed ears.

**？？？**：～♪\
**???**: ～♪

**阿黛拉**：我怎么会忘了，有占卜师在的地方，总有这种小东西！\
**Adèle**: Sprites. Of course. Where else would they be, if not in a diviner's parlor?

**阿黛拉**：别和我捣乱，我现在可没空了解你们又偷了些什么！\
**Adèle**: Let me be clear. I don't care what kind of mischief you're up to in here. Just don't let it involve me!

妖精们尖叫着拍打身上的火焰。尽管并不会被灼伤，它们还是结结实实地吓了一跳。\
The sprites shriek, batting at the harmless flames licking their bodies. Even if they can't be burned, the fright is real enough.

**阿黛拉**：你们成天恶作剧，也该尝尝被捉弄的滋味了。\
**Adèle**: Heh. Not so funny when the joke's on you, huh?

**阿黛拉**：给我带路，听到没有？\
**Adèle**: Now, lead on. Bring me to the owner of this place, understood?

**占卜妖精**：♮♭♮♯♭♯♮♯♭！\
**Divination Sprite**: ♮♭♮♯♭♯♮♯♭!

阿黛拉没理会它们的痛骂。妖精们将她领到了一扇小门前，从透着光的缝隙中挤了进去。\
Ignoring what sounds like their tiny frustrated protests, she follows the sprites to a door. Each one of them slipping inside ahead of her through the glowing crack.

她再次推门。\
She pushes it wide open.

一间由光编织成的屋子。\
The room looks as if it were woven from a million scattered threads of light.

阿黛拉的脑中浮出这个念头。她注视着那些剔透的、闪烁的、折射光芒的水晶，空气中的尘埃在流光里镀金。\
The thought crosses Adèle's mind as she takes in the transparent, shimmering crystals around her, their reflections gilding the dust in the air.

在这间屋子里，每呼吸一次，就咽下矿物的魂魄。\
Here, every breath she takes seems to take in some of the shimmering light, almost like she is devouring the very spirit of the crystals.

**阿黛拉**：……真美丽。\
**Adèle**: How pretty.

**阿黛拉**：我从来没有见过这样的工房……\
**Adèle**: Never seen a parlor quite like this. The way these crystals are displayed ... It feels like they're not meant for sale or for exhibition.

它……它们的摆放方式，不像是为了销售或展览……

她尽可能放轻了呼吸，来削减自己的存在，好融入这片光彩。\
She breathes as softly and shallowly as she can, attempting to blend into the light.

**阿黛拉**：是巧妙的灯光布设让这些水晶变得特别？或者……\
**Adèle**: Is it the lighting that's giving them such an otherworldly glow? Or maybe ...

**？？？**：——哦，也许你想说的是……“辉耀”。它会藉由水晶显现。\
**???**: Perhaps you are thinking of the Sephirot. When captured, they may be manifested through crystals.

远处的声音悦耳而明亮，像轻敲一只玻璃杯。\
A voice echoes from afar—bright, clear, like the sound of gentle tapping on a glass pane.

**？？？**：曾有人说，“辉耀”是神用来创造世界的工具，也是祂不可分割的一部分。\
**???**: Some believe it is through these Sephirot that the creator formed our world. Without them, the divinity is incomplete.

**？？？**：十辉耀……是星界之光、燃烧荆棘的火焰、生命之树顶端的光辉，是“数字”、“圆球”、“漫长的时代”——\
**???**: The ten Sephirot ... The astral light, the flames of the fire which burned in the bush, the glowing stream which flows from the Tree of Life, the "numerals," "spheres," "enos"—

**？？？**：——也是万事万物。\
**???**: —and all aspects of reality.

**阿黛拉**：抱歉，您是……\
**Adèle**: Ah, then you must be ...

**阿黛拉**：贝丽尔·布翁尼女士……？\
**Adèle**: Madame Beryl Bouanich?

工房主人微笑着点头。无需证明，见过她的人都会立刻明了她的身份。\
The shop's owner smiles and nods. No further explanation is needed. Anyone who's seen her would know exactly who she is.

她伸出手，用指尖轻触一枚光芒柔和的灵摆。\
She extends her hand, brushing a softly glowing pendulum with her fingertips.

**贝丽尔**：通过一些特定的物品、仪式，或是与生俱来的灵知与天性，我们偶尔可以捕捉那些光辉。\
**Beryl**: Through certain objects and rituals—or by gnosis gifted at birth—we may catch a glimpse of a splendor that is not of this world.

**贝丽尔**：水晶正是少数具有这种非凡性的存在之一。在它的帮助下，我们得以自意象的宝库中，窥探世界灵魂的奥秘。\
**Beryl**: These crystals are one such object. In their reflection, we are shown the hidden secrets of the Archive of Imagery.

柔和的话语使阿黛拉略微放松了一些。尽管她没有注意分辨句子的内容。\
Her voice soothes Adèle's nerves, though it comes out so softly that she struggles to register the meaning.

**阿黛拉**：请问您……\
**Adèle**: Madame, did you ...

**贝丽尔**：请先随我到里面的贵宾室去吧。这扇门本就是为你而留的。\
**Beryl**: I am pleased that you have made your way here, Madame Tavernier. That door was left open just for you.

松软的玛德琳蛋糕很好地抚平了阿黛拉的不安。

她端起茶杯，嗅着大吉岭茶的浓郁香气，原本的紧张悄悄消退。\
Her teacup exudes the calming floral scents of Darjeeling, and with each bite of Madeleine cake, her remaining tension melts along with the buttery richness.

**阿黛拉**：您今天并没有见到我以外的其他人……我明白了。\
**Adèle**: So I'm the first one here. I see.

**阿黛拉**：而您之所以出现在那间占卜沙龙，是为了追回流出工房的劣质水晶？\
**Adèle**: And you were at Madame Raymond's salon the other day to retrieve your crystals?

**贝丽尔**：近些日子我忙于海外的生意，这才放松了对工房的管理。\
**Beryl**: Indeed I was. I have been occupied in business overseas and neglected the security of this parlor.

**贝丽尔**：我没能注意到有人在偷卖应该废弃的残次品。\
**Beryl**: Someone has been taking my defective crystals and pawning them off to other diviners.

**贝丽尔**：虽然加工后足够瞒过外行的眼睛，但毫无疑问会影响仪式的稳定性。我必须为顾客的安全和工房的声誉负责。\
**Beryl**: Few are able to detect their flaws. But, minute as they are, they render them hazardous for ritual use. I must act before any further harm is done.

她看向阿黛拉，笑容又柔和了一些。\
She looks toward Adèle, her expression softer still, sweeter still, despite her words of caution.

**贝丽尔**：我需要再次向你表示感谢，塔沃尼尔小姐。\
**Beryl**: For that, I owe you my thanks, Madame Tavernier.

**贝丽尔**：你当时的举动为我免去了许多麻烦。\
**Beryl**: You showed courage that day, in your words and actions.

**阿黛拉**：您叫我阿黛拉就可以。以及您不用向我道谢。\
**Adèle**: Just Adèle will do. And there's really no need to thank me.

**阿黛拉**：毕竟我最开始也没打算插手……正巧那位占卜师自己找上了我。\
**Adèle**: Truth be told, I probably wouldn't have interfered if the diviner hadn't tried to make a fool of me.

**贝丽尔**：噢。她的预言让你有些困扰，是吗？\
**Beryl**: Ah. Those words still bother you, do they not?

**阿黛拉**：您还记得？其实我本来打算听听就忘掉的。\
**Adèle**: No, not at all. I don't take things like that seriously, you know.

**阿黛拉**：命运——命运，其实就是看你愿意信什么，不信什么，对吧？\
**Adèle**: After all, fate—it's just a matter of belief, isn't it?

**贝丽尔**：但你无法彻底忘记。因为其中有些模糊的话语令你心生怀疑。\
**Beryl**: You do not believe, yet you cannot seem to put it out of mind. Is that so?

**阿黛拉**：哈哈，您真的和那些占卜师不太一样。\
**Adèle**: Hah. Please, madame. You aren't about to start with the prophecies like all the others, are you?

她再次举起茶杯，朝椅背上靠去。\
She raises her cup again and reclines against the chair.

**阿黛拉**：无意冒犯——我并非认为预言家都是骗子。\
**Adèle**: Forgive me. It's not that I think all diviners are liars. It's just that it's hard to believe that fate is shaped by any kind of higher power. It seems just as likely to me that most divinations are simply self-fulfilling prophecies.

只是一旦你知道它，多少就会被影响判断。

**阿黛拉**：这种仿佛后脑勺时刻被人监视的感觉……让我不太舒服。\
**Adèle**: And whether they be from a higher power or a crystal ball, I won't let prophecies dictate my life.

**阿黛拉**：也许“命运”真的会在该来的时候来，但在那之前我可不想被它裹挟。\
**Adèle**: If I have a fate—some road I'm destined to travel—then I will first go as far as I can down every other road until it's the only option I have left.

**阿黛拉**：我还年轻——我还有很多想做的事儿呢！\
**Adèle**: There's still so much I want to do!

工房主人轻笑着，似乎很乐于听到这样充满活力的宣言。\
But the woman only laughs, not with mocking laughter but with something like genuine delight at her words.

**贝丽尔**：对我来说，命运只是某种既定的规律。就像水晶折射的光线、奔流不息的水流。\
**Beryl**: Fate, dear, is a universal law—the cause and effect of all events. Just as the path of light through a crystal may be predicted to find its refraction, one road inevitably leads to another.

**贝丽尔**：有人说命运无常。有人认为它由始至终已被写好。\
**Beryl**: While some believe our paths to be unpredictable, others see them as written from beginning to end.

**贝丽尔**：而在我看来，它存在着，但其中并无人们苦苦寻找的“意义”。\
**Beryl**: But there is little use in searching for "meaning" in such a thing as fate.

**贝丽尔**：占卜告诉我你今天会来拜访，然后你来了。事情如此发生，仅此而已。\
**Beryl**: My reading foresaw your coming today, and here you are. The light passes through the crystal and falls as it must, as it ever was to be.

**阿黛拉**：等等……那您有没有在占卜里看到我的朋友？\
**Adèle**: You knew I'd come? Then, what about my friend?

**贝丽尔**：我看见的只是你一个人。\
**Beryl**: I saw only you.

**阿黛拉**：好吧，她连来都没来！放了我一天鸽子，她到底跑哪儿去了……\
**Adèle**: Damn! She didn't even bother to come! What is she thinking?

阿黛拉困扰地念叨着。而贝丽尔已经抛出了下一个问题。\
Adèle mumbles in confusion, but Beryl has already moved along to the next question.

**贝丽尔**：你只是因为约定才来到这里吗？\
**Beryl**: You came here only to find your friend?

**阿黛拉**：这……我的确只是因为……\
**Adèle**: I, well, yes, you could say that.

贝丽尔的目光模糊而缥缈，似乎并非望向眼前的人。\
Beryl's eyes track away, gazing out distant and unfocused, as if she wasn't aware of the person in front of her at all.

**贝丽尔**：你为你的疑惑而来。这份疑惑并非源于不信，而是因为相信它正要灵验。\
**Beryl**: There is something more—a question, not about the truth of fate, but of how you might act upon it.

**贝丽尔**：你们家族中每一个人都知道的命运，塔沃尼尔的诅咒……抑或者是“塔沃尼尔的冒险”。\
**Beryl**: The curse in your family, or as some may call it, the path of the Tavernier.

**贝丽尔**：你怀疑现在正是它开启的时刻，是吗？\
**Beryl**: You wonder whether it is your time to walk it, do you not?

**阿黛拉**：——！\
**Adèle**: ...!

**雷曼女士**：你注定逃不过宿命的感召！怀有私心的贤者将玩弄你的命运，死亡的深渊正等待你坠入……\
**Madame Raymond**: The call must be answered! Walk with the wise, but beware their words. Beware the gaping abyss of death.

**雷曼女士**：而那地之上的，终将等同那天之下的……你所有的终将消失，死亡亦将引导你最终的升华……\
**Madame Raymond**: What lies below shall reflect what lies above—one shall ascend, but all must be paid.

**雷曼女士**：直到一切都回归！回归那——\
**Madame Raymond**: All must return! All must restore—

**阿黛拉**：怪了，为什么我这两天遇到的所有占卜师都知道“塔沃尼尔的诅咒”……\
**Adèle**: How come every diviner I meet these days seems to know about that curse?

**阿黛拉**：难道这真的有那么出名吗？\
**Adèle**: Is obscure jewel lore really so popular in this city?

阿黛拉玩笑般抛出这句话。面对这个话题，她向来态度如此。\
Adèle says it like a joke. That's how she always treats the subject.

比起恐惧，戏谑更好。\
Mockery felt better to her than fear.

而贝丽尔只点了点头作为回应。\
Beryl only nods in reply.

**贝丽尔**：某种意义上来说，雷曼女士当时确实窥见了命运——只是不小心看到了太多，招致了预料之外的不幸。\
**Beryl**: Madame Raymond foresaw the future, but she peeked too far, and for that, paid dearly.

**阿黛拉**：什么？您的意思是说——\
**Adèle**: You mean ...

她还是不愿听见这样的答案。\
She still doesn't want to hear that kind of answer.

**阿黛拉**：不不，应该不是我想的那样吧……\
**Adèle**: No, no, no. Please tell me you're just teasing me.

**阿黛拉**：我还以为她是出现幻觉才活活吓死的！\
**Adèle**: You're saying that it wasn't her fear of the Beasts of Gévaudan that killed her but what she saw in my future?

你看，毕竟她死前还说着什么“热沃当的野兽”……

**贝丽尔**：别着急，阿黛拉小姐。我说了是“某种意义上”。\
**Beryl**: Please, Adèle. Allow me to finish.

贝丽尔摇了摇头，平和的语气轻飘飘地托举住了阿黛拉下坠的心。\
Beryl shakes her head. Somehow just that gesture alone is enough to lift her heart.

——随后，却又紧紧攥住了她不安跳动的心脏。\
—Only for her next words to put it right back into a vise grip.

**贝丽尔**：她看见的“命运”并不完全属于你——因为你的身上，正附着另一个阴影。\
**Beryl**: The fate she saw was not entirely yours. There is a shadow which lingers on you.

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉小姐，你的确中了某种诅咒。\
**Beryl**: In a way, it is true. You are indeed cursed.

## AFF-06 午夜咖啡 / Midnight Café

**贝丽尔**：万物都有自己的能量，而我们远比我们所以为的更擅于感受它们。\
**Beryl**: All things carry energy, and we are much more perceptive to it than we think.

**贝丽尔**：集中精神，尝试捕捉任何细微的变化。\
**Beryl**: Now, I would ask that you concentrate on the subtle changes around you. You will sense it; you simply need to feel.

当你注意到它的时候，你会意识到“就是它”。

**阿黛拉**：好的，我明白了。\
**Adèle**: Yes, I'll try.

**贝丽尔**：请告诉我，阿黛拉小姐——哪一颗水晶最吸引你？\
**Beryl**: Tell me, Adèle, which of these crystals draws you the most?

阿黛拉凝视着整齐码放在托盘中、令人眼花缭乱的一排排水晶。\
Adèle stares at the tray, rows of crystals lined up neatly, dazzling to the eye.

几次呼吸后，她将手伸向了位于倒数第二排第三个的那颗。\
After a few steady breaths, she reaches toward the third crystal from the end of the second row.

**阿黛拉**：我想……是这个。\
**Adèle**: Maybe this one.

一块茶褐色的水晶，神秘而神圣的烟雾被冻结其中。\
A tea-brown crystal—mysterious, sacred, its smoke frozen within.

**贝丽尔**：产自巴西的烟晶。\
**Beryl**: A smoky quartz from Brazil. Very good.

**贝丽尔**：它能够引导负向的能量转为正向，帮助持有者稳固精神，破除威胁灵魂的祸殃。\
**Beryl**: This crystal turns negative energy positive. It is a peace-bringer—a banisher of the dangers that trouble one's soul.

**贝丽尔**：请闭上眼睛。\
**Beryl**: Now, close your eyes.

**贝丽尔**：<speed=0.28>——双音有七，万物均如是，辉耀于此化形。\
**Beryl**: <speed=0.05>Seven doubles, seven gates—seven in all reveal the Sephirot.

**贝丽尔**：保持呼吸的规律。往暗处看，你会注意到一些光。\
**Beryl**: Keep your breath steady and look into the darkness—search for the light.

**阿黛拉**：我找到了。很微弱……但确实存在。\
**Adèle**: I see it. Only a soft glow. But it's there.

**贝丽尔**：跟上它。\
**Beryl**: Take it.

**阿黛拉**：是想象它离得更近？还是我走过去？我……\
**Adèle**: How? Do I make it come to me, or should I go towards it? I—

意识在下沉，或向内挤压。\
Her consciousness sinks, or folds inward.

万物沿着思绪流淌，汇入躯壳，又猛然逸散。\
Everything flows through her mind, pours back into her body, then bursts outward again.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

**？？？**：阿黛拉，醒醒——\
**???**: Adèle? Come on, wake up!

**阿黛拉**：唔…………\
**Adèle**: Mm ...

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

**？？？**：你这个懒虫，快给我醒醒！\
**???**: Wake up! Good heavens, how do you live like this!

**阿黛拉**：呃？！\
**Adèle**: Huh?

她扶着脑袋站起身，面前的人伸出手指，愤怒地点了点她的额头。\
She stands, holding her head. The figure before her reaches out and flicks her forehead in anger.

**费利西安**：现在睡醒了？我找了你一整天，没想到你躲在这里消极怠工！\
**Félicienne**: "Huh?" "Good morning," I think you meant to say. I've been looking all over for you, and here you are napping like a pampered cat!

**费利西安**：你还真会享受，知道工房里的沙发比你的车舒服。\
**Félicienne**: You certainly know how to enjoy yourself, don't you? Abandoning me to take a doze in this cushy parlor.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安？！你怎么现在才——我在门口等了你很久，可你一直没出现，然后……\
**Adèle**: Félicienne?! Where were you? I was waiting in the street for hours! You never turned up, so I had to—

**阿黛拉**：奇怪，我记得……贝丽尔女士……\
**Adèle**: Where's Madame Bouanich? Beryl ... She ...

词语在她舌尖打了几个滚，却无法顺利地组成句子。\
Words tumble on her tongue but refuse to form a sentence.

**费利西安**：少做梦了，你自己看看周围，那些家伙早就收工回去了——谁还会特意来找你？\
**Félicienne**: Still dreaming? Look around you. The parlor's already closed.

阿黛拉仔细地扫视一圈，昏暗的房间里的确没有第三人在场。\
Adèle scans the room. They're the only ones there.

**费利西安**：要不是我，等早上你多半会被当成潜进工房的贼抓起来。\
**Félicienne**: You'd likely have woken up behind bars for trespassing if I hadn't come to collect you.

**费利西安**：这里也没什么好看的。走吧，还来得及去逛逛。\
**Félicienne**: What a shame! This place seems more tedious than I thought. Come on, get up. We still have time to look elsewhere.

**阿黛拉**：噢……好。我去开车，我好像把它停在了后门。\
**Adèle**: Oh. Of course. I'll fetch the car. It's by the back door.

**费利西安**：我现在不想坐车。\
**Félicienne**: No, not the car. I'd rather not get into that deathtrap for a while.

费利西安径直穿过走廊，推开正门，带着阿黛拉回到街上。\
Félicienne walks straight through the corridor, pushes open the main door, and takes Adèle back into the street.

夜深沉且寂静。无论是偌大的广场，还是平时熙攘的河岸，都不见一个人影。\
The night is pitch black and silent. The wide square and ever-lively riverbank are strangely deserted.

**阿黛拉**：没听说今天要实行宵禁，人都哪儿去了？\
**Adèle**: The street's totally empty. Where is everyone? Is there a curfew that I didn't know of?

**阿黛拉**：这些房子里连一盏灯都不开……街灯也没有点亮。\
**Adèle**: The street lamps are off. Huh, I don't even see lights on in any windows.

**费利西安**：你真是睡得昏了头，还好我没答应你开车出来。\
**Félicienne**: What is wrong with you? Heaven's sake, it's a good thing I didn't let you behind the wheel.

**费利西安**：那儿不是亮着吗？\
**Félicienne**: Look. Is that not a light right over there?

无人的夜中亮起一间灯火通明的咖啡馆。\
A bright café glows amid the empty darkness. Clusters of flowers hang around its name so thick they almost swallow the sign.

大团的花簇垂坠而下，几乎将整块招牌吞没。

**阿黛拉**：……花神咖啡馆？\
**Adèle**: Is that Café de Flore?

**阿黛拉**：他们的营业时间有这么长吗？我之前都没注意……\
**Adèle**: Do they really stay open so late? Hmm. I suppose I've never checked.

**费利西安**：去给我买点吃的。我不想进去，里面太吵了。\
**Félicienne**: I'm starving. Go see if they have any food. I'll wait outside.

她推了阿黛拉一把，玻璃门敞开，那团明晃晃的光瞬间淌满了街道。\
She nudges Adèle forward. The glass door swings open, and bright light spills out into the street.

即使是深夜，咖啡馆仍然接近满座。\
Even this late, the café is near to bursting with life.

阿黛拉边走向柜台，边猜测这些客人的来处。左岸的某个艺术小团体，或者刚结束戏剧排练的演员……\
Adèle walks toward the counter, wondering who these patrons might be—some left-bank art group, or theater folk fresh from rehearsal ...

**客人？**：是的，乔治·巴塔耶正在为他的社团招募刽子手。\
**Customer?**: As I was saying, Georges Bataille is looking for executioners for his secret society.

**客人？**：是的，刽子手，他和他所有的社团成员都宁愿成为活祭仪式上的祭品，却没有人愿意当刽子手。\
**Customer?**: Executioners—that's right! Every one of the members would rather be sacrificed in the ritual than be the one to swing the axe.

**客人？**：这些越轨分子竟然没有胆量对他人施暴，我该说他们善良吗？\
**Customer?**: Ha! Who would have thought? The norm breakers can't even bring themselves to commit violence. Is it a mercy or just selfish martyrdom?

**客人？**：你看过大木偶剧场的新剧了吗？杰克·若文根本就不是那块料。\
**Customer?**: Did you see the last performance at the Théâtre du Grand-Guignol? Jack Jouvin has been the worst director I've ever seen.

**客人？**：我们所向往的血腥与肢解都被他所谓的戏剧性给冲淡了，那个喜欢卖弄自我的肥猪就这样把大木偶剧场变成了上演蹩脚滑稽戏的地方。\
**Customer?**: He ruined all the gory scenes with his so-called theatrics. What a self-absorbed man! It's hardly a theater anymore—more like a circus.

**客人？**：我想要在恐怖的舞台前昏厥，而不是被他气晕！说真的，我很想念我美丽的马克萨，她的每一次死亡我都忘不掉。\
**Customer?**: I wanted to gasp at the sight of shattered bones and slit throats, not from sheer disappointment! Honestly, I miss dear Paula Maxa. Every death she brought to the stage was impeccable.

**客人？**：换句话说，一个时代所有人都认为某个东西存在，这个东西就会真的存在？\
**Customer?**: Miss, I must confess I'm confused. You're saying that something will just pop into existence if everyone believes it exists?

**客人？**：根据我最新的研究，或许问题的关键就在人们的共通想象之中。\
**Customer?**: In a manner of speaking, yes. According to the studies we've been conducting, the answer may be hidden in our collective imagination.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚？！\
**Adèle**: Célia!

她喊出的名字像一把骤然落下的刀，轻易地撕裂了这块画布。\
The name cuts through the air like a blade, slicing the animated canvas around them apart.

大厅里的声音都消失了。只剩下她后退时鞋跟摩擦地面的细碎响动。\
Every sound in the hall vanishes, leaving only the scrape of her heels retreating against the floor.

所有客人在同一时间转过头，一动不动地注视着这名莽撞的闯入者。\
All the customers turn toward her in unison, motionless, eyes locked on the intruder.

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉？你来了！我还以为你对我们的研究不感兴趣……\
**Célia**: Adèle? What a surprise! I thought you had no interest in my studies.

好友轻快地小跑过来，阿黛拉紧盯着她，无法挪开视线。\
Her friend slinks over to her. Adèle holds a dumbfounded stare, completely unsure of what she's seeing.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

她的目光紧锁在西莉亚背后蠕动的黑暗中。客人们的轮廓逐渐消融，取而代之的是獠牙与……皮毛。\
She fixes on the darkness writhing behind Célia's back. The outlines of the customers melt away, replaced by fangs and ... fur.

**西莉亚**：你的脸色好差……留下来和我们一块吃些东西吧？不会耽误多久……\
**Célia**: You look pale. Come, sit with us, and have a bite to eat. It won't take long.

**西莉亚**：啊！\
**Célia**: Ah!

阿黛拉攥住好友的手腕，猛地将她扯到身边，冲向身后的玻璃门。\
Adèle grabs her friend's wrist, yanking her close as they sprint for the glass door behind them.

**阿黛拉**：快走！\
**Adèle**: We need to go, Célia!

**西莉亚**：好痛——怎么了？阿黛拉！阿黛拉——\
**Célia**: You're hurting me. What's going on? Adèle? Ah!

她勉强回过头，望向身后的同伴——\
She glances back.

那些面孔已经无法辨认。皮肉融化成肮脏泥泞的粘稠液体，坠入桌边的黑暗。\
Their faces are no longer recognizable. Mounds of dark flesh melt into a filthy, oozing slurry that drips into the surrounding dark.

属于人的部分在剥落，而闪动的幽火冉冉上升。\
What's left of their human parts peels away, and a ghostly fire drifts upward around them.

**？？？**：——\
**???**: *roar*

砰——！\
*bang*

**阿黛拉**：该死，车停在巷子里……西莉亚，跟紧我！\
**Adèle**: Damn it, the car—it's still in the alley! Célia, stay close!

**阿黛拉**：费利西安，快跑！\
**Adèle**: Félicienne! Run!

她冲出门时，街道上空无一人。

阿黛拉第一次由衷地祈祷费利西安贯彻了任性的作风，她最好是已经独自离开。\
When she bursts through the door, the streets are empty. Adèle finds herself actually hoping that Félicienne stuck to her stubborn ways and she's already long gone.

**热沃当的野兽**：——！\
**Beast of Gévaudan**: ...!

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚，到我前面来——\
**Adèle**: Go on ahead, Célia.

她刚想转过身为西莉亚争取一点逃跑的时间，引擎的轰鸣已迅速逼近，甚至盖过了野兽的吼叫。\
She tries to turn, intending to buy Célia a few more seconds to escape, but the roar of an engine drowns out even the beast's howl.

**司机**：快上车！\
**Driver**: Get in!

**阿黛拉**：你是……白天的那个司机！你不是被送去接受治疗了吗？\
**Adèle**: You! Wait, shouldn't you be in the hospital?

**阿黛拉**：不管了，先上车！\
**Adèle**: Ah, you can explain later. Célia, get in the car!

她一把拉开车门，将恍惚的西莉亚推上去，自己也跳进了后座。\
She yanks the car door open, shoves the dazed Célia inside, then jumps into the back seat.

**阿黛拉**：快点！把油门踩到底！\
**Adèle**: Go! Go! Hit the gas!

## AFF-07 好梦，朋友 / "Sweet Dreams"

**阿黛拉**：你还好吗，西莉亚？\
**Adèle**: Are you alright?

友人疲惫地点头，努力地平复呼吸。跑得太急了，她的脸色在灯光下格外苍白。\
Her friend nods, catching her breath. But Adèle cannot help but notice how pale she is—far too pale—beneath the yellowy glow of the street lamps.

**阿黛拉**：没事就行，我相信你有分寸……\
**Adèle**: Good. I knew you were tougher than that.

阿黛拉松了一口气，凑近车窗，看见几道黑影被远远甩开，消失在身后的夜色中。\
Adèle exhales, leaning toward the window to see the shadows fade behind them into the night.

**阿黛拉**：哈——就算有四条腿，也跑不过四个轮子。\
**Adèle**: Hah. Even with twice the legs, they still couldn't outrun us.

**阿黛拉**：文森特先生——没错吧？我们的车不久前“打过照面”。\
**Adèle**: Er, Mr. Vincent, yes? We bumped into each other yesterday, remember?

**阿黛拉**：多亏您出现得及时！不过，我还以为您会多休息一段时间……\
**Adèle**: I appreciate the help. You came just in time! But shouldn't you still be in a hospital bed?

**文森特**：法语里没有不可能这个词！我的康复之日早已临近！\
**Vincent**: There is no "impossible" in French. I was back on my feet in no time!

司机短促地笑了两声。他再一次加大油门。\
The driver lets out two short, rough laughs and slams on the accelerator again.

**阿黛拉**：是吗？祝您早日恢复健康。\
**Adèle**: Bravo, sir. Glad to see you're doing well.
