**西莉亚**：阿黛拉……\
**Célia**: Adèle ...

友人拍了拍阿黛拉的肩膀，但没能立刻引起注意。\
Her friend pats Adèle's shoulder, but she doesn't notice.

**阿黛拉**：您刚才在咖啡馆门口见过其他人吗？\
**Adèle**: Did you notice anyone waiting outside the café earlier, Vincent?

**文森特**：没有。\
**Vincent**: No.

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉，别再问了——我觉得——\
**Célia**: Adèle, please. Something feels wrong.

阿黛拉握了握她的手，向前倾身，离驾驶座近了些。\
Adèle squeezes her hand, leaning forward, closer to the driver's seat.

**阿黛拉**：我刚发现，您副驾驶车窗上的口红痕迹，很像我的一个朋友留下的。\
**Adèle**: Those lipstick marks on your passenger window. Rude, wouldn't you say?

**阿黛拉**：这太巧了。和她写在我车上的句子一样、位置一样——连不小心抹掉的一个角都一样！\
**Adèle**: People really need to learn where to put their lipstick these days, huh? Funny that you got the same message, in the same spot, with the same smudges!

**阿黛拉**：我早就把痕迹擦掉了。可它为什么出现在你的车上？这真的是你的车吗？\
**Adèle**: But I wiped it off yesterday. And how did it get here? Where did you get this car?

**阿黛拉**：或者——这一切根本就是一个噩梦！\
**Adèle**: Or is this even real? Am I in a dream?

**西莉亚**：你一定是太累，才以为自己在做梦，问出这么奇怪的话……\
**Célia**: You're speaking nonsense, Adèle. How could this not be real? Have you been sleeping alright?

**阿黛拉**：够了！难道你就不是我梦见的假货吗？！\
**Adèle**: Enough, Cici! You're just a part of this nightmare like everything else!

西莉亚睁大眼睛，她看起来越发虚弱了，像一支无力燃烧的白蜡烛。\
Célia's eyes go wide. She's looking weaker by the moment, like a candle burning out the last of its wick.

**西莉亚**：……啊。\
**Célia**: Ah.

车已经没有再往前行驶。它悬置在一片黑暗中。\
The car isn't moving forward or backward now. It seems to simply hang suspended in darkness.

幼龙攀上了驾驶座的靠背，跳到司机肩上。\
Her dragon climbs up the seatback and leaps onto Adèle's shoulder.

**阿黛拉**：唯以真知炼化虚妄！\
**Adèle**: By fire, what is false is purged.

在火焰灼烧之下，兽类的尖牙撕裂了属于人的躯壳。\
Under the flame's glare, the beast's fangs rip through the man's human shell.

**“文森特”**：——！\
**"Vincent"**: ...!

“文森特”跳出车窗，扭曲的身影立刻被夜色吞没。\
The beast that once was "Vincent" leaps out the window, his twisted form swallowed up by the abyssal night.

阿黛拉感到胃里一阵烧灼般的疼痛。她错觉那片黑暗生有绒毛、尖牙，属于一只更庞大的兽类，从靠近的身躯上榨出粘稠的血。\
Adèle's stomach twists. In the dark, she imagines fur, fangs—something larger, hungrier—draining blood from a fallen body.

它守着满腹饥饿等待许久，直至今日。\
It had waited, starving, until now.

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉！阿黛拉——阿黛拉！\
**Célia**: Adèle? Adèle! Adèle!

**阿黛拉**：你——\
**Adèle**: You—

在她回神前，幼龙的尾巴已经卷上西莉亚的手臂。但火焰只燃起了一瞬，比一道呼吸更短暂。\
Before she can react, her dragon's tail coils around Célia's arm. The flame flares for a heartbeat—no longer.

**阿黛拉**：你真的是——？\
**Adèle**: You're really—

她没来得及说完下文，西莉亚已经猛地握住了她的手。\
Célia seizes her hand.

**西莉亚**：听我说！阿黛拉！我想起来了！我知道了“热沃当的野兽”是怎么回事——\
**Célia**: Listen to me, Adèle! I remember now. I know the truth about the Beasts of Gévaudan—

**西莉亚**：“重塑之手”撬开了意象宝库，导致了所有的癔症和失踪案！再这样下去，他们会毁掉整个巴黎！\
**Célia**: Manus Vindictae cracked open the Archive of Imagery! That's what's been causing all the disappearances and madness! They're trying to destroy Paris!

**西莉亚**：不要相信罗西教授，不要急着来找我，你必须先做一件事——\
**Célia**: Don't trust Roseau, and don't come looking for me! Take this.

冰冷的物件落进阿黛拉手中。\
Something cold drops into Adèle's palm.

阿黛拉低下头。她认识项链上缀着的这枚钻石。\
She looks down, instantly recognizing the diamond now hanging from the necklace.

它的光彩无可比拟，它早已变成一个难以触及的传说。\
A brilliance like that could never be matched. It was a legend, one that should be far beyond her reach.

**阿黛拉**：这……这是法兰西之蓝？！\
**Adèle**: What? Is this the French Blue?

**阿黛拉**：不可能……它一定是……\
**Adèle**: But surely this isn't the real thing.

她所知的鉴别知识都告诉她，这是真的。

但这太过突然……谁会相信骤然落入手中的稀世珍宝？\
Yet everything she knows about her ancestral trade screams at her. It's inarguable. This jewel is authentic. But it's too sudden. Who would ever believe a treasure like that could just fall into their hands?

**西莉亚**：别考虑它的来历了，意象宝库绝不能被开启！\
**Célia**: Just take it! There's so much more I want to say, but just remember this: the Archive of Imagery must stay closed!

西莉亚用力握住她的手，帮她攥紧了拳头。\
Célia forces Adèle's palm closed around it.

**西莉亚**：你一定要烧掉它——\
**Célia**: Destroy the stone.

**阿黛拉**：——西莉亚！\
**Adèle**: Célia!

**贝丽尔**：——于此破暗归真。\
**Beryl**: —From darkness, light.

脑海中沉重的黑暗被扫去。阿黛拉左右打量着周围，感到太阳穴隐隐地抽痛。\
The heavy darkness in her mind lifts. Adèle looks around, her temples throbbing.

**阿黛拉**：呃……我是在……\
**Adèle**: Ugh. Where am I?

**贝丽尔**：请深呼吸，阿黛拉小姐。\
**Beryl**: Take a deep breath.

柔软的沙发，明亮的水晶灯，温和的香薰气味，手中的钻石。\
Soft couch, bright crystal lamp, gentle scent of incense, a diamond in her hand.

一切都和接受“净化仪式”前的情景别无二致。\
Everything exactly as it was before the cleansing ritual.

就连坐在对面沙发的贝丽尔，都保持着和阿黛拉闭上眼睛前相同的姿势。\
Even Beryl, sitting opposite, looks down at her from the very same pose she had been in before Adèle closed her eyes.

**阿黛拉**：我……是做了一场梦？\
**Adèle**: Was that ... Was I dreaming?

**贝丽尔**：不完全是。你沉入了潜意识的深处，找出了盘踞在那里的阴影。\
**Beryl**: Not quite. You plunged into the depths of your mind and uncovered the shadow lurking within.

**阿黛拉**：我的确看到了“热沃当的野兽”……在花神咖啡馆里……\
**Adèle**: I saw them—the Beasts of Gévaudan at the Café de Flore.

**阿黛拉**：所以净化仪式成功……\
**Adèle**: So, did we cast the beasts out of my mind, then?

她突然愣住了。\
She freezes.

手中的钻石。它本该是一颗烟晶。\
The diamond in her hand. It had been a smoky quartz, but now ...

**阿黛拉**：这不是我挑选的那颗水晶！是西莉亚在梦里给我的……\
**Adèle**: Damn, this isn't the crystal I chose! This is the one Célia gave me in the dream.

**阿黛拉**：……法兰西之蓝？\
**Adèle**: The French Blue ...

**阿黛拉**：为什么？为什么它会出现在这里？\
**Adèle**: But how is this possible?

**阿黛拉**：我还在那个噩梦中吗？我……没有醒来？\
**Adèle**: Am I still asleep? Is this part of the dream too?

她听到自己的声音在颤抖。\
She hears her own voice trembling.

她下意识地望向贝丽尔，在场的、仅剩的、或许能够帮助她的人……\
Instinctively, she looks toward Beryl—the only one left who might be able to help her.

贝丽尔的脸上浮现出淡淡的疑惑。\
But a glimmer of genuine confusion passes over Beryl's face.

**贝丽尔**：你在说什么，阿黛拉小姐？你并未挑选过水晶。\
**Beryl**: You must be confused. There was no other crystal.

**贝丽尔**：那颗钻石——你从一开始就握在手中。\
**Beryl**: That gem was already in your hand when you came in.

## AFF-08 法兰西之蓝 / The French Blue

**执夜人**：关于重塑之手，你当时了解多少？\
**Vigil Officer**: What did you know about Manus Vindictae at that time?

谈话室中，一叠照片被推到了阿黛拉的面前。\
A stack of photos slides across the table toward Adèle.

**灰调蓝**：一个觉得神秘学家高人类一等的密教组织，仅此而已。\
**Brume**: Only that it was some kind of secret society that believed arcanists are superior to ordinary humans.

**执夜人**：这个说法让他们听起来无害太多了。\
**Vigil Officer**: That's just the surface. They're responsible for so much more.

**执夜人**：挑动争端、吸纳信众、谋划战争……重塑之手不会放过任何制造混乱的机会。\
**Vigil Officer**: Fueling conflicts, inciting wars, manipulating minds ... If there's an opportunity to bring chaos, they take it.

**执夜人**：他们会将自己的力量渗透到每一个角落，你所在的时代也不例外。\
**Vigil Officer**: Their power extends to all corners of the world in almost every time period, including yours.

**执夜人**：黄金黎明会、无头、各种各样的蔷薇十字会后继者，甚至卡尔·荣格与西格蒙德·弗洛伊德都自觉或不自觉地与他们有所往来。\
**Vigil Officer**: The Hermetic Order of the Golden Dawn, Acéphale, and what remains of the Rosenkreuzer ... Even Carl Jung and Sigmund Freud were associated with them, whether knowingly or not.

**执夜人**：——你也一样，在巴黎时你应该也和重塑之手接触过。\
**Vigil Officer**: And it looks like you got caught up with them, too. You must've encountered them in Paris.

一面黑色的镜子被摆在了桌上，蒙了雾一样的镜面模糊地映出阿黛拉的面容。\
A black mirror is set down on the desk. Its foggy surface reflecting her face in a blur.

**执夜人**：你接下来的发言至关重要，我们会用这个确认你的话是否属实。\
**Vigil Officer**: Ms. Tavernier, what you say next is critical. From this moment on, everything you say will be monitored by a lie detector.

**执夜人**：灰调蓝小姐，你是否同意？\
**Vigil Officer**: Do you consent?

**灰调蓝**：……我同意。\
**Brume**: I do.

她打量镜中面目模糊的自己，下意识抚摸着另一只手的手背。\
She studies the image of herself while absentmindedly touching the back of her hand.

**灰调蓝**：其实我至今也认为，我应该没有招惹过什么重塑之手……\
**Brume**: You seem confident I've encountered them, but I really have no clue how I would have any connection with them.

**执夜人**：现在我们正要弄清这一切。\
**Vigil Officer**: Then you've got nothing to worry about.

**执夜人**：这是你画的当时出现在你手上的项链，没错吧？\
**Vigil Officer**: This is your drawing of the diamond necklace you saw in your dream, correct?

一张铅笔画替换掉了那叠照片，纸张上的笔触略显生涩。\
The photos vanish, replaced by a rough pencil sketch.

**灰调蓝**：没错。\
**Brume**: Yes.

他的指尖点向项链上缀着的那枚硕大的钻石。\
The fingertip points to the diamond pendant drawn on the paper.

**执夜人**：你声称上面的钻石是法兰西之蓝。\
**Vigil Officer**: You identified it as the French Blue, correct?

**灰调蓝**：是的。\
**Brume**: I did.

阿黛拉的回答没有半分迟疑。\
Adèle answers without hesitation.

**执夜人**：……据说是世界上最美丽的蓝钻石，法兰西之蓝。\
**Vigil Officer**: The French Blue—said to be the most beautiful blue diamond ever. It seems whoever it ends up with meets a horrific end.

每一个曾拥有过它的人最终都厄运缠身。

**执夜人**：法国经济崩溃，太阳王在晚年光辉尽失。然后是路易十五死于天花，最后洪水滔天……\
**Vigil Officer**: First, Louis XIV suffered defeats in his final years, his son was taken by smallpox, and France fell into financial ruin.

**执夜人**：至于像蒙特斯庞夫人、尼古拉·富凯、叶卡捷琳娜二世、乔治四世、托马斯·霍普那些人的故事，你应该比我更熟悉。\
**Vigil Officer**: Then Madame de Montespan, Nicolas Fouquet, Catherine the Great, George IV of England, and Thomas Hope ... I'm sure you're familiar, Ms. Tavernier.

**执夜人**：毕竟最初将它带回法国的，就是塔沃尼尔家的人。\
**Vigil Officer**: After all, if it weren't for your ancestors, the diamond would never have come to France in the first place.

**灰调蓝**：是啊，从小我听过无数关于这枚钻石的故事。\
**Brume**: That's true. I grew up hearing all those stories.

**执夜人**：那你应该清楚，你不可能拿到它。\
**Vigil Officer**: Then you must also know that it's impossible for you to be in its possession.

**灰调蓝**：……我明白你的意思，执夜人先生。\
**Brume**: Of course, sir.

**灰调蓝**：早在一个世纪前，法兰西之蓝就被重新切割，不复存在了。\
**Brume**: The French Blue was recut more than a hundred years ago.

**灰调蓝**：现在它留下的最大的那一块叫做希望钻石，最多只有曾经一半的风采。\
**Brume**: The biggest piece became the Hope Diamond. I doubt it retains even half its former glamor.

**灰调蓝**：但执夜人先生，那个时候我只能得出这个结论。\
**Brume**: But believe me, at that moment, it was the only conclusion I could reach.

她迎上对方满是怀疑的目光，镜中的影像并未发生任何谎言招致的扭曲。\
She faces the questioner from her side of the table. The mirror image holds still, untouched by any lie.

**灰调蓝**：那枚钻石只可能是法兰西之蓝。\
**Brume**: That diamond in my hand could only be the French Blue.

只有时钟的响声在水晶工房的会客室内回响。\
The ticking of the clock rises up over the silence of the room.

**阿黛拉**：嗯……\
**Adèle**: Hmm ...

**贝丽尔**：你已经看了三个小时了，阿黛拉小姐。\
**Beryl**: You have spent three hours studying that diamond, Adèle.

宝石鉴定专家保持着仰头的姿势，抛开手部翻弄钻石的动作，她已经与雕塑无异。\
The jewel expert still feels frozen in place, her head tilted, the diamond in her hand lying forlorn; she is more statue than woman.

**阿黛拉**：……真的。\
**Adèle**: It's real.

**贝丽尔**：怎么了？\
**Beryl**: Whatever do you mean?

**阿黛拉**：没有一点伪造痕迹，绝对不是仿品，重量大概有60……70……67克拉？\
**Adèle**: No sign of forgery. Weighs around 60 ... 70 ... Hmm, let's say 67 carats.

**阿黛拉**：外形也和家族图谱上记载的一样……\
**Adèle**: And it matches the picture in my family's archives.

**阿黛拉**：难道麦克林夫人的希望钻石是假货？真正的法兰西之蓝其实一直在它的发现者，塔沃尼尔家族内流传？\
**Adèle**: But how? Is the Hope Diamond a fake? Has the true French Blue always been in the hands of the Taverniers?

**阿黛拉**：——怎么可能有这种天方夜谭！\
**Adèle**: It's impossible. None of it makes any sense. None at all!

她放下那颗钻石，有些崩溃地向占卜师提出质疑。\
She firmly sets it down, her composure breaking as she questions the diviner.

**阿黛拉**：贝丽尔女士，您究竟想干什么？找来这么大一颗蓝钻对我恶作剧？这就是您说的净化仪式？\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, what is the meaning of this? Are you playing tricks on me? Am I seeing illusions because of that cleansing ritual?

**阿黛拉**：您如果坚持这是我的，那我可就拿走了！\
**Adèle**: If you insist I arrived with it, then I'm taking it back home!

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉小姐，水晶工房不出售钻石。\
**Beryl**: Adèle, I run a crystal parlor. I neither sell nor possess any such diamonds.

**贝丽尔**：我和你同样确信它不属于自己。\
**Beryl**: I am just as certain as you that I am not its owner.

**阿黛拉**：法兰西之蓝早就是历史了！它已经被切割成希望钻石，不再存于世！\
**Adèle**: This diamond—this French Blue—it doesn't exist. It ... It cannot exist!

**贝丽尔**：可你刚刚才确认过。它货真价实，此刻就在你的手中。\
**Beryl**: And yet here it is before you. It has passed every test.

话题回到了原点，宝石鉴定专家只能看着眼前切实的证据不知所措。\
The discussion circles back to where it began. Faced with the proof before her, the jewel expert is left speechless.

**阿黛拉**：我不明白……我梦见西莉亚把它给了我，然后它就真的到了我手上……\
**Adèle**: I don't understand. Célia gave this to me in my dream. How could it be here in reality? How does something from a dream become real?

但梦中的事物怎么会现实化……？而且连触感都这么真实？

**贝丽尔**：梦境往往更能示人以真。\
**Beryl**: Dreams often reveal truths greater than our senses allow us to see.

贝丽尔的面色依然平静，就像在谈论理所应当之事。\
Beryl remains like an island in a storm, still and unmoving as if the matter were self-evident.

**贝丽尔**：按照卡巴拉主义者的观点，物质世界只是完全的灵性在经过精神四世界时不断劣化的最终结果。\
**Beryl**: The material world is a result of contraction, shattering, and reconfiguration of pneuma on its descent through four primary spiritual worlds.

**贝丽尔**：任何物质都是其精神的劣化，其消亡也无法反馈到精神。\
**Beryl**: Everything we see is a mere manifestation of its true form. If destroyed in this world, it will yet persist in the spiritual world.

**贝丽尔**：只要精神仍存在，经由灵性的再次流溢而回归物质世界也并非不可能。\
**Beryl**: So long as the idea of it remains, it may return to the world of matter through an Emanation of pneuma.

**贝丽尔**：你握在手上的，或许正是再次物质化的精神。\
**Beryl**: Perhaps this diamond in your hand is the idea of it manifested for a second time.

占卜师的分享无懈可击。\
The diviner's reasoning is flawless.

但这番话只让年轻的司机更加糊涂了。\
But her words only leave Adèle more lost.

**阿黛拉**：不可能，梦就是梦，怎么会成真？\
**Adèle**: But how? All I did was see it in a dream.

她攥紧了拳头，尝试分辨这是否是另一个梦——但除了一些不必要的疼痛外，毫无结果。\
She clenches her fist, feeling the pricking of her nails, wondering if this too could be another dream, but all she feels is needless pain.

**阿黛拉**：如果它能成真，为什么只有钻石“物质化”了，我醒来却没有见到西莉亚？\
**Adèle**: So, if this dream made the diamond real, why only it? Why not my friend, Célia? She was there too!

**阿黛拉**：该死……真像是亲人去世前会做的那种晦气的梦！\
**Adèle**: Damn it all! It's like I'm trapped in a dream where you just know something awful is about to happen!

阿黛拉懊恼地拍了一下脑门，开始与梦中逻辑进行无谓的缠斗。\
She groans and taps her forehead, tangling herself in the logic.

最终，某种更为具体的担忧占了上风。\
In the end, a more tangible worry wins out.

**阿黛拉**：我得去找西莉亚……我有种不好的预感。\
**Adèle**: All this is giving me a terrible feeling. I need to find Célia.

**阿黛拉**：就算这枚古怪的钻石真的从梦里来到了现实中，在搞清楚它和西莉亚的关系前，我也不能就这么听从一个梦的指示烧毁它。\
**Adèle**: The things she said in that dream ... I have to speak to her before I do anything else.

她按住了幼龙刚刚对准钻石的脑袋，思考起好友可能的位置来。\
She presses down on her dragon's head before it can lunge at the diamond—a momentary respite from her growing concern.

**阿黛拉**：我应该去学校？不，西莉亚可能在外面调研。干脆，去她家里堵她……？\
**Adèle**: Would she be at the campus now? Or still in the field? Maybe I should wait for her at her place?

她望着店里的水晶，忽地意识到眼前正有一条捷径。\
She lets her eyes wander as she thinks, coming to a sudden realization that there's an answer hanging right in front of her.

**阿黛拉**：……对了，贝丽尔女士。您能占卜出西莉亚现在的位置吗？\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, you couldn't do a divination to tell me where Célia is now, could you? This diamond came from her, so you can trace it back to her, right?

就用她给我的钻石——

**贝丽尔**：很遗憾，阿黛拉小姐，虽然这枚钻石的质地非常纯粹，它提供的视野却并非如此。\
**Beryl**: I am afraid not. Though it may be a fine material for divination, it will not provide the vision you seek.

**贝丽尔**：要想找到你的朋友，最好是提供她曾长期持有的、寄有感情的物件。\
**Beryl**: If we are to find your friend, we require an item she has often used or something dear to her.

**阿黛拉**：那我立刻回家里一趟找找看！请您在这里等我……最多半个小时！\
**Adèle**: No problem! I just—I just need to pick something up from my place. Please, madame, would you wait here for me? I'll be back in 30 minutes at most!

我是开车来的，这不费多少时间——\
宝石鉴定专家差点就要夺门而出。

占卜师轻抚了一下裙摆，也随之站了起来。\
She bolts up from her seat and makes for the door. The diviner smooths her skirt and rises to follow.

**贝丽尔**：抱歉，阿黛拉小姐，我今天要关门了。\
**Beryl**: I am sorry, Adèle, but I must close the parlor now.

**阿黛拉**：呃——？\
**Adèle**: Ah ...

年轻人所有的急切都扑到了空气中，她尴尬地张开了嘴。\
Her urgency scatters into the air, leaving her with an open mouth searching for the words to fill it.

**阿黛拉**：那我——\
**Adèle**: Then I ...

**贝丽尔**：——但我并不介意在回去的路上，坐你的车绕上一小段路。\
**Beryl**: But I am willing to take a little detour on my way home, if I can be of help.

阿黛拉反应了半天，随即雀跃起来，热情地为占卜师拉开了大门。

对她来说，这无疑是一个好得多的方案。\
It takes Adèle a moment to process, then she beams, springing to her feet to hold the door open for the diviner. "An even better plan," she reasons.

**阿黛拉**：真不好意思，让您特意和我走一趟……\
**Adèle**: Thank you! I mean, sorry for taking up your evening. Ah, yes, how much do I owe you for the divination?

对了，您还没有告诉我占卜的费用呢？

**贝丽尔**：不必在意。我说过，那扇门为你而开。\
**Beryl**: Think nothing of it. As I said, the door was opened just for you.

**贝丽尔**：命运会把你的报酬在合适的时机支付给我。\
**Beryl**: Fate will see to the payment when the time is right.

**阿黛拉**：我没太弄明白……您这句话，是说您的老板是“命运”？\
**Adèle**: Wait. So, fate is the one paying you? Not the client? So, what, you work for fate?

**贝丽尔**：命运是我的老板……？\
**Beryl**: I work for fate?

司机惊讶地看见，自己随口的俏皮话竟真令贝丽尔思考了片刻。\
The driver is startled to see her offhand remark actually made Beryl pause to think.

**贝丽尔**：……嗯，你是第一位从这个角度阐释的人。\
**Beryl**: Hm. I have never heard anyone put it quite like that.

占卜师得体地微笑着，关上了水晶工房的门扉。\
She offers a polite smile as she locks the parlor entrance behind her.

**贝丽尔**：现在先让我们出发吧。为了你的朋友，还有我的“老板”。\
**Beryl**: Let's go. Let us see what your friend and my "employer" has in store for us.

## AFF-09 先觉者 / The Seer

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚？西莉亚？……果然不在。\
**Adèle**: Célia? It's Adèle! Are you home? *sigh* I thought not.

阿黛拉转向了隔壁的门，从口袋中摸出一把钥匙。\
Adèle turns to the next door, pulling a key from her pocket.

**阿黛拉**：只好先在我家找找了。\
**Adèle**: I-I live right across the hall. There must be something of hers in there.

公寓里的物件比起水晶工房还要多，只是它们没有水晶那般璀璨。\
Her little apartment is festooned with almost as many ornaments as the Parlor of Crystals—just with less glitter.

未经打磨的原石、展览会的宣传册、城市道路地图和下水道地图、修理机械的各种工具……\
Uncut stones, exhibition pamphlets, city maps, sewer maps, an assortment of repair tools ...

**阿黛拉**：嗯……让我找找，西莉亚有不少东西是放在我这儿的。\
**Adèle**: Hmm. Come on, Cici. You must've left something here.

在积木般整齐码放的小玩意之中，贝丽尔的目光锁定了一张被装裱好的照片。\
Among the stacks upon stacks of odds and ends, Beryl's eyes land on a framed photograph.

**贝丽尔**：这是你和西莉亚吗？看上去，你们关系很好。\
**Beryl**: Ah, this is her, is it not? The two of you seem very close.

黑白照片中的形象仍旧鲜活，一个小女孩兴致勃勃，另一个则紧张得快跑出镜头。\
In the black-and-white photo, the figures feel alive: one little girl gleeful, the other so nervous she's nearly out of frame.

**阿黛拉**：当然。老爸老妈忙于他们的大冒险，我俩差不多是一块儿长大。小时候我没少出现在她家的饭桌上……\
**Adèle**: Almost like sisters, actually. My parents were always traveling, so her family often took care of me—making dinners, that sort of thing.

阿黛拉一边逐个拉开抽屉，一边应答着贝丽尔的问题。\
Adèle answers Beryl's questions as she pulls open drawer after drawer.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚表面文静，但我知道她其实比谁都勇敢。\
**Adèle**: Looks like the quiet type, doesn't she? But she's hugely ambitious underneath it all.

**阿黛拉**：现在，比起我来，她的志向可远大得多了。\
**Adèle**: She's certainly set her sights higher than I ever have.

**阿黛拉**：怎么回事，想找时一个东西也找不到……用这个行不行？\
**Adèle**: Ah, come on now. When I don't need them, they're all over the place, but now ... Aha! Will this do?

阿黛拉从最下方的抽屉中抱出一摞信件。\
From the bottom drawer, she lifts out a stack of letters.

信件的邮票来自世界各处，信封却差异不大，上面都写着出奇工整的一行字。\
The stamps are from all over the world, though the envelopes themselves look the same, each bearing a single neat missive.

“女儿阿黛拉·塔沃尼尔收”\
"To our daughter, Adèle Tavernier."

贝丽尔拿起一封仔细端详。邮票的边角已经翘起，略微泛黄，与崭新的信封格格不入。\
Beryl picks one up for a closer look. The stamp's edges curl slightly, yellowed, mismatched against the fresh white envelope.

**阿黛拉**：贝丽尔女士？\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich?

阿黛拉忍不住催促。她不喜欢贝丽尔了然的神色，也不想在此时谈论信件的来历。\
Adèle looks to her with urgency but finds a worrisome response on Beryl's face, a knowing look, as if she can see right through her.

**贝丽尔**：这些信……好的，当然可以。\
**Beryl**: Letters ... Yes. They will do nicely.

她看了看阿黛拉脚边空着的抽屉。它在最常使用的书桌最不起眼的角落。\
Beryl glances at the empty drawer by Adèle's feet—the least conspicuous spot on a well-used desk.

**贝丽尔**：你的父母很久没有回到巴黎了。比起他们，你与西莉亚的确会更加熟悉。\
**Beryl**: It is little wonder Célia came to be like family to you, with your own so often away.

**阿黛拉**：没什么大不了的，他们在我人生中存在的时间本就不多。\
**Adèle**: Right. Not that I mind really. They've hardly been around since I was little.

**贝丽尔**：我明白了。我会尽力为你找到你重要的朋友。\
**Beryl**: I see. Shall we begin? Let us find this chosen family of yours.

她开始一封封翻阅信件，只像是日常生活的一部分。\
She begins leafing through the letters, treating it as part of some quiet routine.

直到双眼开始失焦，她的动作也不曾停下，只是摸索过、阅览过每一个字母，从中捕捉不可见的辉光。\
Her eyes lose focus, but her hands keep moving, tracing every letter, searching for the invisible gleam between the lines.

最终，光线落回了她的眼中。\
Finally, the light returns to her gaze.

**贝丽尔**：你的友人被这座城市吞没，坠入幽暗的洞穴。\
**Beryl**: I see her ... swallowed by the city ... sinking beneath the ground.

**贝丽尔**：大瘟疫的遗产，地下的另一个世界……与起舞的亡灵同在。\
**Beryl**: In a relic of the Great Plague ... In the world below ... Dancing with the dead.

**阿黛拉**：吞没……坠入……地下的另一个世界……\
**Adèle**: Swallowed? Beneath the ground?

出租车司机的眉头紧紧拧着，随后豁然开朗。\
She frowns, first with concern and then curiosity, until she suddenly brightens.

**阿黛拉**：噢，是地下墓穴！对了，她昨天说过要去研究死亡之舞！\
**Adèle**: Could it be the catacombs? Oh, of course! The Dance of Death she talked about. It's there!

**阿黛拉**：她现在一定在地下墓穴能观察到那些骷髅壁画的地方！该死，她以前就喜欢往这些地方跑……\
**Adèle**: She must've gone to see the mural! Ah, Célia, you never pick the easy places, do you?

**阿黛拉**：您的用词真是吓了我一跳，我还以为她是真去了另一个世界呢……\
**Adèle**: You had me worried, madame—the way you said it. It sounded almost like she'd passed on to the other side.

确认目标的年轻人没有踌躇，立刻奔向了公寓门。占卜师却叫住了她。\
Now certain of her goal, she jolts up and heads for the apartment door, but Beryl raises her hand.

**贝丽尔**：——我在她的命运中也见到了你，阿黛拉。\
**Beryl**: I see you there too, Adèle.

**阿黛拉**：嗯？\
**Adèle**: Hmm?

**贝丽尔**：如果你仍要前往，前方注定会有牺牲。\
**Beryl**: And the shadow of death follows close behind.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

这并非提醒，而是陈述。\
The words don't feel like a warning. They're a statement.

她隐约感觉到，贝丽尔似乎的确能看见一些遥远的事物。\
The diviner looks on past the confines of her room as if seeing something far in the distance.

但她只是笑了笑。\
Yet Adèle cannot help but laugh.

**阿黛拉**：从小到大，这种话我听得太多了。\
**Adèle**: Hah. It's hardly the first time I've been warned about a shadow of death, is it?

我可不能为了一句缥缈的预示就放弃西莉亚，放弃我想弄明白的事。\
There's no way I'm leaving Célia there by herself after what you've said.

**阿黛拉**：我尊重命运的方式，就是听从自己的判断。\
**Adèle**: Your vision may be right, but still, I'll make my own decision.

贝丽尔仍然平静地看着她，那透明的目光让阿黛拉有一种古怪的感觉。\
Beryl watches her from behind her calm, translucent eyes.

似乎贝丽尔的目光并不在当下，而是更加遥远的某处。\
Eyes that never fix on the moment, always beyond, always.

片刻后，她勾起嘴角，声音一如平日的优雅。\
Moments pass, and then she speaks.

**贝丽尔**：——是了，你是会如此回答。\
**Beryl**: I expected no less.

两人回到了公寓楼下，司机逐渐放缓走向爱车的脚步，似乎这能让时间变慢。\
The two of them return to the street below. But as she walks, Adèle slows her steps toward the car, as if moving slower would stretch time itself.

虽然得到了好友的位置，但她心中的疑惑并未减少分毫。\
Though she may have some idea where her friend is, she's only grown more confused.

**阿黛拉**：……贝丽尔女士，对占卜师而言，梦境是否可控？\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, if you'll pardon my asking, can dreams be controlled?

**贝丽尔**：物质可以是劣化的精神，精神也可以只是较高的物质。\
**Beryl**: Think first of matter as the lower form of spirit and spirit as the refined form of matter.

**贝丽尔**：而有形的物质终究是可以交互与干涉的，这个回答如何？\
**Beryl**: When we dream, we tread in the spiritual world above, and thus, we may shape it, just as we do our material world.

**阿黛拉**：那就是说，控制梦境，对您这样的占卜师并不算难事。\
**Adèle**: Then is it possible for a diviner such as yourself to decide what I dream?

直逼核心的发问。\
A question aimed at the heart of it.

贝丽尔偏过头，神色如常。这句话远不够锋利，无法划破她的笑容。\
Beryl tilts her head; the words aren't sharp enough to pierce her.

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉小姐，我不曾操纵过你的梦境。\
**Beryl**: I did not interfere with your dream, Adèle.

如果你不愿相信，我们本也不必进行这番占卜。\
But if your concerns are too great, you do not need to accept my readings.

**阿黛拉**：不。我没有不相信您的意思。\
**Adèle**: No, I didn't mean it like that.

**阿黛拉**：只是梦境成真这件事实在难以置信，而您又是对此最为了解的人。\
**Adèle**: I'm still trying to make sense of all this—a dream turned into reality.

恰好，我最近只接触过两个占卜师，其中一个已经死了……\
And I've met two diviners in the past couple of days, and one of them is dead. I felt I had to ask ...

**贝丽尔**：没关系。换做是我，也会有类似的怀疑。\
**Beryl**: I understand. I would feel much the same were I in your position.

**阿黛拉**：感谢您的理解……请上车吧。您住在哪里？我一定为您规划一条最快的线路——\
**Adèle**: Thank you. Uh, I should take you home, madame. I know a shortcut.

她打开副驾驶的车门，尽到优秀司机的礼仪，却发现已有人占了座位。\
She opens the passenger door—a professional habit—only to realize the seat is occupied.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安？\
**Adèle**: Félicienne?

**费利西安**：真是让我好等！你想怎么辩解？阿黛拉？\
**Félicienne**: You're just getting better and better, aren't you? Leaving me waiting once again. What's your excuse this time, hm?

另一位失踪人士的及时出现令阿黛拉松了一口气。\
Despite it all, Adèle feels genuine relief to see her once-missing employer.

**阿黛拉**：我的大小姐，现在到处都在闹罢工。你这样满身贵族气质，可不能到处乱走了。\
**Adèle**: I ... Where have you been? There are strikes going on all over the place, Félicienne. You've got to stop sneaking off and roaming around by yourself!

**阿黛拉**：不对，你的项链从哪儿来的？\
**Adèle**: H-Hold on. Where did you get that necklace?

**费利西安**：别岔开话题。你把我忘到现在的理由呢？不说些什么维护你的忠诚和名誉么？\
**Félicienne**: Excuse me? Who are you to lecture me? You're the one who left me alone in this car!

大小姐轻巧地拿起一枚马卡龙，舌头则编织着苛刻的单词。\
The refined woman picks up a macaron with gingerly grace, but she doesn't take a bite, her lips preoccupied instead with launching her signature razor-sharp critiques.

**阿黛拉**：那是西莉亚给我的项链！怎么会在你这里？！\
**Adèle**: That necklace! Célia gave it to me! How did you get it?

阿黛拉赶紧伸手摸入口袋，却发现里面空空如也。\
Adèle reaches into her pocket, but it's empty.

费利西安放下了手中的甜点，举起了胸前的项链。\
Félicienne puts down the sweet and lifts the necklace at her chest.

**费利西安**：哈？西莉亚给你的？难道你不是法国人？还是你真的蠢到无以复加？\
**Félicienne**: Célia gave it to you, did she? *scoff* Are you mad? This is a priceless national treasure, my dear, not a friendship bracelet.

**费利西安**：我再向你说明一次，给我好好刻在你的脑子里。\
**Félicienne**: I say this to you for the last time, and I shall not repeat it again.

**费利西安**：这是我的东西！我亲自找回的宝物，是我一生中冒险的最高收获。\
**Félicienne**: This is mine and always has been mine, the finest of all treasures I collected on my many adventures.

**费利西安**：没有被未来伤害的，巴隆家的宿愿，那美好时代的遗物。\
**Félicienne**: It's a relic of a more beautiful era, shattered and distorted, along with the vision of the Baron family—my family.

**费利西安**：这是我的宝石！明白么？我的，我的，我的！\
**Félicienne**: This jewel is mine, do you hear? Mine, mine, mine!

**费利西安**：高傲的小姐将宝石一把攥住。她注视着阿黛拉，愤怒的语气却没有配上愤怒的视线。\
**Félicienne**: She clenches the diamond in her fist, staring daggers at Adèle. Though the look in her eyes doesn't feel like rage.

就像是发现了一件不堪用，甚至没有资格承受怒火的工具。\
She finds a pocket between disdain and malice, like finding a rat mid-feast in her pantry.

**阿黛拉**：你说……什么？\
**Adèle**: What are you talking about?

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉小姐，你还好吗？\
**Beryl**: Is something wrong, Adèle?

贝丽尔从身后扶住了摇摇欲坠的司机。\
Beryl steadies the staggering driver from behind.

**贝丽尔**：你还在担心那位“费利西安”吗？\
**Beryl**: You are still worrying about Félicienne, is that so?

**阿黛拉**：什么担心？她就在这儿！你到底怎么了，费利西安？\
**Adèle**: Well, not anymore! Turns out she's been waiting for me in the car! And Félicienne, what do you mean it's yours?

**阿黛拉**：……费利西安？\
**Adèle**: Félicienne?

贝丽尔顺着她手指的方向望向副驾驶席。\
Beryl follows Adèle's pointing finger toward the passenger seat.

——她的声音停顿了片刻。\
Her voice catches.

**贝丽尔**：可是……阿黛拉小姐，你看。\
**Beryl**: But, my dear.

**贝丽尔**：副驾驶席上并没有任何人。\
**Beryl**: There is no one in your car.

**贝丽尔**：你打开车门之后，就一直在和空气争吵。\
**Beryl**: You have been arguing with an empty seat since you opened the door.

半晌，阿黛拉才取回自己的声音。\
Adèle blanks, mind and tongue stammering at the colliding dissonance of what was and is.

**阿黛拉**：………………咦？\
**Adèle**: How?

## AFF-10 城市的癔症 / Paris in Hysteria

年轻的出租车司机深吸一口气，勉强挤出一个笑容。\
Adèle forces a broken smile to her face.

**阿黛拉**：布翁尼女士，您的玩笑确实不错。但很抱歉，我得先找到费利西安那家伙！\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, as much as I appreciate your humor, now really isn't the time for it. Where did she go?

**阿黛拉**：再怎么任性，她都不该拿走朋友送我的项链——\
**Adèle**: I'm quite used to her attitude, but stealing that necklace crosses a line!

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉小姐。\
**Beryl**: Adèle.

占卜师始终保持着得体的社交距离，直至此刻，这层界限被主动打破了。\
The distance in her voice and manners disappears—the diviner becomes mortal. Her voice laced with genuine concern.

**贝丽尔**：我从未见过你口中的那位“费利西安”。\
**Beryl**: Félicienne was never here.

**贝丽尔**：你的项链也许是落在了哪儿，我可以帮你占卜它的下落。\
**Beryl**: Perhaps it fell out of your pocket. Allow me to aid you in its return. I believe it is best you not act alone in your current state.

以你现在的状态，不适合独自行动。

**阿黛拉**：哈……您当然没见过她，因为她迟到了，没有和我一起来店里！\
**Adèle**: Ah, I've got it now. She didn't come to your parlor today, so she must've gone somewhere else, and she's been waiting in the car ever since. No wonder she got angry and stormed off.

所以她刚刚才会在车上等我，然后突然发火跑掉……

她烦躁地转着袖口的纽扣，只想迅速从这场闹剧中脱身。\
She fidgets with her sleeve button, desperate to escape this farce.

**阿黛拉**：好了，已经耽误很多时间了！如果您实在担心我因为占卜出了问题，改天，也许明天，我再来拜访您——\
**Adèle**: Ay ay ay, that's enough! What a day! I think it's better we speak again another time, Madame Bouanich. Would tomorrow work? I—

**贝丽尔**：你们第一次见面是什么时候？\
**Beryl**: When did you first meet this Félicienne?

**阿黛拉**：我说——\
**Adèle**: Oh, my goodness!

贝丽尔比她更快地伸出手，关上了那扇车门。\
Beryl moves faster, forcing the car door closed.

**阿黛拉**：……您究竟是怎么了？\
**Adèle**: Honestly, what on earth is happening today?

**阿黛拉**：如果您非要证据……真是疯了，我还有必须证明自己的雇主是个活人的一天！\
**Adèle**: You want proof? I'll give you proof. Hah, madness! Never thought I'd have to actually convince someone that I work for that terrible woman.

她不耐烦地摸索了一阵，在口袋里找到了那个钱夹。\
She rummages impatiently through her pockets until she finds her wallet.

**阿黛拉**：……我还记得那天下雨，费利西安小姐上车的时候抱怨泥水溅湿了鞋，让我立刻开到香榭丽舍大街。\
**Adèle**: It was raining. She started complaining about the mud on her shoes the moment she stepped into the car, then insisted we head straight to the Champs-Élysées.

**阿黛拉**：她出手阔绰，每次我都得专门花时间清点票子和硬币，第一天，她还给了我几枚金法郎做纪念，就在这儿……\
**Adèle**: You know, wealthy young ladies like her are always generous with payment. I often have to take time out of my evenings just to count all her tips. That very first day, she even gave me some gold francs as keepsakes. I've got them in here.

**阿黛拉**：……？！\
**Adèle**: ...?!

阿黛拉脸上写满了不可置信。她将钱夹翻来覆去，倒了个个儿，拉开又合上。\
Her face twists in disbelief as she flips it open and closes it again.

遗憾的是，没有一枚硬币或一张票子从里头掉出来。\
Not a single coin or bill.

**阿黛拉**：不对，肯定是收到了别的地方。\
**Adèle**: Oh. Hah. I must've put them somewhere else.

**阿黛拉**：您让我回车上，我还有其他证据！\
**Adèle**: Give me a moment to check the car. I've got other proof, too!

**阿黛拉**：那几盒马卡龙——有一盒她还没吃完！还有掉落的头发，小物件，随便什么……\
**Adèle**: Ah. The macaron boxes. There's a full one somewhere! And her hair, little bits and pieces she left in the car.

有一瞬间，她真的承认了那个荒诞的念头。\
For a brief moment, she accepts the absurd conclusion.

费利西安从不存在。\
Félicienne never existed.

**阿黛拉**：那天……我们……\
**Adèle**: I remember ... that day ...

本该熟悉的画面愈发模糊，她与这些记忆之间就像隔着一扇遍布划痕的车窗。\
Her every recollection of Félicienne takes on a strange blur, as if she were viewing them from behind a fogged-up windshield.

**阿黛拉**：我只是……我太累了。您稍等一会儿！马上就——\
**Adèle**: I ... I must be tired. It's been a long day. It'll come to me soon.

贝丽尔轻轻拍了拍她的手背，示意她先放下空荡的钱夹。\
Beryl strokes the back of her hand, gently urging her to let go of the empty wallet.

**贝丽尔**：你想不起任何细节。\
**Beryl**: But there is nothing to remember.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

**阿黛拉**：或许是我的问题……预言、占卜、那个梦和项链，光这些就够叫人头疼……\
**Adèle**: Something's wrong with me. Prophecies, dreams, the necklace—it's all playing havoc with my mind.

**阿黛拉**：一定是我记混了，您看！真对不起，硬币肯定就在车里……\
**Adèle**: I need to clear my head! Just bear with me. Those coins have to be in here somewhere.

**贝丽尔**：没关系，阿黛拉小姐。这并不是你的问题，而是这个时代共有的疾病。\
**Beryl**: Do not worry, Adèle. It is not only you who is confused in this era.

**贝丽尔**：别忽视我们周围的人群。来吧，瞧瞧他们。\
**Beryl**: Look at the people around you.

**阿黛拉**：他们……\
**Adèle**: People?

周遭的喧闹忽然撞进耳中，她忍不住揉了揉脑袋，以此抵抗涌起的眩晕。\
Sound crashes back in. She rubs her temples, fighting the dizziness.

**罢工群众Ⅰ**：不容忍暴政！不妥协压迫！\
**Protester I**: No more atrocities! No more oppression!

**罢工群众Ⅱ**：自由！平等！\
**Protester II**: Liberty! Equality!

**罢工群众Ⅲ**：保卫巴黎！保卫共和！\
**Protester III**: Stand with Paris! Stand with the people!

**罢工群众Ⅳ**：公社万岁！法兰西万岁！\
**Protester IV**: For the commune! For France!

**贝丽尔**：您好，先生。\
**Beryl**: Excuse me, sir.

贝丽尔叫住了离车最近的工人，他正挥舞着鲜红的弗里吉亚帽。\
Beryl calls out to the nearest worker—a man waving a bright red Phrygian cap.

**贝丽尔**：你们这是打算做什么？\
**Beryl**: Where are you going?

**罢工群众Ⅰ**：我们要跟上国民自卫军，和那些卖国的政府军斗争到底！\
**Protester I**: We're following the Garde Nationale to fight the royalists!

**罢工群众Ⅱ**：而我，要去当铺把自己的床垫拿回来！\
**Protester II**: Yes, and then I'm going straight to the pawnbroker to get my mattress back!

**罢工群众Ⅰ**：说得好，但如果我们能保住巴黎，那么以后就会有更好的日子！\
**Protester I**: You do that, sister! Brighter days lie just ahead if we fight as one for our city!

**贝丽尔**：这并不是一件容易的事。但你们今日吹响的号角声，也许会远比你们以为的要更加嘹亮悠长。你们会如愿以偿。\
**Beryl**: It is no easy feat. But your voices today may echo further than you know. You will triumph in time.

**罢工群众Ⅰ**：多谢您的祝福，女士！我们都相信巴黎公社的影响绝不是一时的！\
**Protester I**: Thank you, madame! For the Commune de Paris!

工人转身离去，立刻汇入了街头的人潮之中。\
The man turns and disappears into the crowd.

**阿黛拉**：大家的生活都不算容易。看起来他们是为了改变现状开始游行了。\
**Adèle**: Well, everyone's fighting to survive these days. Looks like another protest.

**阿黛拉**：等等，巴黎……公社？\
**Adèle**: But did he just say "Commune de Paris"?

**贝丽尔**：在他们眼中，现在正是那个炎热的1871年夏天。\
**Beryl**: He did. In their minds, this is the burning summer of 1871.

又是那样近乎透明的目光。人们的所思所想就像落在水晶上的光线，贝丽尔阅读它，却并不打算为它所改变。\
Those almost-transparent eyes again. People's thoughts pass through her like light through crystal. Beryl reads them but never bends to them.

**贝丽尔**：无数繁杂的思绪正在这座城中汇聚，这注定是一段不平静的时日。\
**Beryl**: Unconscious thoughts, countless in number, are converging upon this city. This is a volatile time indeed.

**贝丽尔**：有人见到亲人与好友消失，有人目睹了不应存在之幽灵，有人自称追随着入土的皇帝，有人被一百年前流行的谣言生物袭击。\
**Beryl**: Some worry for their missing family and friends, some are terrified by ghosts and spirits, some obsess over a long-dead emperor, and others are shaken by the phantom attacks of a beast of legend.

**贝丽尔**：当整座城都被恐慌笼罩，在混乱之中，现实便会开始动摇。\
**Beryl**: The edifice of reality is shaking. Chaos has been invited into its foundation.

**贝丽尔**：这就是流言，或者癔症、一种城市的症候……也是“热沃当的野兽”的真相。\
**Beryl**: Whispered fears, murmured madnesses ... A sickness is sweeping the city, and the Beasts of Gévaudan have multiplied.

她的视线追随着缓缓向前的人群。\
She watches the flow of the moving crowd.

**贝丽尔**：而这并非某一个群体，或者哪一个特定存在的过错。\
**Beryl**: Those who invited this chaos did not comprehend that the flaws of reality are not the fault of a single person nor group of people. This is not the way to mend Paris.

**贝丽尔**：人的个性即是与时代和群体的差异，一个人无法成为他人，单一的集体和无数的个体也无法等价，但如今这个铁则被打破，成为了一场混乱的癔症。\
**Beryl**: Everyone—everything—has an identity, whether it be individual or collective. To attempt to unify them all so recklessly will not create order, but chaos.

**贝丽尔**：这癔症使人成为野兽。\
**Beryl**: Chaos is what turned those people into beasts.

**阿黛拉**：您想说“热沃当的野兽”们都是活人？是巴黎的市民？\
**Adèle**: You mean the sightings of the Beasts of Gévaudan were all people? That the citizens of Paris have been turning into monsters?

**阿黛拉**：是他们害了占卜沙龙里的女士，诅咒了我，还带走了西莉亚，让刚才的人产生幻觉……？\
**Adèle**: Then are they the ones who killed Madame Raymond? Who cursed me, took Célia, and trapped all these protesters in this delusion?

**阿黛拉**：还有费利西安，可能也……\
**Adèle**: And Félicienne, too?

她自幼时起就没有相信过童话与传说，现在也不可能承认类似的说辞。\
The things she describes are fairy tales, myths, urban legends meant to scare children. They aren't real. They aren't meant to be believed.

年轻人咬了咬牙，她终于再也无法忽视心中的疑惑。\
She grits her teeth, unable to reconcile her doubts with her experiences.

**阿黛拉**：——说实话，布翁尼女士，我很难再相信您的这些话！\
**Adèle**: Truthfully, madame, I'm having a hard time believing you or even my own eyes.

**阿黛拉**：在我看来，所有真正的异常都是我见到您之后开始的。\
**Adèle**: Everything turned completely mad the moment I entered your parlor.

**阿黛拉**：占卜沙龙里我也听过“野兽”的论调，可我见到您以后，才在您的水晶疗愈中做了那个奇怪的梦！\
**Adèle**: The Beasts of Gévaudan were nothing more than a rumor before I met you, but in your parlor—in that dream—there they were, attacking me!

**阿黛拉**：我不愿怀疑您，可也是您先提出质疑，说费利西安是我的幻觉。即使先不提那些——您要怎么解释如此的巧合？\
**Adèle**: And now you claim that Félicienne isn't real, that I just made her up! What are you trying to do here?

**贝丽尔**：这是你自己的命运。我无权干涉它，也无从解释它。\
**Beryl**: I play no part in your fate, Adèle. It is what brought you here. I am only a witness.

**阿黛拉**：可以。那您能占卜出我项链的下落吗？它切切实实地从我身上消失了——您看到了，离开工房的时候它还在！费利西安把它拿走了！\
**Adèle**: "Only a witness"! You've got a clever answer for everything, don't you? Then tell me where the necklace is. You must've seen Félicienne take it, right?

**阿黛拉**：您打算怎么解释这一切？\
**Adèle**: So? Did you "witness" that, madame?

**贝丽尔**：如你所说，这条项链也是你在梦中取得的。\
**Beryl**: You received that necklace in a dream.

**贝丽尔**：它忽然出现在你手中，现在又忽然消失，也许这才符合现实的规律。\
**Beryl**: It is only natural that it would vanish into another.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

她无从辩驳。\
Her reasoning is as solid as it is absurd.

**贝丽尔**：精神的世界可以干涉物质的世界，这条项链已经为你证明了。\
**Beryl**: That necklace proves the truth of my words. The spirit world is as real to us as the physical world.

**贝丽尔**：我也能为你占卜“费利西安”的命运，如果她的确是一个真实存在的人，如果你愿意相信。\
**Beryl**: I will happily read Félicienne's fate. That is, if you still believe she is real.

**阿黛拉**：……我自己能处理好！\
**Adèle**: I don't need you to read anything!

**阿黛拉**：我想我现在最需要的是找个地方独自静一静，离开这些乱七八糟的、荒谬的事，把我的脑子整理清楚！\
**Adèle**: I-I need space! To get away from all this madness and think for myself!

谈话间，贝丽尔已经离开了那扇车门，阿黛拉趁机猛地探身，抓住了把手。\
Beryl steps back from the car door, unconsciously giving way, allowing Adèle to lunge forward and seize the handle.

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉……\
**Beryl**: Adèle ...

耳鸣与眩晕又出现了。街头的喧哗轰然而来。\
The ringing in her ears returns, and the street noise rushes in all at once.

但她已经决心丢开这一切。只要回到车里，踩下油门……\
But she's made up her mind. If she can just get in, start the engine ...

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉！后面！\
**Beryl**: Adèle! Behind you!

**阿黛拉**：什……\
**Adèle**: Wha—

潮湿而腥涩的气息从她颈边吹来。\
A damp, metallic breath brushes her neck.

**热沃当的野兽**：——！\
**Beast of Gévaudan**: ...!

**贝丽尔**：往后退。\
**Beryl**: Stay close to me.

阿黛拉的反应足够快，她顺着贝丽尔拉扯自己的力道后撤，同时抬起了胳膊。\
Adèle reacts instantly, pulling back with Beryl's tug, raising her arm.

一团火光顺着她的指尖窜出去，幼龙拍动翅膀，赶在那头野兽消散之前点燃了它的皮毛。\
A burst of flame shoots from her fingertips. Her little dragon beats its wings, setting the beast ablaze before it can fade away.

**阿黛拉**：您的手！让我瞧瞧——是被抓伤了吗？\
**Adèle**: Your hand! Did it get you?

**阿黛拉**：真见鬼，这可是大白天的街头……它们从哪儿来的？！\
**Adèle**: Bloody hell! This is no dream! How did they get here?

不远处的队伍里也间歇传来几声惊呼。\
Shouts rise from the nearby crowd.

阿黛拉喘着气，警惕地观察了一圈。在确定没有第二只野兽会扑过来后，她终于松下肩膀。\
Adèle gasps, scanning the street. Seeing no second monster, she finally exhales.

**阿黛拉**：这是您刚才说的……？\
**Adèle**: Is that what you meant earlier?

占卜师很轻地点了点头，血从她更加苍白的皮肤上淌落。\
The diviner nods faintly, blood running down her now-paler skin.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

如果她们的反应慢一些，流血的就不仅是贝丽尔的手臂。\
If they'd been a moment slower, Beryl's arm wouldn't be the only one bleeding. Adèle doesn't believe she's worth that kind of sacrifice.

她自认自己没有如此大的价值，值得谁用这种代价换取信任。

**阿黛拉**：……我承认，您说的有些话是真的。比如“热沃当的野兽”。\
**Adèle**: Maybe you do have a point. At least about the Beasts of Gévaudan.

她拉开车门翻找了一阵，向贝丽尔递出一块手帕。\
She opens the car door, searching inside with purpose, before handing Beryl a handkerchief.

**阿黛拉**：您受伤了。虽然看起来不严重，但我不能就这样放着您不管。\
**Adèle**: Here, take this. It should help with the bleeding. *sigh* I can't just leave you like this. You'll have to come with me, madame.

**阿黛拉**：抱歉，我不能送您回去了——我需要加快脚步找回那两位失踪的朋友，否则她们很可能有生命危险。\
**Adèle**: But I'm afraid I can't take you home. I must find my friends before anything happens to them.

**阿黛拉**：既然您说的至少有一部分是真的，那我就更不能放着这些怪异不管了。\
**Adèle**: I can't just leave them wandering the city while these monsters prowl the streets.

**贝丽尔**：这样吗？\
**Beryl**: Is that so?

占卜师稍显惊讶，但还是接过了这份好意。\
She looks surprised but accepts the gesture.

**贝丽尔**：你还是要去地下墓穴，即使预言告诉你，前路会有牺牲。\
**Beryl**: I foresaw death in the catacombs, and yet still you aim to go there.

**阿黛拉**：当然。\
**Adèle**: Of course.

**阿黛拉**：不论这是假的还是真的，巴黎是将天翻还是地覆，我要做的事都不会改变。\
**Adèle**: I've made up my mind. I need to find Célia. I don't care what it costs.

她顿了顿。贝丽尔流血的手臂仍牢牢抓着她的视线。\
Adèle pauses, her vision locked on Beryl's bleeding arm.

**阿黛拉**：说实话，我还是不能彻底地相信您……但我也能感受到，您对我并无恶意。\
**Adèle**: I'm still not sure if I can trust you. But for now, at least, I don't believe you want to do me any harm.

**阿黛拉**：可以告诉我，您一直引导我的目的是什么吗？\
**Adèle**: But I need to know—why are you helping me?

**阿黛拉**：难道只是为了卖我一个人情……？\
**Adèle**: You didn't even ask for payment. What do you want from me?

贝丽尔弯起眼睛，就像听见一个孩子执着地讨要一粒灰尘。\
Beryl's translucent eyes barely restrain a visible roll. It's affectionate—almost motherly.

这疑问无伤大雅，只是天真而可笑。\
Her question is harmless, if utterly naive.

**贝丽尔**：原来你只是想问我这件事？\
**Beryl**: So this is what you choose to ask.

**阿黛拉**：……当然，这是我最想知道的事。\
**Adèle**: Why wouldn't it be?

**贝丽尔**：关于死亡的预言，巴黎的癔症，这些对你来说都不重要，你只是想询问一个关于“我”的问题？\
**Beryl**: Of all there is to question—your future, this chaos—you choose to ask about me.

**阿黛拉**：我不明白，女士……难道这很奇怪吗？\
**Adèle**: What's so strange about that?

她目睹的光彩转瞬即逝，那副挑不出错处的温柔笑容又回到了贝丽尔脸上。\
Her flawless, gentle smile returns, from matron back to diviner.

**贝丽尔**：不，你的疑惑才是正当的。\
**Beryl**: Nothing. Your curiosity is only natural.

**贝丽尔**：我在工房时并没有欺骗你，阿黛拉。你的身上有一个诅咒，一个命运攀附的阴影。\
**Beryl**: I have never once lied to you, Adèle. You are cursed—haunted by a shadow. A shadow of fate.

**贝丽尔**：而我想知道它会向何处发展。\
**Beryl**: I only wish to see what will become of you.

**阿黛拉**：……可您不是已经做出了关于我结局的预言吗？对您来说，这又有什么可看的呢？\
**Adèle**: But don't you already know? I'll die in the catacombs. What else is there to see?

**贝丽尔**：你也已经知道了这个预言，可你仍要前往地下墓穴。\
**Beryl**: You know this yourself. Yet here we are.

**贝丽尔**：我与你的理由并没有分别。或者说，至少在此刻，我们的利益仍是一致的。\
**Beryl**: We have a common interest in that fate, you and I. Let us leave it at that.

**贝丽尔**：去地下墓穴寻找你的答案吧，阿黛拉。你在那里还会需要我的。\
**Beryl**: Go to the catacombs, Adèle, with me by your side. You will need my help once you enter.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

这是一个迟到许久的同行要求。\
It's a long-delayed request to travel together.

她难以从贝丽尔的神情中看出更多东西。但她也没有时间了。\
Adèle can't read much from Beryl's expression, but there's no time left.

稍作思考后，她再次打开车门。\
After a brief thought, she opens the car door again.

**阿黛拉**：上车吧。您手上有伤，不太方便。我帮您打开门。\
**Adèle**: Please, get in. Careful. Let me open the door.

**贝丽尔**：多谢。\
**Beryl**: Thank you.

标致201穿过人群，拐进一条更空旷的小路，驶向它既定的终点。\
The Peugeot 201 slips through the crowd, turning down a quiet street toward its destined end.

## AFF-11 岔路口 / Confluence

几层楼高的砖石与泥土足以隔断阳光下的喧嚣，漆黑的地下通道中，脚步声踏出单调的回音。\
Bricks and soil several stories high shut out the sunlight above. Footsteps making dull echoes through the underground passage.

**阿黛拉**：好了，到这里应该差不多了。\
**Adèle**: This should be about where the restricted area begins.

**阿黛拉**：虽然城里的警察朋友们现在大概也顾不上看管这里。\
**Adèle**: Though I doubt the police have the luxury of worrying about our trespassing.

灯罩内侧的刻印发出微光，柔和的光亮均匀地照亮了四周。\
The carvings inside the lampshade emit a steady faint light, bathing the tunnel in a soft glow.

粗粝石砖铺就的幽深甬道中，不知已沉寂多少年的灰尘飞舞在空中，欢迎着罕见的访客。\
Dust long settled on the rough stone floor rises into the air, as if the space were rushing up to meet its rare visitors.

**阿黛拉**：据说这些通道最初是中世纪时为了开采石头挖的，算起来已经有几个世纪的年头了。\
**Adèle**: I've always wanted to explore the catacombs; it's almost eerie to think they've been lying beneath our feet for centuries.

**阿黛拉**：18世纪的时候，城里墓地人满为患，几百万位先生小姐们就被搬迁到了这里。\
**Adèle**: And it only got spookier once they started stuffing the dead away down here. A vast labyrinth lined with skeletons ...

**阿黛拉**：后来又开挖了地下排水系统和地铁，加上那些据说在大革命时期或是战争期间挖的秘密通道——\
**Adèle**: But, despite the spookiness, I still feel it has a special charm—secret passages used by revolutionaries and soldiers, surviving in their own way against the march of progress.

**贝丽尔**：一座历史悠久的地下迷宫。\
**Beryl**: The catacombs have a rich history indeed. Yet only a small portion of it remains open to the public.

对外开放的只是一小部分，它的绝大多数身躯都还藏在黑暗中。

**贝丽尔**：这位老朋友就睡在人们的枕边，但没有谁看清过它的全貌。\
**Beryl**: It is a place dear to the spirit of the city, yet one that is hidden away.

同行者补上了阿黛拉还未说完的话语，语调一如既往的平静如水。\
Her companion finishes the sentence Adèle hadn't.

**阿黛拉**：瞧我……忘了您不是那些外地来的客人，不用我介绍。\
**Adèle**: Oh, pardon. I'm treating you like one of my clients. I'm sure you don't need a guide to tell you these things.

**阿黛拉**：放在平常我可以带您慢慢逛，但这次没时间耽搁了。\
**Adèle**: Besides, we aren't here for sightseeing.

**阿黛拉**：我必须尽快找到西莉亚，确保她一切平安。\
**Adèle**: I need to find Célia and get her to safety as soon as possible.

阿黛拉望向通道前方的岔路口，眉头紧锁。\
They come to a confluence of paths. Adèle's heart tugs as her purpose meets yet another frustration.

**阿黛拉**：这些通道加起来足足有差不多三百公里长，我们不能在这里大海捞针。\
**Adèle**: But these tunnels stretch out almost three hundred kilometers in all directions. We can't go looking for a needle in a haystack.

**阿黛拉**：既然占卜告诉了您西莉亚的所在，想必您一定能再做一次，对吗？\
**Adèle**: Madame, your divination revealed Célia's whereabouts before. Could you perhaps try it again?

**贝丽尔**：太多人的命运在这里交汇，要捕捉其中的一滴水珠比平时要困难得多。\
**Beryl**: The fates of many commingle here. To trace her would be to catch a single stream from a flowing river.

**贝丽尔**：但你来了。你们的命运紧密相关，窥探你的命运，也能辨识她的去向。\
**Beryl**: But it seems her stream is deeply entangled with your own. Perhaps, by observing yours, I may discern her presence.

**贝丽尔**：属于你的水流很特别。你背负着塔沃尼尔的诅咒，而诅咒有时候是一种天赋，能令人踏上与旁人不同的道路。\
**Beryl**: Your stream is quite unique. The familial curse you bear—it may be a gift in some strange way, setting you on a path unlike any other.

**阿黛拉**：……我也是第一次听到这种解读方式。\
**Adèle**: I've certainly never thought of it that way.

司机想起了她在水晶工房里开的小玩笑。关于命运与“老板”。\
Though in saying that, she finds herself back in the Parlor of Crystals, weighing her attitude toward fate—her dismissal of it.

她晃晃脑袋，叹了一口气。\
She shakes her head and sighs.

**阿黛拉**：总之您的意思是可以？\
**Adèle**: But you're saying you can track her, aren't you?

**贝丽尔**：我能为你指出模糊的方向。\
**Beryl**: It will not show me where she is, but I will gain some sense of where she has been.

**阿黛拉**：足够了，总比毫无头绪要强得多。\
**Adèle**: Awesome. Better than searching blindly.

贝丽尔点点头，水晶灵摆散发出微弱的荧光。\
Beryl nods, her crystal pendulum emitting a dim light.

**贝丽尔**：左边。\
**Beryl**: To the left.

**阿黛拉**：行，听您的……往左。\
**Adèle**: Okay, then we go left.

折过又一个拐角，映入眼帘的通道与此前大同小异。\
They turn another corner, and the next corridor ahead looks much the same as the last.

**阿黛拉**：等等！我做个记号。\
**Adèle**: Wait! I should leave some sort of mark.

阿黛拉拾起一块碎石，在墙壁上划出不知第多少个箭头。\
Adèle picks up a stone and scratches yet another arrow on the wall.

**阿黛拉**：我们已经来到相当深的地方了，但走了这么久什么都没找到。\
**Adèle**: Umm, we've been walking for a while now, but we still haven't found anything. Forgive me, madame, but are you sure your divination—

布翁尼女士，您的占卜真的告诉您——

**贝丽尔**：嘘。\
**Beryl**: Shh.

**贝丽尔**：看起来我们有所收获了。\
**Beryl**: Look. The fruits of your search.

阿黛拉沿着贝丽尔的眼神看去——通道的尽头，一个轮廓一闪而过。\
Following Beryl's gaze, she catches a silhouette flicker at the far end.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

她压低身子，稍稍抬起手臂。如果对方突然扑过来，迎接他的将会是一团火焰。\
She crouches, raising her hand slightly, ready to strike with her flames if needed.

在阿黛拉戒备的目光中，人影走入煤油灯的光亮。\
Adèle watches guardedly as the figure steps into the light.

**罗西教授**：是来探险的人吗？请帮帮忙，我的头灯出了故障，又和学生们失散了……\
**Professor Roseau**: Who's there? Oh, a fellow explorer? What luck! You see, my headlamp's gone out, and I've been separated from my students.

**罗西教授**：等到了地面——嗯？你是昨天的那个小姑娘？\
**Professor Roseau**: I wonder if you might help me get to the surf—wait, you! Are you not that same young lady from yesterday?

**罗西教授**：还有……贝丽尔·布翁尼女士？\
**Professor Roseau**: And you, Madame Beryl Bouanich?

**罗西教授**：你们怎么会来这种地方？\
**Professor Roseau**: What on earth are you two doing here?

**阿黛拉**：你们认识？\
**Adèle**: You know each other?

她回头看向贝丽尔，而怀疑与戒备只换来了同行者泰然自若的回应。\
Adèle looks back at Beryl, but her suspicion washes up against her calm composure.

**贝丽尔**：我曾旁听过罗西先生的公开讲座，他的一些想法让我很感兴趣。\
**Beryl**: I have attended a number of Professor Roseau's lectures. His ideas are most intriguing.

贝丽尔的介绍戛然而止，提供的信息足以展示她广泛的人脉。\
Beryl's introduction is cut notably short. But it hints all the more at how wide her influence reaches.

但对于这个突然出现在此处的男人，熟人的熟人还算不上值得信任的理由。\
But this man himself does not earn any trust for being an acquaintance's acquaintance.

**阿黛拉**：罗西教授，我无论如何都联系不上西莉亚，您知道她去哪儿了吗？\
**Adèle**: Was Célia with you, Professor? I've been looking for her.

**阿黛拉**：我打了好几通电话到您的研究室，但始终没人接听。\
**Adèle**: It's serious. I tried calling the campus, but no one answered.

**罗西教授**：西莉亚？今天她的确没有露面，本来她应该和我们一起来的……但我还以为她只是临时有事？\
**Professor Roseau**: Célia? She was supposed to join us today, yes, but I'm afraid I haven't seen her. Most unlike her to do such a thing, but perhaps she had a change of plans.

阿黛拉打量着面前一脸茫然的男子，一个猜测浮现。\
Adèle studies the man's bewildered face. A thought crosses her mind.

**阿黛拉**：冒犯了。\
**Adèle**: Forgive me.

**罗西教授**：什么？\
**Professor Roseau**: Huh?

这一步鉴宝火循环+音效\
Feufeu lunges for the professor's wrist, sending fire crawling up his fingers.

幼龙猛地扑向教授的手腕，火焰顺着手指爬上他的皮肤。\
The flames flicker, fading quickly, leaving only a trace of warmth. The fire accepts him.

它们短暂带来少许热度，随后飞快熄灭。火认可了他的身份。

**罗西教授**：塔沃尼尔小姐！你这是……\
**Professor Roseau**: Ms. Tavernier! What are you doing?

**阿黛拉**：鉴定真伪的神秘术。\
**Adèle**: No need to be alarmed; it's just my arcane skill. It's a relief to know you're as real as you appear.

这下我们可以放心了，您是真的。

**阿黛拉**：您应当也听说过“热沃当的野兽”出没的传闻，加上地下墓穴里本就有不少魔精栖息……\
**Adèle**: But you have heard about the reappearance of the Beasts of Gévaudan, no? To say nothing of the Critters that surely nest down here ...

**阿黛拉**：也许会有怪物披上人皮接近身边，必须谨慎些。\
**Adèle**: Monsters wearing human skin could be lurking nearby. We can't be too cautious.

**罗西教授**：感谢你的提醒。\
**Professor Roseau**: I appreciate the warning.

他掸了掸袖口并不存在的灰烬，拾起之前被打断的话题。\
He brushes away imaginary ashes from his sleeve and resumes the prior conversation.

**罗西教授**：西莉亚之前也有过整理资料太投入而迟到的时候，你确定她不在家吗？\
**Professor Roseau**: Knowing Célia, it may very well be that she lost track of time organizing her research materials. Are you quite certain she's not at home?

**阿黛拉**：她是提过要出门为课题做准备。我去过她家里了，没人在。\
**Adèle**: That does sound like her. But I went to her place. No one was there.

**罗西教授**：她去哪家咖啡馆了也说不定。西莉亚是成年人了，你为什么这样急着找她呢？\
**Professor Roseau**: In all likelihood, she's in some café with her nose buried in a book. But miss, why is it that you are so concerned with finding her?

**罗西教授**：——就像你知道她肯定会有危险。\
**Professor Roseau**: It's as if you're certain she's in some kind of danger.

阿黛拉注意到教授将手背向身后。那是一个警戒姿势。\
She cannot help but notice he's moved one hand behind his back—a guarded stance.

**阿黛拉**：布翁尼女士能为我作证。因为……\
**Adèle**: She may well be. Madame Bouanich has had a premonition.

她向教授简单描述了预言与噩梦，以及那条作为证据的项链。\
They go over a brief account of the prophecy, the nightmare, and the necklace that serves as proof.

听完这些，教授松了一口气——紧接着笑出声来。\
When she finishes, the professor exhales softly, before bursting into laughter.

**罗西教授**：布翁尼女士。我本来不该对您说这些，但您实在太纵容塔沃尼尔小姐了。\
**Professor Roseau**: Madame Bouanich, forgive my bluntness, but you've been indulging this young lady far too much.

**罗西教授**：您还看不出来吗？她该做的是回家好好睡一觉。\
**Professor Roseau**: Scurrying about down here? What this young lady needs is a good rest.

**贝丽尔**：她有自己的判断。\
**Beryl**: It is her will that brought us here.

他转向阿黛拉，神情中仍然带着怜悯和不以为意，仿佛刚才听到的一切都不值得被认真考量。\
He turns to Adèle, pity mingling with paternalism in a single toxic facade, as if she had only been some babbling child pointing at a monster beneath her bed.

**罗西教授**：我明白你们感情好，所以你会过度担忧西莉亚的安危。\
**Professor Roseau**: Miss, I know you're a dear friend of Célia's and worried about her safety ...

**罗西教授**：但现在城里蔓延的癔症传染性很强，防不胜防，谁都可能不知不觉着了它的道。\
**Professor Roseau**: But you mustn't let yourself become paranoid, especially with all of this hysteria spreading through the city as of late.

**阿黛拉**：……您的意思是我疯了，这些都是我幻想出来的？\
**Adèle**: Are you saying I'm making things up? That this is just some kind of mania?

**阿黛拉**：这不可能！如果一切都是我的幻想，那条项链要怎么解释？\
**Adèle**: It isn't! Absolutely not! How else could you explain the necklace!

**罗西教授**：也许是你记错了，也许你感染癔症的时间比你以为的要早得多。\
**Professor Roseau**: There may be many explanations—many indeed. Though I fear, in the worst case, that you've been under the spell of this mania for much longer than you realize.

**罗西教授**：孩子，你再仔细想想。真有这样一条你在梦中拿到的项链？那它现在在哪里？\
**Professor Roseau**: Think, miss. This necklace you were given in this dream of yours ... Where did it go? Where is it now?

**阿黛拉**：这……它被拿走了。费利西安她……\
**Adèle**: I-It was Félicienne. She—

阿黛拉迟疑地停下。\
Adèle hesitates mid-step.

她意识到如果宣称它被一个会凭空消失的雇主带走了，只会让自己听起来更像是个疯子。\
Bringing up her vanishing employer would only make the situation worse.

**阿黛拉**：我记得……我看见……\
**Adèle**: I remember ... I saw it ...

她拼命从脑海里挤轧出一些模糊的画面。\
She wrings her memory like a dry sponge.

在墓穴尽头的黑暗里，她似乎又看见了与梦中完全相同的皮毛。\
At the end of the tomb's darkness, she spies the same fur that had haunted her dream.

**阿黛拉**：——小心！\
**Adèle**: Watch out!

毛绒绒的黑影尖叫着躲闪，声音甚至盖过了她的惊呼。\
The furry shadow screams and darts away, its cry louder than her gasp.

**罗西教授**：我说了你需要休息，塔沃尼尔小姐。你瞧，那只是随处可见的普通魔精。\
**Professor Roseau**: Please, miss, those were simply ordinary Critters, not mythological beasts. I'm afraid my verdict stands. What you need is rest, my dear.

男子遗憾地摇了摇头，略带歉意地向一旁的贝丽尔递去一个眼神。\
The man shakes his head in regret, casting an apologetic glance toward Beryl.

**罗西教授**：我尊重占卜这门技艺，事实上我的研究领域也与其有许多重合。\
**Professor Roseau**: As much respect as I may hold for the art of divination—in fact, my own field of study overlaps with it quite a bit—

**罗西教授**：但在我看来，占卜终究是帮助人们做出决定的辅助材料。\
**Professor Roseau**: Ultimately, divination is but a tool, and an auxiliary one at that.

**罗西教授**：在这个时代，我们试图从谷底爬起来。许多人都在寻找向上的路，可还没有谁找到最好的那条。\
**Professor Roseau**: In this era, everyone is clamoring to find the true path out of their predicaments, but I have yet to hear of anyone who has found an ultimate answer.

**罗西教授**：这是条艰难的路，唯有所有人的心意合一才有可能实现，我也好，我在研究中认识的同道也罢，包括西莉亚在内，大家都在为之努力。\
**Professor Roseau**: I believe that it is only when all of society is united that we will have any chance of success. Indeed, that is my team's and Célia's shared goal.

**罗西教授**：可总有无耻之徒冒充先知，谎称自己找到了答案，用谎言去控制集体。\
**Professor Roseau**: There are, of course, those who claim to have found the secret to creating such a society. But they are nothing but imposters.

**罗西教授**：那些谎言给他们带去了本不必经历的厄运。他们以为能控制集体，最终被集体的记忆反噬。\
**Professor Roseau**: Little do they know that the lies they spout are destined to backfire, causing suffering and disaster, as they too are devoured into the collective unconscious.

**罗西教授**：每个人的判断都只能由每个人自己做出。你说对吗，阿黛拉小姐？\
**Professor Roseau**: We must make our own decisions. Wouldn't you agree, Ms. Tavernier?

**阿黛拉**：……您说的有道理。\
**Adèle**: I suppose you have a point.

面前的年长者言辞诚恳，那股涌上胸口的怒气逐渐消散。\
His words seem to be, against all her desires to the contrary, painfully earnest, and the anger rising in her chest fades.

冷静下来后，阿黛拉意识到刚才的自己有些不对劲。她原本并不是易怒的人……\
But the calm itself is revealing. She has never been this quick to anger before.

**阿黛拉**：……不过您误会了，我很确定一定有什么地方不对劲。\
**Adèle**: But I'm certain something is wrong. And that's exactly why I'm here!

我正是为了弄清这一切而来的——

她依然注视着狭长的墓穴通道，深浅不一的黑暗仍在涌动。\
Adèle glances back to the narrow tomb passage, where she spots the shifting darkness once more.

它越来越近，越发清晰，凝聚成再熟悉不过的人影。\
It draws closer, sharper, until it solidifies into a familiar figure.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚……？！\
**Adèle**: Célia?

**阿黛拉**：等等！\
**Adèle**: Don't go!

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉？\
**Beryl**: Adèle?

人影一晃，消失不见。

甚至顾不上重新点燃熄灭的煤油灯，阿黛拉立刻抬腿追去。\
The shadow flickers and vanishes. Without even relighting her lamp, Adèle runs after it.

**罗西教授**：阿黛拉小姐，不要一个人行动——\
**Professor Roseau**: Wait, miss! Please don't venture off alone!

身后的呼喊声与光亮很快远去。\
The light behind her fades, and with it the shouting of the professor.

## AFF-12 天国阶梯 / A Ladder to Heaven

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚，等等我！你跑什么？\
**Adèle**: Célia, wait! Why are you running from me?

追着模糊的影子，阿黛拉转过又一个拐角，错愕地停下了脚步。\
Chasing the blur, Adèle turns another corner and stops, startled.

**阿黛拉**：死路？\
**Adèle**: A dead end?

煤油灯被重新点燃，照亮道路的尽头。那里除了堵得严实的砖石外空无一物。\
Her relit lamp reveals nothing ahead of her but tightly packed bricks.

**阿黛拉**：她去哪里了——\
**Adèle**: Where did she go?

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉！为什么你和他们在一起？\
**Célia**: Adèle! Why are you with them?

一双手忽然从身后抓住了阿黛拉的双肩，她被猛地扳过了身子——映入眼中的是好友急切的面孔。\
Two hands grab Adèle's shoulders and wrench her around—face-to-face with her lost and very anxious friend.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚？我明明看到你在前面，你是怎么……\
**Adèle**: Célia? How did you ...? I-I just saw you over there.

**阿黛拉**：你还好吗？到底发生了什么？你不知道我有多担心……\
**Adèle**: Never mind. Are you alright? What happened to you? I've been worried sick.

扣住肩膀的手猛地用力，关切的话语被惊慌地打断。\
The grip tightens, concern turning into panic mid-sentence.

**西莉亚**：我在问你！你为什么会和他们在一起？\
**Célia**: Answer me! Why are you with them?

**阿黛拉**：他们？谁？\
**Adèle**: Them? Who do you mean?

**西莉亚**：——重塑之手！\
**Célia**: Manus Vindictae!

一个仅在梦中出现过的名字被咬牙切齿地喊了出来。\
A name heard only in dreams bursts out through clenched teeth.

**西莉亚**：罗西骗了我们所有人，他一直是重塑之手的一员——他根本不想拯救任何东西！\
**Célia**: The professor deceived us all. He's been a member of Manus Vindictae this entire time. He never wanted to help anyone!

**西莉亚**：绝对不能让他把门打开！意象的巴黎绝不能降临！\
**Célia**: We can't let him open the gate! We can't let him unleash the Imagerial Paris!

**阿黛拉**：等等、等等！西莉亚，冷静点。\
**Adèle**: Wait-wait-wait! Hold on a minute, Célia.

**阿黛拉**：那个什么重塑之手……还有世界毁灭？从头慢慢说，好吗？\
**Adèle**: Manus Vindictae, an imaginary Paris ... Please, I don't understand.

阿黛拉抓住好友的双手握紧，这起了效，手心传来的颤抖逐渐减弱。\
Adèle grasps her friend's trembling hands, holding tight until the shaking subsides.

**西莉亚**：……你还记得文森特吗？\
**Célia**: Do you remember Vincent?

**阿黛拉**：当然，我记得他，那个在街上乱开车的家伙！\
**Adèle**: The madman that rammed into my car?

**阿黛拉**：我还梦到他变成了“热沃当的野兽”——西莉亚，你也在那个梦里。\
**Adèle**: He turned into a Beast of Gévaudan in my dream. You were in it, too, Célia.

她试探性地看向好友。\
She looks to her friend, expecting yet more doubt.

**西莉亚**：不，阿黛拉……那不是梦。\
**Célia**: No, Adèle. It wasn't a dream.

**西莉亚**：昨天上午，我去医院想要探望文森特。\
**Célia**: Yesterday morning, I went to the hospital to check in on him.

**阿黛拉**：正好是我去布翁尼女士的水晶工房的时候。\
**Adèle**: That would be around the time I visited Madame Bouanich's parlor.

西莉亚点了点头。她看起来镇静了许多，但嘴唇仍在微微打着颤。\
Célia nods. She's put on a calm face, but the slightest quiver in her lips shows through.

**西莉亚**：到了医院后，医生说他已经被家里人接回故乡休养了。\
**Célia**: But when I arrived, I was told that he'd been taken to his hometown by his family. I truly didn't think much of it at the time, although I was remiss to have lost my chance to say goodbye.

当时我没有多想，只是遗憾没能道声别……

**西莉亚**：可就在回去的路上，我却看到文森特坐上了一辆雪铁龙。\
**Célia**: But on my way back, I saw him again. He was getting into a car, one that I recognized right away—Professor Roseau's.

我认得那辆车，那是罗西教授的座驾。

说到这里，她深吸了一口气——再吐出时，气息中带着惊怒交加的颤抖。\
She takes a deep breath, her breath holding back both shock and fury.

**西莉亚**：这太奇怪了，我放心不下，立刻拦下一辆车追了上去，看到他们从一处隐蔽的入口进了地下墓穴。\
**Célia**: It was altogether too strange. I couldn't just let it go. So, I hailed a car and tailed them. They parked in a hidden spot and entered the catacombs together.

**西莉亚**：他们一路向下，我悄悄跟在后面。不知过了多久，就在我以为要走到地狱了的时候……\
**Célia**: They kept going deeper, and I followed. I don't know how long we walked. It felt like we were descending into hell itself.

**西莉亚**：我看到了一个房间。\
**Célia**: Then I saw the room.

**罗西教授**：你大可感到荣幸，不是所有人都拥有来到这里的资格。\
**Professor Roseau**: You should feel honored, Vincent. Few have ever had the privilege to stand in this place.

向身后投去施舍般的一瞥，男子阔步走入道路尽头的房间，神情恍惚的青年紧随其后。\
He throws a dismissive glance over his shoulder, striding deeper toward the room at the corridor's end, a dazed young man trailing behind.

片刻后，藏在拐角处的年轻女子才谨慎地探出身来。\
Moments later, the hidden young woman peeks around the corner.

**西莉亚**：这是什么地方……？\
**Célia**: Where are we?

入口处透出的奇妙光亮刺入她的双眼，透着说不出的诡异。\
The strange light spilling from the entrance stings her eyes, unnervingly bright.

**西莉亚**：……\
**Célia**: ...

她定了定神，小心翼翼地向二人身影消失的地方靠近。\
She steadies herself and edges closer to where the two figures vanished.

空荡的地板正中赫然张开着一个规整的圆形洞口，洞壁挂着一架看不出材质的爬梯。\
The center of the room is dominated by a strange circular pit, its interior wall fitted with a ladder of unknown make.

**文森特**：一架向下的梯子？我还以为我们已经在地下墓穴的最深处了……\
**Vincent**: A ladder? I thought we were already in the deepest part of the catacombs.

**文森特**：请您原谅我的愚蠢，我的陛下——这梯子通向哪里？\
**Vincent**: N-Never mind my mumbling, Your Majesty. Only, could I ask—where does this ladder lead?

**罗西教授**：如其在上，如其在下——不要被眼前的表象迷惑。\
**Professor Roseau**: As above, so below—don't let appearances fool you.

**文森特**：什么？您是说……\
**Vincent**: Huh? You mean ...?

**罗西教授**：是的，这里就是它的入口。\
**Professor Roseau**: Yes, this is its entrance.

**罗西教授**：意象宝库、世界灵魂、所有人的梦境、集体潜意识的海洋……它有太多的称呼，但我更愿意称呼它为——迷思海。\
**Professor Roseau**: The Archive of Imagery, the anima mundi, the shared dream, the sea of collective unconscious ... It goes by many names, but I prefer to call it the Depths of Myth.

**罗西教授**：它的确存在，就在你的面前。\
**Professor Roseau**: And it exists in a more tangible form than you may think, my dear boy. In fact, it is right in front of you.

**文森特**：噢……天哪！我从没想到……\
**Vincent**: My God! This is beyond my wildest imagination.

**罗西教授**：但一条小小的裂缝只能引来一缕微光，不过是杯水车薪。\
**Professor Roseau**: For now, it is but a small crack in the veil, nowhere near enough.

**罗西教授**：想要真正光复曾照耀这片土地的荣光，我们需要更多的光亮——就像是奥斯特里茨的太阳曾带来的那般光亮。\
**Professor Roseau**: We must open the gateway. If we wish to restore the glory that once shone on this land, we need a far more radiant light, like the brilliance of the Sun of Austerlitz.

他的目光向下，双眼倒映着忽明忽暗的光芒。\
He stares downward, his eyes reflecting the brilliant, flickering light below.

**罗西教授**：这有一定风险。意象的混沌盛宴会吞没所及之物，下潜者对灵与肉的认同将被颠覆，成为另一副模样。\
**Professor Roseau**: As I told you, there is risk here. The maelstrom of imagery will devour any who dive into it, reshaping their body and soul into something else entirely.

**罗西教授**：——不过别担心，文森特。你还记得我对你的教导吗？\
**Professor Roseau**: But I have faith in you, my boy. You remember what I taught you, don't you?

**文森特**：当然……当然！这是何等的荣幸！\
**Vincent**: O-Of course! I'm ready! It would be my greatest honor!

年轻人没有犹豫哪怕片刻。

他沿着那架爬梯向下，灵巧地活动起手脚，眨眼间便消失不见。\
The young man doesn't hesitate for even a moment. He descends the ladder, his movements deft and sure, as he vanishes into the deep.

**罗西教授**：你应当会发现一把钥匙，一枚法兰西之蓝——它是一位可敬前人的临终发现。\
**Professor Roseau**: You must find the key—the French Blue—a pivotal discovery by one of our most venerable pioneers.

**罗西教授**：她在下潜时不幸消融在了迷思的深处，却也找到了一只至关重要的锚。\
**Professor Roseau**: Sadly, her existence dissolved into the Depths of Myth just as she had nearly claimed it. Still, her discovery has paved the way for our victory today.

**罗西教授**：它会帮助我们架起物质与精神世界之间的天梯，帮助我们到达那个完美的世界——你找到它了吗，文森特？\
**Professor Roseau**: Together we will build a bridge between the material and spiritual realms, one that will guide us toward a more perfect world. Have you found it, Vincent?

**文森特？**：是的，我找到了！\
**Vincent?**: I have it! I have it!

首先沿着梯子抓上来的是一双粗大的利爪。\
The young man reappears, but where his hands should be, he instead grips the side with a pair of massive lupine talons.

**文森特？**：如此炽热、如此耀眼——那颗太阳就在这里！\
**Vincent?**: It's bright, so blindingly bright, as bright as the Sun!

随后，扭曲的头颅从洞口探出，锐利的獠牙间闪烁着瑰丽的蓝色。\
A twisted head follows, jaws glinting with vivid blue ichor dripping from its fangs.

——那副模样显然已经不再属于人类。\
An inhuman, monstrous face.

**罗西教授**：很好，很好！就是这样，将它带给我——带到这一侧来！\
**Professor Roseau**: Wonderful! That's it, bring it to me! Bring it to me!

但下一秒，那缕蓝化作飘散的光点，消失不见。\
But in the next instant, the blue scatters into drifting light and fades away.

**罗西教授**：……\
**Professor Roseau**: ...

爬梯边男子脸上狂喜的神色凝滞片刻后，逐渐褪去。\
The rapture on the man's face freezes only to melt away to nothing.

**罗西教授**：真是遗憾，亲爱的文森特……看来你并不是合适的人选。\
**Professor Roseau**: What a shame, dear boy. It seems you weren't worthy after all.

野兽发出沮丧的悲鸣。

男子并未理会，将视线平静地转向了入口处。\
The beast lets out a mournful cry. But the professor ignores it as he turns toward the entrance.

**罗西教授**：也许你可以帮我完成最后的实验——西莉亚，我最聪明的学生。\
**Professor Roseau**: Perhaps then, the final experiment must fall to you, Célia, my brightest student.

**西莉亚**：——！！\
**Célia**: ...!!

**西莉亚**：劳伦·罗西根本就是一个疯子……\
**Célia**: Laurent Roseau is a madman.

愤怒与悲伤扭曲了好友一向温和的面孔。\
Rage and sorrow twist her friend's once studious, gentle face.

**西莉亚**：我以为他真的想用超心理学研究改变现状，而且已经走得比所有人都远……\
**Célia**: I thought he genuinely wanted to make the world better through parapsychology. He'd gone much further than anyone else.

**西莉亚**：现在我终于明白了，他引用的那些前所未见的观点，他口中所说的理想，全都是为了欺骗我们——\
**Célia**: But I was perhaps too foolish, too naive to realize that all his novel theories—all the inspiring dreams he shared with us—were lies, meant to ensnare us, to use us.

**西莉亚**：传闻中城里出没的所有那些怪物、那些癔症和失踪案，都是他和重塑之手搞的鬼。\
**Célia**: All those rumors of monsters in the city, the madness in the streets, the disappearances—they were his handiwork. He and Manus Vindictae.

**阿黛拉**：罗西、迷思海、重塑之手……？\
**Adèle**: Professor Roseau? The Depths of Myth? Manus Vindictae?

**西莉亚**：是的。文森特就在我面前变成了“热沃当的野兽”，我亲眼看到了……我也……\
**Célia**: I saw him—Vincent. He became a Beast of Gévaudan. I saw it with my own eyes. Then he turned to me and ...

好友的声音哽咽了。

无数疑问接踵而至，但它们最终都为一件事让开了道路。\
Her voice breaks with emotion. Countless questions crowd forward, but in the end, they all yield to one.

**阿黛拉**：谢天谢地，还好你逃了出来！\
**Adèle**: But you're safe now, Cici. That's all that matters!

**阿黛拉**：我们先离开这个鬼地方，其他事出去了再说！\
**Adèle**: We'll figure things out later. For now, we need to get out of this accursed place.

**Adèle holds Célia's hands so tight her knuckles blanch. Whatever else, she's certain of one thing**: she won't lose sight of her friend ever again.

阿黛拉抓紧了那双手。她有十足的自信，不会再弄丢寻回的珍藏。

于是她迈开了步子——并没有脚步随之跟上。\
So she steps forward, yet no footsteps follow.

**阿黛拉**：……怎么了，西莉亚？快走啊？\
**Adèle**: Cici, what's wrong? Let's go, come on! We have to go!

她拉着的人仍站在原地，苦涩地扯起了嘴角。\
Her friend doesn't move with her; she stands motionless, expressionless, until her mask is broken by the hint of trailing light and faint concern written on her face.

**西莉亚**：太好了，阿黛拉……\
**Célia**: I'm so very glad, Adèle.

**西莉亚**：在你看来，我还是原来的模样吗？\
**Célia**: I still truly seem myself through your eyes, right?

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚，你……你刚才……\
**Adèle**: Ah, Cici, what do you mean? What else would you look like?

有那么一瞬间，眼前熟悉的面孔覆上了一层黑色的阴影——那绝不是幻觉。\
For an instant, she sees it through the veil of shadow. It's no illusion.

**西莉亚**：……我没能跑掉。他们发现了我，把我从那架梯子上扔了下去。\
**Célia**: They captured me, Adèle, and threw me down the ladder.

**西莉亚**：数不尽的声音钻进我脑袋里，我感觉不到自己身体的存在……\
**Célia**: So many voices flooded my head—an endless number—until I couldn't feel my own body anymore.

**西莉亚**：就是在那些声音中，我得知了“重塑之手”这个名字……一切就像是一场噩梦，疯狂、混乱……\
**Célia**: They told me things—whispered about this Manus Vindictae. Huh, everything struck me so quickly, so chaotically, yet it felt so long, like an endless moment.

**西莉亚**：但慌乱中，我摸到了一个东西——那把钥匙，那颗钻石。\
**Célia**: But I found something in the current—a diamond—the key to all this.

**西莉亚**：重塑之手的人要利用它打开迷思海的入口，到时候巴黎会被混乱的意象侵占。\
**Célia**: If that diamond falls into their hands, they'll use it to unleash the Depths of Myth. And when that happens, all of Paris will be drowned in the maelstrom of imagery. And I'm afraid everyone will suffer just as Vincent and I have.

恐怕所有人……都会遭遇和文森特一样的事。

**西莉亚**：我必须把它带走，可之后呢？\
**Célia**: I had to get the diamond away from them; I had to make sure they couldn't use it.

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉，你说过，真正的法兰西之蓝早已被二次切割。这枚钻石只可能是重塑之手制造的仿品。\
**Célia**: But I remembered what you told me, Adèle. That the real French Blue was recut long ago. Then, the diamond must be an imitation, something fabricated by Manus Vindictae, no?

**西莉亚**：——你的神秘术可以销毁它。\
**Célia**: So a thought struck me: if it's only a forgery, then your arcane skill can destroy it.

**西莉亚**：所以我想着这件事……我想着，我一定要见到你。\
**Célia**: I kept thinking about that over and over and told myself I had to reach you.

**西莉亚**：随后，我的眼前真的出现了一扇门，一扇我拉开过无数次的出租车副驾驶席的门。\
**Célia**: Then, just like that, a car door appeared in front of me, one I truly could not forget. It was your passenger door.

西莉亚长舒一口气，脸上浮现出一种解脱般的神情。\
She releases this long-held truth like a taut rubber band, immediately snapping the moments together.

**西莉亚**：也许那片迷思海真的连接着所有人的梦境……甚至能模糊现实与梦的边界。\
**Célia**: Maybe the Depths of Myth really does connect our dreams, blurring the line between what's real and what's imagined.

**西莉亚**：它让我见到了你。\
**Célia**: At the very least, it led me to you.

**阿黛拉**：那个梦……所以那时候真的是你？\
**Adèle**: So then, in that bizarre dream, it really was you?

**西莉亚**：是的。迷思海是很伟大的发现，它可以将我们都联系起来。\
**Célia**: Yes, it was. The Depths of Myth—how it connects us—truly is amazing. But I'm afraid I can't go any further. Too much has changed. I've changed.

可我的冒险……也到此为止了。

**西莉亚**：他们不会就此罢休的。罗西掘地三尺也会将那枚钻石找回来，继续实现他梦中的巴黎。\
**Célia**: They won't stop chasing their key. Roseau will do whatever it takes to retrieve it and inflict this suffering on all of Paris.

**西莉亚**：必须阻止他们。告诉我，阿黛拉，你一定已经烧毁它了，对不对？\
**Célia**: Please, Adèle, tell me you destroyed the diamond as I asked. You did, didn't you?

她急切地回握阿黛拉的双手，试图求得一个令自己安心的答案。\
She clutches at her, desperate for an answer.

阿黛拉哑然了。半晌，她才颤抖着寻回了自己的声音。\
But Adèle is at a loss for words, unable to summon up an explanation without stammering.

**阿黛拉**：我……那时候发生的一切都太诡异了……\
**Adèle**: I-I ... It was all so strange and confusing ...

**阿黛拉**：我担心你是不是真的出了事，害怕那就是唯一的线索，所以我……\
**Adèle**: I was worried about you, and I thought the diamond might be the only clue as to where you were, so I ...

**阿黛拉**：……我还没有销毁它。现在它在费利西安那里。\
**Adèle**: I didn't destroy it; it should be with Félicienne now.

**西莉亚**：——！\
**Célia**: ...!

**西莉亚**：费利西安……“费利西安”？\
**Célia**: Félicienne ... That's terrible! You can't mean that Félicienne?

**阿黛拉**：对，就是吃饭时我和你提到过的那个老主顾——\
**Adèle**: That's right. I told you about her over dinner.

**西莉亚**：不……不对！我终于明白了，原来……\
**Célia**: No! This is terrible! I see now. They're all ...

**西莉亚**：听我说，阿黛拉！那个费利西安也和他们是一伙的，是重塑之手的人！\
**Célia**: Listen to me, Adèle! Félicienne is an enemy! She's with Manus Vindictae!

**西莉亚**：你绝不能再靠近她了！你不知道，她早就已经——\
**Célia**: You mustn't trust her! She's more dangerous than she—

**西莉亚**：呃……唔……\
**Célia**: Uhh—ughhh ...

**阿黛拉**：什么……\
**Adèle**: Huh ...?

**Félicienne**: How rude. You really ought to reflect on your choice of friends, my darling.\
**Félicienne**: I've no patience for personal slander.

**费利西安**：我亲爱的阿黛拉，你的朋友真是没有教养。\
**费利西安**：我最讨厌别人在背后对我说短论长。

## AFF-13 与你同在 / Soul Mate

**阿黛拉**：不……不！西莉亚！\
**Adèle**: No. No! Célia!

她扑向倒在血泊中的好友，不知何处传来的细语声钻入脑海，声音越来越大。\
She falls to her knees beside her friend's body, the blood pooling around her, as a whisper slithers into her mind, growing louder and louder.

**阿黛拉**：呃……我的头…好疼……\
**Adèle**: Ugh ... My head ... hurts ...

鲜血、无力垂下的手掌、宝石闪耀的瑰丽光芒、熟悉嗓音的冷笑声……一切都被卷入混沌的漩涡。\
Blood. A limp hand. The gem's brilliant glow. A familiar voice, the cold sneers ... Everything spirals into chaos.

世界天旋地转，而后，黑暗笼罩其上。\
The world spins, and darkness swallows everything.

**？？？**：——深呼吸，亲爱的阿黛拉。\
**???**: Take a deep breath, Adèle.

**？？？**：来，把你的手给我。\
**???**: Come. Take my hand.

忽然间，模糊的声音沁入耳中。\
Soft, muffled voices seep into her ears.

**？？？**：该醒来了。\
**???**: Time to wake up, dear.

**阿黛拉**：——！

灯光是什么时候亮起来的？几次缓慢的眨眼后，她看清了眼前的面容。\
When did the lights come on? After several slow blinks, she begins to make sense of the faces staring down at her.

**阿黛拉**：布翁尼……女士？\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich?

**贝丽尔**：感觉好些了吗？\
**Beryl**: Feeling better?

**贝丽尔**：别着急，别动。我们就这样待一会儿，放轻松。大家都在这里。\
**Beryl**: Take a breath; rest a moment. We are here with you now.

**阿黛拉**：大家？\
**Adèle**: "We" ...?

看清一旁的另一个人影后，阿黛拉当即将贝丽尔拽到了身后。\
Seeing another figure beside them, Adèle instinctively leaps up to put Beryl behind her.

**阿黛拉**：离他远些，布翁尼女士！他就是罪魁祸首！\
**Adèle**: Stay away from him, Madame Bouanich! He's the one behind all this!

**罗西教授**：什么？\
**Professor Roseau**: What?

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚已经告诉我了！她亲眼看到你将自己的学生变成“热沃当的野兽”！\
**Adèle**: Célia told me everything! She saw you turn Vincent into a monster!

**罗西教授**：阿黛拉小姐……我看你需要一位医生。\
**Professor Roseau**: Oh, my dear girl. When we get you back to the surface, we must get you some immediate mental care.

**罗西教授**：您刚才在原地来回打转、又哭又笑，本以为布翁尼女士成功唤回了您的神智，结果您又突然说这种莫名其妙的话……\
**Professor Roseau**: You've been pacing around in circles, talking to yourself, laughing, and crying for who knows what reason. And now, just as I thought Madame Bouanich had managed to calm you down, you start spouting this nonsen—

**阿黛拉**：够了，别以为你能够骗过我！\
**Adèle**: Enough with your lies! You can't fool me!

**阿黛拉**：我劝你最好老实交待你知道的一切，然后和我去警局自首——\
**Adèle**: If you know what's good for you, you'll confess all your evil plots and come with me to the police.

**阿黛拉**：等等……什么？\
**Adèle**: Wait. Isn't that ...?

她本已蓄势待发，却在余光瞥见不起眼的小小印记时僵住了。\
She's ready to strike, but something in her periphery catches her eye.

在她身旁的墙壁上，赫然刻着一枚小巧的箭头符号。\
A small arrow mark carved into the stone beside her.

**阿黛拉**：这是……我之前划下的记号？\
**Adèle**: That mark. It's the one I made earlier.

**阿黛拉**：不会错，这个连笔画法的确是我的笔迹……\
**Adèle**: It ... It's exactly how I made it.

**阿黛拉**：但……我应该追着西莉亚跑出了很远，怎么会又回到了原地？\
**Adèle**: But I followed Célia; we went so far. How could I be back where I started?

**罗西教授**：我说过了，您一直在原地自言自语！\
**Professor Roseau**: Aren't you listening? All you've done is pace in circles and mutter to yourself! And now this rubbish about Célia.

而且您说什么西莉亚……

**罗西教授**：您真是疯了！好好看看，她根本不在这里！布翁尼女士也可以作证！\
**Professor Roseau**: For pity's sake, girl, look around! She's not here! Ask Madame Bouanich if you must!

**阿黛拉**：但……但我亲眼看见了！西莉亚伤得很重，我看见费利西安把她……\
**Adèle**: B-But I saw her with my own eyes. Félicienne stabbed her!

**阿黛拉**：我没有说谎！我的手上和脸上还有她的血……\
**Adèle**: It was real. It was true! She was dying in my arms. Her blood was on my face, my hands.

她下意识看向一路同行的女子，急切地伸出自己曾从血泊中抱起西莉亚身体的双手。\
She holds out her hands, the very ones she used to lift the bloodied body of her dearest friend.

——但那双手上除了方向盘磨出的薄茧之外，只有灰尘。\
But there's nothing there. No stains of red, nothing but old calluses.

**阿黛拉**：这怎么可能……\
**Adèle**: How could this be?

**阿黛拉**：这……这一定是有什么障眼法，您要相信我！\
**Adèle**: Th-This must be another one of his deceptions. You have to believe me!

她急切地抓起贝丽尔的手，像是扑向最后一根救命稻草。\
She grabs Madame Bouanich desperately, as if she were the only thing keeping her afloat.

**阿黛拉**：您可以用占卜验证我说的都是真的！\
**Adèle**: Can't you use your divination to see the truth? Please, madame!

求您了，布翁尼女士！

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚很危险，需要急救——她——\
**Adèle**: You have to help Célia. She's dying somewhere.

阿黛拉的声音逐渐低了下去，最终消失在空气里。\
Her voice trails off.

因为她看到了贝丽尔的表情，那个温柔的、沉默的微笑，背后有她并不想听见的答案。\
Adèle realizes that Beryl's answer isn't what she wants to hear.

**贝丽尔**：你身上的诅咒没有完全祛除，以至于产生了可怕的幻觉。\
**Beryl**: It seems this curse still shadows over you. What you saw were simply illusions.

**贝丽尔**：请放心，我会为你解决这些。\
**Beryl**: Rest assured. I will do what I can to help you through this.

贝丽尔向她伸出手，这反而让阿黛拉下意识地后退了两步。\
Beryl reaches toward her, but Adèle steps back.

**阿黛拉**：幻觉？不可能……\
**Adèle**: Illusions? So, even you think I ...?

**阿黛拉**：我分明看到了西莉亚……还有费利西安……对了！还有那枚钻石！\
**Adèle**: But there's no mistaking it! I saw Célia and Félicienne and the diamond!

**阿黛拉**：它被费利西安拿走了，西莉亚告诉我必须要毁了它！\
**Adèle**: Félicienne has it. Célia told me it has to be destroyed, or else ... or else ...

否则——否则——

阿黛拉再次开始感到天旋地转，那些窃窃私语声又开始在脑海中轰鸣，直到她听到贝丽尔疑惑的声音。\
The spinning returns, whispers swelling in her mind again, until she hears Beryl's puzzled tone.

**贝丽尔**：钻石？\
**Beryl**: The diamond?

**贝丽尔**：你是说你戴在颈间的这一枚吗？\
**Beryl**: You mean the one strung around your neck?

**阿黛拉**：……什么？\
**Adèle**: Huh?

阿黛拉跟随贝丽尔的视线低下头去——在她的胸前，分明闪烁着那抹瑰丽的蓝色。\
Following Beryl's gaze, Adèle lowers her head. There, on her chest, glimmers that same brilliant blue jewel.

**阿黛拉**：这怎么……可能？它应该在费利西安那里……\
**Adèle**: I-Impossible. Félicienne took it from me.

**阿黛拉**：它……一直戴在我的脖子上？\
**Adèle**: B-But how can it be here again?

**阿黛拉**：——不，这不可能！\
**Adèle**: No! This is absurd!

迷茫与错愕在惊骇的催化下，变为愤怒的熊熊烈火。\
Confusion and shock, under the weight of her fractured mind, ignite into searing rage.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚说的没错！这颗钻石一定有问题！\
**Adèle**: Célia was right! This wicked imitation must be destroyed!

**阿黛拉**：必须立刻毁掉它——小家伙！\
**Adèle**: It must be destroyed now! Come, Feufeu!

她呼唤肩头的幼龙，炙热的火焰蓄势待发——\
She calls to the little dragon on her shoulder, its little flame gathering to burst into a torrent—

本该如此。\
A blaze capable of destroying that false stone.

**阿黛拉**：怎么……？\
**Adèle**: Huh?

烈焰并未燃起。\
But the fire never comes.

**阿黛拉**：你在做什么，小家伙？快把它烧毁——\
**Adèle**: What's wrong, Feufeu? Destroy the diamond!

**阿黛拉**：小家伙？\
**Adèle**: Feufeu?

她侧过头，终于发现肩膀上空无一物。\
She feels the lack of weight before she sees it. Her beloved little companion has become the latest to disappear.

**阿黛拉**：怎么……回事？\
**Adèle**: What's going on?

与她共生的小小生灵是意识与灵魂的延伸，它本来绝不可能悄无声息地消失不见。\
But Feufeu is more than just a pet. It shares her mind and soul. It could never vanish like Célia did.

大脑一片空白，她逐渐感到一阵眩晕。\
Her mind goes blank again, dizziness swelling in waves.

**阿黛拉**：这……太奇怪了。\
**Adèle**: This is all too strange.

**阿黛拉**：我……我要做什么来着？\
**Adèle**: Wh-What was I doing again?

头疼欲裂，她听不到周围的任何声音，唯独自己的呼吸声震耳欲聋。\
Her head pounds. All sound vanishes except her own panicked breathing.

**阿黛拉**：对了，法兰西之蓝，西莉亚给我的那枚钻石……\
**Adèle**: Ah, right, the diamond that Célia gave to me.

**阿黛拉**：梦境是真的，我该烧掉它……\
**Adèle**: What she said was real. I have to destroy it.

决心短暂地浮出水面，随后迟疑的浪涛袭来，将它拍入深海。\
Resolve flickers to the surface, only to be dragged down by the tide of hesitation.

**阿黛拉**：但……这可是法兰西之蓝，所有人都以为永远消失的奇迹……\
**Adèle**: But this isn't any ordinary diamond; it's the miraculous French Blue.

**阿黛拉**：先人们成就的象征……我怎么能够毁了它呢?\
**Adèle**: Do I really have the right to destroy a national treasure?

吸入空气，吐出。光是这个动作就已经用尽了她的全力。\
Inhale, exhale. Even that simple act stretches her mental state.

**阿黛拉**：我想起来了……是西莉亚让我烧毁它，那是西莉亚给我的。\
**Adèle**: Who was it who asked me to destroy it anyway? Oh, it must've been Célia!

**阿黛拉**：那是西莉亚给我的……给我……我的！\
**Adèle**: But Célia ... She gave the diamond to me! Ah! It's mine!

最终，一声怒喝斥退了搅动大脑的一切杂音。\
At last, a sharp voice cuts through the noise clouding her head.

呼吸骤然变得通畅了起来，折磨着她的那种钻心的头疼消失了。\
Her breathing steadies, the stabbing pain recedes.

**阿黛拉**：…………\
**Adèle**: ...

急促的呼吸逐渐舒缓，一种如同酩酊般的安心感让一切烦恼与疑问都离她而去。\
She stops. A drowsy calm spreads through her. Every worry, every doubt slips away into a warm abyss.

**罗西教授**：您真的应该好好休息一下了，阿黛拉小姐。\
**Professor Roseau**: Please, miss. You seem to have been through a lot. You need some rest.

**罗西教授**：也许是地下郁积的那些不好的气息加重了您的症状……跟我来吧，我们先出去。\
**Professor Roseau**: Perhaps some fresh air might ease your symptoms. Come, I'll lead the way back to the surface.

**罗西教授**：刚好我和学生们订了餐厅，您可以和我们一起来吃些东西。\
**Professor Roseau**: My colleagues and I have a reservation at a restaurant nearby; please, join us for dinner.

宽厚的手掌拍上她的肩膀，她发现自己对此不再抗拒。\
A firm hand falls on her shoulder, and at last she finds herself unable to resist it.

**阿黛拉**：您说得对。\
**Adèle**: I think you're right, Professor.

**阿黛拉**：也许我的确需要呼吸一些新鲜空气了。\
**Adèle**: I need some fresh air.

阿黛拉听到自己欣然应下。镶着瑰丽蓝钻石的项链仍然沉甸甸地挂在颈间，触感十分真实。\
Adèle hears herself agreeing softly—meekly. The necklace, heavy with its vivid blue diamond, hangs against her skin—tangible, real.

仿佛它一直都在这里。\
As if it had always been there.

## AFF-14 大木偶剧场 / Grand Guignol

需要预约的高级餐厅或许不适合探险之后的晚宴。\
A fine restaurant that requires reservations may not be an ideal spot for dinner after an adventure.

没有释放压力的畅饮与欢谈声，所有人都在礼仪的约束下用餐。\
The atmosphere brooks no laughter, no clinking glasses—just conversation restrained under the weight of etiquette.

室内唯有微弱的交流声，以及刀叉与餐盘碰撞的交响。\
The room hums with quiet small talk pierced by the faint scraping of silver over porcelain.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

**贝丽尔**：你没法用单手切牛排的，先放下项链吧。\
**Beryl**: You cannot cut steak with a necklace in your hand, Adèle. Why not put it down? Just for a while.

**阿黛拉**：没有关系，就这样就行，不能再弄丢它了。\
**Adèle**: No. Thank you, madame, but I can't afford to lose it again.

右手的餐刀机械式地劈砍着牛排，不协调的敲击声在雅静的餐厅内回荡。\
She saws through her steak mechanically, arrhythmically, lost in undercooked thought.

直到瓷质餐盘的边缘出现裂缝，肌肉才终于断开，但仍有筋腱相连。\
The sawing becomes like a chore; she pushes through muscle and sinew until she's all but sawing the plate in half.

**阿黛拉**：该死的，快些分开。\
**Adèle**: Damn! This is practically a tire, not a steak!

**贝丽尔**：我来帮你。\
**Beryl**: Allow me.

**阿黛拉**：……不必了，这是我的事情。\
