**Adèle**: No. Thank you.

闲谈期间，身旁餐桌的食客走上前来。\
During idle conversation, a diner from the next table steps forward.

**阴郁的少年**：贝丽尔女士，好久不见。您果然也在巴黎。\
**Pensive Young Man**: Oh, Madame Bouanich. It's been a long time. I'm glad to see that you're still in Paris.

**贝丽尔**：你还在寻找遗失的命运吗？\
**Beryl**: And you? Still in search of your lost fate?

**阴郁的少年**：我……我不知晓，贝丽尔女士。\
**Pensive Young Man**: I ... I'm not sure anymore.

**阴郁的少年**：也许如您所言，命运本身只是无常的水流，赋予其意义只是一种无稽之谈。\
**Pensive Young Man**: What you said may have been right: fate is a kind of erratic stream—to search for meaning in it or impose meaning upon it is pointless.

**阴郁的少年**：但我仍想进行……一些无用的尝试。我们总能找到办法的。\
**Pensive Young Man**: Even so, some part of me still longs to try. Perhaps it will one day be in reach.

**阴郁的少年**：不提这些了。听说劳伦·罗西先生在起死回生术上有了成功的尝试。也许我们都离掌握命运更近了一步。\
**Pensive Young Man**: But I wouldn't want us to dwell on my insignificant problems. I understand that Professor Roseau has made some interesting breakthroughs in the resurrection of the dead.

**阴郁的少年**：对了，您身边的这位女士是？\
**Pensive Young Man**: Though first, perhaps you'd introduce the lady here?

**贝丽尔**：她是我之前提到的，站在水流交汇处的人。\
**Beryl**: She is the one I spoke of before, the girl who stands at the confluence of streams.

**贝丽尔**：阿黛拉，这位是我的一位老主顾。我们都叫他“蜂鸟”。\
**Beryl**: Adèle, this is a regular of mine. We call him Hummingbird.

**阿黛拉**：……你好。\
**Adèle**: A pleasure, I'm sure.

**蜂鸟**：原来是你。\
**Hummingbird**: Ah, yes, I see what she means.

**蜂鸟**：阿黛拉女士，您现在感觉如何？是否时常看见不属于尘世之人的身影，听见那些遗失的声音？你是否仍是你自己？\
**Hummingbird**: You look a little pensive, miss. I wonder have you found yourself seeing otherworldly figures and hearing elusive voices? Are you still yourself?

**阿黛拉**：你在说什么？我无法理解。\
**Adèle**: What are you talking about?

少年细心地注意到阿黛拉异常的举动。片刻后，他端来了另外的食物——一碗炖土豆泥，以及一碟马卡龙。\
The young man notices Adèle's behavior. A moment later, he returns with new dishes—a bowl of mashed potatoes and a plate of macarons.

**蜂鸟**：比起牛排，也许您会更喜欢这些。\
**Hummingbird**: I'd say you'd prefer these over steak.

右手放下了握着的刀，在两个瓷盘间摇摆，最终接过了那碟马卡龙。\
She sets down her knife, wavering between the two plates before finally taking the macarons.

**阿黛拉**：味道不错。\
**Adèle**: They're passable.

**阿黛拉**：可惜还是拉杜丽的出品要更好些。\
**Adèle**: Though nowhere near as good as Ladurée, I must say.

算不上褒奖的话语，但手并没有就此停下。\
Her words weren't meant as praise, yet she can't help but return to the plate for another.

**蜂鸟**：演讲就要开始了。贝丽尔女士，或许我们可以之后再聊聊。\
**Hummingbird**: The professor is about to give his speech. If you don't mind, Madame Bouanich, might we continue our chat later?

老主顾回到了自己的餐桌，那一侧的客人们纷纷向此处致意，或许那儿是老主顾集会。\
He returns to his table. Guests around him greet him cordially, giving the whole event a sense of ritual familiarity.

**阿黛拉**：罗西那家伙，究竟在捣鼓些什么？\
**Adèle**: What on earth is Roseau up to?

**贝丽尔**：他有一个重大的好消息要宣布，事关他一生努力的成果。\
**Beryl**: He has an announcement to make, one that defines his life's work.

**贝丽尔**：你瞧，他已经换好了衣服。\
**Beryl**: Ah. It seems he's made himself presentable for the occasion.

**罗西教授**：各位同胞，今天我们聚集在此，只为了庆祝一个伟大的发现。\
**Professor Roseau**: Greetings, dear brethren. We gather here today to celebrate a momentous discovery.

**罗西教授**：一个属于神秘学家的伟大发现，人类注定无法窥探的秘密。\
**Professor Roseau**: One that belongs to arcanists alone. A breakthrough that lies far beyond the reach of human comprehension.

**刻薄的老妇人**：够了，不要再进行无意义的问候了。\
**Old Woman**: Enough with the self-aggrandizing. Get to the point.

**刻薄的老妇人**：我远道而来，绝不是为了欣赏你浮夸的演技，你找到的起死回生术呢？\
**Old Woman**: I didn't come all this way to watch you pump yourself full of hot air.

**罗西教授**：不必急着扮演不解风情的责问者，阿尼姆斯。我会讲的。\
**Professor Roseau**: There's no need to rush, is there, Animus? We have all the time we need.

**罗西教授**：自1999年之后，我们对被应许的世界的追寻就不曾停止。\
**Professor Roseau**: Since the year 1999, our search for the promised land has never ceased.

**罗西教授**：我们在引导之人的意志下不断揭露“暴雨”之后的奥秘。无数同胞为此献身，他们的生命化作种子，为我们带来丰收。\
**Professor Roseau**: Following the will of the Guiding One, we have unraveled countless mysteries of the "Storm." For this great cause, many of our noble comrades paid the greatest sacrifice, their souls sowing the seeds of our coming harvest.

**罗西教授**：这注定是条漫长的道路，但请想想吧，回到应许世界的形式难道只有“暴雨”？\
**Professor Roseau**: Our endeavor was never expected to be easy, but, tell me, has it ever crossed your minds whether the "Storm" is the sole path to the promised land we have collectively sought to bring about?

**罗西教授**：而且，在座的各位，包括我，难道我们理想中的应许世界都一致吗？难道不是只有基金会驯养的狗才会怀揣完全一致的思想？\
**Professor Roseau**: Further still, do all of us here, myself included, share in the same vision of that world? We are nothing like the Foundation's numb, obedient lapdogs incapable of independent thought, wouldn't you agree?

**罗西教授**：比起利用“暴雨”在注定有瑕疵的物质世界中挣扎，由迷思海将集体的理想化为现实，不是更可靠吗？\
**Professor Roseau**: The "Storm" promises only a change to our imperfect, superficial world. Yet I believe a transcendent world may be drawn up from the Depths of Myth—a world where each and every dream becomes reality. Tell me, which would you prefer?

**阿尼姆斯**：这是你第二次用这套说辞了。\
**Animus**: Same old song and dance.

**阿尼姆斯**：展示你的新成果，不然你什么都别想从我这儿得到。\
**Animus**: Perhaps you'd care to show something new and actually feasible, for once? Otherwise, you'll get naught from me.

**罗西教授**：你太急躁了，阿尼姆斯，我当然准备了新的内容。\
**Professor Roseau**: My dear Animus. Worry not, for I have come well-prepared to open your eyes.

**罗西教授**：我们发现了打开迷思海的方法，成功借此实现了一个奇迹，一个起死回生的奇迹！\
**Professor Roseau**: I have discovered a means to access the Depths of Myth, and, through it, achieved a miracle—the miracle of resurrection! Allow me to demonstrate.

教授在众人的目光中走向宴会厅的一角。\
The professor walks toward a corner of the banquet hall, holding rapt attention from the gathered diners.

反复取用着马卡龙的右手在投来的视线中停下，优雅地抓起餐巾。\
Her right hand, presently reaching for another macaron, stops mid-motion, deftly, automatically, switching to pick up a napkin instead.

**罗西教授**：当我们的灵与肉同时处于迷思海中时，肉体可能会消亡，会沉沦其中，会陨落，会被吞噬。\
**Professor Roseau**: When one's flesh and spirit are fully immersed in the Depths of Myth, their body frays and sinks until, eventually, it disintegrates.

**罗西教授**：但灵并不会消亡。在灵性的世界中，意识才是真正的物质。\
**Professor Roseau**: Yet the spirit remains intact. For in that realm, the spirit is itself the most authentic and pristine substance.

**罗西教授**：凡庸的现实不过是迷思海的降格，只要意识仍存在迷思海中，就能无数次归来。\
**Professor Roseau**: Reality as we know it is nothing more than a crude layer of degraded substance laid over the Depths of Myth. And so long as one's consciousness remains within its maelstrom, that person may be raised from it again!

**罗西教授**：费利西安就是意识能直接化为现实的最好证明！曾经肉体死亡的她，如今再次回到了这里！\
**Professor Roseau**: Our Félicienne here is the very proof that the mind alone may be brought back to physical reality! Though she perished, she now sits before us once more.

**罗西教授**：——让我们欢迎她以更纯粹的灵性姿态复生！\
**Professor Roseau**: So, one and all, let us raise a toast to her revival!

**阿黛拉**：怎么了，罗西？你究竟想表达什么？\
**Adèle**: Roseau? What in heaven's name are you trying to say?

她放下餐巾，站起了身。\
She sets down her napkin and rises from her seat.

**罗西教授**：哦，费利西安，你还没清醒过来吗？说点什么吧。\
**Professor Roseau**: Ah, Félicienne, you've fully rejoined us now, haven't you? Won't you please introduce yourself?

**阿黛拉**：难道你不知道我是谁？还要劳烦我来做自我介绍？\
**Adèle**: What do you expect me to say? You know very well who I am.

一旁的占卜师投来关注的目光，而那目光的焦点却不在宴会厅的任何一角。\
The diviner's eyes follow her, though the focus of her vision lies far beyond this hall.

**贝丽尔**：你还好吗？\
**Beryl**: How are you feeling?

**阿黛拉**：这是我的事，贝丽尔，如果你再像这样怜悯我，我会当作受到了侮辱。\
**Adèle**: I would feel a great deal better without your patronizing tone, madame. I have neither need nor want of your sympathy.

**阿黛拉**：咳哼。\
**Adèle**: Ahem.

她端起了桌上的红酒杯，举至胸前。\
She lifts a glass of red wine to her chest.

**“费利西安”**：我，费利西安，雷电的祭司，太阳王的宠臣，引导之人忠实的追随者。\
**"Félicienne"**: And here, before you now is Félicienne, Priestess of Lightning, advisor to the Sun King, vassal of the Guiding One.

**“费利西安”**：于此刻，宣布自己战胜了命运与死亡。\
**"Félicienne"**: Attend to my words: I have conquered fate and overcome death itself to stand here!

**“费利西安”**：我从迷思海中归来，只因为我是我，而不是罗西的那些失败的学徒。\
**"Félicienne"**: I arose from the Depths of Myth by my own power, unlike the poor, unworthy fools Roseau sent in.

**“费利西安”**：罗西的演讲似乎在说这是他的研究成果，真是恬不知耻。\
**"Félicienne"**: Yet he dares to claim this miraculous deed for his own. What a disgrace, sir. Have you no shame?

**“费利西安”**：你们总是这样，蒙受我和引导之人的恩惠却不自知，甚至引以为傲。\
**"Félicienne"**: But of course, you don't. All of you nonentities lack in both gratitude and shame. Basking in the grace of the Guiding One and myself, without even realizing it.

**“费利西安”**：难道你们不懂什么叫作谦逊？这等小偷行为，我真该赐死你，罗西。\
**"Félicienne"**: Did you think you had even scratched the surface of the power that dwells here? Roseau—you utter fool, this affront of yours ought to cost you your life.

**“费利西安”**：不过我慷慨又宽容，就放过你吧。\
**"Félicienne"**: Yet, I am not so base as to destroy what may still have use. So, just this once, I will forgive you.

**“费利西安”**：而且我也宽恕你们所有人未向我祝酒就用餐的无礼！\
**"Félicienne"**: As for the rest of you, my forgiveness likewise extends to the rudeness you all showed in stuffing your faces before toasting to my health.

**“费利西安”**：祝健康！\
**"Félicienne"**: Now, to my health!

**蜂鸟**：这……真是一项不可思议的奇迹。\
**Hummingbird**: This is a miracle!

**蜂鸟**：起死回生，这果然是能够实现的吗？\
**Hummingbird**: Bringing the dead back to life—it isn't really possible, is it?

**巨大玩偶**：引导之人的要求，起死回生术，这个怎么样？\
**Giant Puppet**: She came back to life? So we can't die anymore, like what the Guiding One said?

**阿尼姆斯**：胡闹。\
**Animus**: Pah. What a farce.

**阿尼姆斯**：你操控一个无关者的思想，让她相信自己是费利西安，还把这称为复生的奇迹？\
**Animus**: All you've done is manipulated some girl into believing she's Félicienne, and yet you dare to call it a "miraculous resurrection."

**阿尼姆斯**：真是亵渎了奇迹二字，我以后该用什么词去赞颂引导之人的伟业？\
**Animus**: What utter blasphemy! An offense to the word "miracle" and to the Guiding One Herself!

**小巧的女孩**：还有另一种声音……不属于费利西安的声音……\
**Petite Girl**: I heard another voice in Félicienne, one that belongs to someone else. Could that mean ...?

**冷淡的女性**：此时并无质疑的必要，稍后审问吧。\
**Distant Lady**: Why do we speak as if she is not present? Let us bring our concerns to her.

**冷淡的女性**：有些事必然只有真正的费利西安知晓。\
**Distant Lady**: There are things only the true Félicienne would know.

**蟹脸男**：精神化为物质？但若费利西安的神秘术无法归来，任何复生都毫无意义。\
**Crab-Faced Man**: Mind alone returning to reality? But has Félicienne lost her arcane skills in the process? If so, then this revival is meaningless.

**蜂鸟**：在我们找到足够优秀的炼金术师之前，这的确是炼制“不老泉”之外的一个合理的方向。\
**Hummingbird**: Whatever the case may be, if this is a true venue of life eternal, should we not seize it? At least until we find an alchemist capable of concocting the Fountain of Youth.

**蜂鸟**：但这个方法似乎仅限于迷思海内死亡的死者。也就是说，必须确保死者在迷思海里存有“母本”……\
**Hummingbird**: I believe I see one drawback already. Only one who dies in the Depths of Myth may be returned from it. To die elsewhere would be to lose the original image of one's being.

**蜂鸟**：也许我们可以在“暴雨”到来前，全面打开迷思海的缝隙，让整个时代的所有人都被储存进其中？\
**Hummingbird**: I imagine this is our shared goal then—to unleash the Depths of Myth upon the material world so that we might render a collective image of all who dwell in this era to be raised anew.

角落中微弱的声音打断了激烈的辩论。\
A demure and polite voice in the corner interrupts their debate.

**女性的画像**：伙伴们……我们是不是应该先庆祝费利西安的归来？\
**Portrait of a Woman**: But ought we not to first celebrate Félicienne's return?

**女性的画像**：哈哈，虽然她的变化真的很大。和之前“判若两人”……\
**Portrait of a Woman**: Though, I must say it is a strange sort of return. How different she looks, doesn't she?

**蟹脸男**：确实，新躯壳太过贫贱，与她的气质不合。\
**Crab-Faced Man**: True. This dowdy girl is a poor vessel for one so noble.

**“费利西安”**：这已经是我的身体了，注意你们的语气。\
**"Félicienne"**: Mind your tongues. You're speaking of my new body here.

**“费利西安”**：阿黛拉并不穷酸，她只是缺乏欣赏美的眼睛，我早就说了她不该做出租车司机。\
**"Félicienne"**: For all her faults, I would not call the girl "dowdy." She simply chose to turn a blind eye to beauty. I've always felt she picked the wrong career.

**“费利西安”**：虽然这确实锻炼了她察言观色和讨人欢心的能力。\
**"Félicienne"**: I admit it did her some good. She learned to read people and how to put them at ease.

**“费利西安”**：但也使她不像她的先祖，少了宝石猎人应有的审美。\
**"Félicienne"**: But it pulled her further from her true heritage and from the refined taste expected of a jewel hunter.

**女性的画像**：嘿，费利西安，你的右手还好吗？\
**Portrait of a Woman**: So, Félicienne, your right hand—is it alright?

**“费利西安”**：我好得很，怎么了？\
**"Félicienne"**: Whatever do you mean?

**女性的画像**：它正在颤抖……你怎么了？！\
**Portrait of a Woman**: Do you not feel it trembling? Damn! Is something wrong?!

超出了主人的控制，右手擅自将酒泼向了自己的面庞。\
Her right hand moves on its own, splashing the wine across her face before she can stop it.

**“费利西安”**：阿黛拉！你这无礼之徒！\
**"Félicienne"**: Uggh! Adèle, you insolent ...!

**阿黛拉**：嘶……呼！\
**Adèle**: *deep breath*

仿佛被凉水从睡梦中浇醒，她用力深呼吸后观察起周遭，然后惊觉。\
It's like being shocked awake by cold water. Her eyes freeze open as she scans the room.

身边是属于异形和怪人的动物园，而自己才是被观赏的动物。\
Around her sits a gawking zoo of monsters and aberrations, and she's the exhibit.

**阿黛拉**：你们……\
**Adèle**: You ...

**阿黛拉**：重塑之手！你们把我带到这儿想要做什么？\
**Adèle**: You're Manus Vindictae! Why did you bring me here? What are you doing to me?

她理解了自己的处境，突然的紧张感令她握紧手中的钻石，血和酒一同淌下指缝。\
Realization hits. Panic tightens in her chest; she clutches the diamond in her hand. Trickles of blood and wine seep through her fingers.

**阿黛拉**：……收起你们的神秘术！火渡船！还有歌唱家！\
**Adèle**: Stop! I will not accept any damage to my body, Ustrina! Nor from you, Lyra!

**阿黛拉**：再敢动一下我就把你们变成焦炭！\
**Adèle**: One move and I'll burn you to a crisp, inside and out!

**女性的画像**：费利西安……冷静些，这是为你办的宴会……\
**Portrait of a Woman**: What's happened, Félicienne? It is only us. We're still here at the banquet thrown in your honor.

**阿黛拉**：闭嘴，你这个储藏室！谁给了你开口的资格？\
**Adèle**: Stop your prattling, you rubbish dump! Another word and I'll rip that canvas to shreds!

**女性的画像**：呜……\
**Portrait of a Woman**: *sniff*

**巨大玩偶**：她好凶，她真的是费利西安。\
**Giant Puppet**: She's so angry. That means she has to really be Félicienne.

**阿黛拉**：真是感谢你的指认，假想敌。需不需要我指认下玩偶里面的人是你？\
**Adèle**: Words of wisdom from a puppet of all things. Need I point out who pulls your strings, Hypothetik?

**阿黛拉**：一群失败者、小孩，再加上快要死的老古董与白痴学者就想与我为敌？！\
**Adèle**: You cowards, ganging up on a poor innocent woman! Each and every one of you is a monster! I won't play whatever game you have in store for me!

**阿黛拉**：快给我把路让开！\
**Adèle**: Get out of my way!

**罗西教授**：在费利西安的意识进入合适的躯体后，旧意识仍会偶尔进行抵抗。\
**Professor Roseau**: Fascinating. Though Félicienne's spirit has seized control of her body, the former spirit seems able to resist.

**罗西教授**：导致二者的记忆与思考混合，表现出精神错乱。\
**Professor Roseau**: If I am indeed correct, what we are seeing is their thoughts and memories beginning to blend, causing this confusion.

一旁的教授拿着惯用的笔记本记录着面前的一切。\
The professor scribbles down notes in a rapturous flurry, recording every little tic, word, and movement.

**阿黛拉**：劳伦·罗西……你果然和重塑之手勾结！你在骗我，西莉亚说的都是真的！\
**Adèle**: Laurent Roseau, you've been in league with Manus Vindictae all along! You were lying to me! Everything Célia said was true!

她努力展示敌意，换来的却只有好奇与观察的视线。\
Adèle attempts a show of defiance, but all she receives in return are curious, observant stares.

**贝丽尔**：从这场宴会开始，没有人提过重塑之手这个名字。\
**Beryl**: My dear, no one here has mentioned Manus Vindictae but you.

**贝丽尔**：刚才被你叫到名字的人，有些完全没有做过自我介绍。\
**Beryl**: Yet you seem to know a great deal about those present already.

**贝丽尔**：但你却认识他们，了解他们的身份。\
**Beryl**: Far too much to be a mere guess. You have met these people before.

**阿黛拉**：休想再唬骗我，贝丽尔。西莉亚已经告诉了我一切……\
**Adèle**: I won't let you play with my mind again, Beryl. Célia told me all about these thugs. She told me everything!

她终于意识到了逻辑上的漏洞。\
Then it dawns on her. A flaw in her own reasoning.

**阿黛拉**：……也许西莉亚并没有说这么多……但她确实说了！是重塑之手杀了她！\
**Adèle**: Maybe not exactly everything. But she did tell me that it was Manus Vindictae that killed her!

**阿黛拉**：是罗西，还有费利西安，杀了她！你们都是危险的重塑之手……你们……\
**Adèle**: Roseau! Félicienne! You killed her! You-You murderous Manus scum!

**贝丽尔**：你应该面对真相。\
**Beryl**: I believe it is time you faced the truth.

**阿黛拉**：你又想说什么？我说了我不会再被你骗……\
**Adèle**: The "truth"? What is it this time? You think I don't see through you?

**贝丽尔**：你确实杀死了西莉亚。\
**Beryl**: You killed Célia.

**贝丽尔**：在意象宝库与现实的交叠之处，你亲手所为。\
**Beryl**: In that place where the Archive of Imagery overlapped with reality, you killed her by your own hand.

**阿黛拉**：什，么？\
**Adèle**: Wh-What?

**贝丽尔**：你又为何要为这真相愤怒呢？\
**Beryl**: You remember it, do you not? You allowed it to happen.

她开始思考，思考如何证明自己不是另一个人。\
She searches for any sort of proof she might have to match her claims.

或许根本不应该听进这些疯子的话语，直接用这双手撕开他们。\
She should never have listened to these lunatics. Maybe she should've just torn them apart with her bare hands.

从这个多嘴的女人开始，撕开一条道路，回到车上，然后离开，然后……\
Start with that woman. Tear open a path, get back to the car, drive off, and then ...

宴会以一场闹剧收尾，所幸宾客们都习以为常，迟来的服务生开始打扫现场。\
The banquet ends in chaos, though the guests hardly seem to take notice or seem to even care. A small band of waiters arrives to begin clearing the scene.

教授跨过破碎的玻璃与瓷片，来到贝丽尔的面前。\
The professor steps over the shards of glass and porcelain to where Beryl sits.

**罗西教授**：费利西安可真是大闹了一场，我们的同胞在这时却总爱当旁观者。\
**Professor Roseau**: Félicienne has quite the flair for the dramatics, doesn't she? And as always, our audience simply sat back, their eyes glued and mouths agape.

**罗西教授**：还好您的预言从不出错。\
**Professor Roseau**: We are indeed fortunate for your skill in divination.

**罗西教授**：等到费利西安醒来，我们就按照之前的计划行动。\
**Professor Roseau**: We will have to wait for Félicienne to return to her senses, but thereafter we follow the plan as discussed:

**罗西教授**：用法兰西之蓝作为迷思的起点，呼唤出真正完美的，由人群选出的巴黎。\
**Professor Roseau**: Using the French Blue as our focal point, we will draw up the true, perfect Paris from the Depths of Myth.

**罗西教授**：那个没有被任何外力干涉，存在于所有人理想中的巴黎！\
**Professor Roseau**: Democratic, independent, chosen by her people, and shaped by the dreams of every one of her citizens.

**贝丽尔**：在这座城里，一切都有可能。我甚至见过巴黎在燃烧呢。\
**Beryl**: I have seen many versions of Paris, from flames to paradise. Nothing is beyond possibility.

贝丽尔只回应了一句不着边际的答复。她始终望着餐厅敞开的大门，然后没有再说话。\
Beryl offers a vague, distant reply; she looks out toward the open doors but says nothing more.

教授瞥了一眼贝丽尔握在手中的灵摆，猜测她又陷入了某种占卜带来的恍惚，没有再多打扰她。\
The professor holds his stare on the pendulum in Beryl's hand, guessing she's once again trapped in a trance, and leaves her be.

预言是一项令人崇敬，也令人敬而远之的能力。\
Prophecy is something to be revered and feared.

**罗西教授**：一旦明天的太阳升起，我们就去埃菲尔铁塔进行最后的仪式。\
**Professor Roseau**: So, tomorrow at dawn, we will perform the final ritual atop the Eiffel Tower.

## AFF-15 巴黎遥远 / Paris Out of Reach

**罢工群众Ⅰ**：我们要求的是自由、平等，以及博爱！那些政客们允诺却不曾给我们的东西！\
**Protester I**: Liberty, equality, fraternity! Deliver what was promised!

**罢工群众Ⅱ**：让他们知道！我们的要求是什么！\
**Protester II**: Hear our voice! Respect our demands!

**罢工群众Ⅲ**：八小时工作制！涨工资！带薪假！\
**Protester III**: Eight-hour workdays! Better wages! Paid vacations!

**罢工群众Ⅳ**：我们要食物！\
**Protester IV**: No more hunger!

**罢工群众Ⅰ**：巴士底狱吓不倒我们，国王与皇后今天就要做出答复！总工会必须得到他们的权力！\
**Protester I**: We will not let the Bastille frighten us! Let the king and queen answer! Give power to the people!

**热沃当的野兽**：——\
**Beast of Gévaudan**: *roar*

**罢工群众Ⅱ**：让他们滚出凡尔赛！到巴黎来看看这一切！\
**Protester II**: Drive them out of Versailles! Bring them here to Paris!

**罢工群众Ⅲ**：自由！或死亡——呃啊！！\
**Protester III**: Liberty or death! Ah!

野兽的怒吼声混杂在错乱的口号中，不时有惨叫与撕咬声传出。\
The beast's roar mingles with the chaotic chants. Screams of death and horrific brutality echo through the streets.

但只要仍有一人站着，这场戏剧狂欢般的游行就不会终止。\
But as long as one person still stands, this grotesque carnival of protest will not end.

**罢工群众Ⅳ**：自由！或死亡！！\
**Protester IV**: Liberty or death!

蔓延整个巴黎的癔症，似乎已经演变成混乱不堪的闹剧。\
Hysteria has spread across Paris, twisting the city of lights into a bedlam—into utter chaos.

而三名毫不在意的人从旁经过，尖叫声如同他们的伴奏。\
Three people pass through the turmoil, unbothered by the screams around them.

**“费利西安”**：我赐予你渴望的青春，你献给我钻石的项链～\
**"Félicienne"**: You longed for youth, and I gave it freely, so you tied a diamond around my neck.

**“费利西安”**：话语随口而出，千万莫为虚妄～\
**"Félicienne"**: Honeyed words, your false embrace, bound me in a cage.

**罗西教授**：你看上去心情不错，费利西安。\
**Professor Roseau**: What a surprise! The great Félicienne seems in better spirits now.

**“费利西安”**：所有可贵的，都深埋地下～\
**"Félicienne"**: And all we once shared was sealed in silence.

**“费利西安”**：将你的献礼，锁入盒中～\
**"Félicienne"**: Locked in a box, far below the earth.

**罗西教授**：现在的场合并不适合这首歌，费利西安。\
**Professor Roseau**: Though, I feel this isn't the time or place for such a song, miss.

费利西安停下了把玩着钻石的动作，将鄙夷的视线投向一旁。\
Félicienne stops fiddling with the diamond and casts a disdainful glance toward her increasingly insufferable toady.

**“费利西安”**：阿黛拉就没有你这么不识趣，她不会在我唱歌时打断我。\
**"Félicienne"**: Tsk, Adèle would never interrupt me the way you did.

**“费利西安”**：可惜她不认识这首歌……\
**"Félicienne"**: What a shame she never heard this song.

**“费利西安”**：既然你想聊正事，那就聊吧。\
**"Félicienne"**: But you wish to speak business, yes? Then, let us talk.

**“费利西安”**：这么多次“暴雨”过去，你们让引导之人的意志传播到了哪儿？\
**"Félicienne"**: First, answer me this: why has there been near on no progress in passing on the Guiding One's teachings, despite the many changes in era?

**“费利西安”**：你忽略了最为重要之事，将至高的恩赐浪费在自己的求知欲上。\
**"Félicienne"**: You've elected to ignore your most sacred duty, throwing aside her benevolent instructions in favor of your pursuit of "knowledge."

**“费利西安”**：离开了我，你们这群废物就堕落成了这样。\
**"Félicienne"**: Without my leadership to inspire you, this organization is about as useful as a chocolate teapot, it seems!

**罗西教授**：只要等我解开迷思海的奥秘，一切问题都会得到解决。\
**Professor Roseau**: Please, miss, all these problems will be solved once I unravel the deepest secrets of the Depths of Myth.

**“费利西安”**：在以前，像你这样高谈空想的骗术师，会被我家佣人用扫帚打出去。\
**"Félicienne"**: Look at you still clinging to that old drivel. Did I not already expose your worthlessness? I'd have had you swept out by the servants in my day.

**罗西教授**：你是从迷思海中归来的人，难道你不相信我的研究吗？\
**Professor Roseau**: But you're living proof of my thesis! You came back from the Depths of Myth. How can you not believe?

**“费利西安”**：没有人在乎你所谓的“心中巴黎”。\
**"Félicienne"**: What I believe in is my ability to conquer death. I have no particular interest in your imaginary Paris.

**“费利西安”**：如果不是为了起死回生术，你以为其他人会来听你大谈理想？\
**"Félicienne"**: Nor your babbling nonsense about "ideals."

**罗西教授**：我们的目的难道不就是回到那真正的时代？现在捷径就在眼前了，相信我吧。\
**Professor Roseau**: It is our shared goal to return the world to its most glorious era, isn't it? We've found the means; I only ask that you trust me.

**“费利西安”**：登上埃菲尔铁塔，用我的钻石完成最后的仪式彻底打开迷思海。\
**"Félicienne"**: Trust? You'd have me scale the Eiffel Tower of all things to use my diamond to unleash the Depths of Myth ...

**“费利西安”**：而你只在一旁记录，这就是你的捷径？\
**"Félicienne"**: While you stand at a safe distance and watch? That's your brilliant plan?

**罗西教授**：是的，我们之前都错了，迷思海并不在地下。\
**Professor Roseau**: I admit we made a mistake, miss, but I've discovered the truth: the Depths of Myth don't lie below, but above.

**罗西教授**：高处象征着升华，这正是文明自古的迷思。\
**Professor Roseau**: Altitude represents ascension—a primordial image as old as civilization itself.

**罗西教授**：所以我们应该到高处去，如果我的理论正确，巴黎乃至世界都会露出他们的另一面貌。\
**Professor Roseau**: That is why you must reach the peak of the city's tallest structure. There, all of Paris—perhaps even the entire world—will transcend, if my theory proves correct.

**“费利西安”**：没有人要你说明你的理论……与你合作真是最无趣的事。\
**"Félicienne"**: Theories, theories, theories ... Ugh! What torture it is to listen to you.

**“费利西安”**：还有你，贝丽尔，你打算盯着我到什么时候？\
**"Félicienne"**: And what of you, madame? Why are you staring at me like that?

**“费利西安”**：你的视线令我犯恶心，立刻给我挪开。\
**"Félicienne"**: Your gaze is nauseating. Stop it.

一直沉默的女士仍保持着没有焦点的注视。\
The silent woman's eyes are vacant and neutral.

**“费利西安”**：你到底有没有听我说话？\
**"Félicienne"**: Are you even listening to me?

**贝丽尔**：我在听。\
**Beryl**: I am.

她的回答也轻微而缥缈。\
Her reply comes faint, barely more than a whisper.

**“费利西安”**：……哼。\
**"Félicienne"**: Hmph.

三人巧妙地避开罢工群众，继续向着战神广场走去。\
The three weave past the protestors, heading toward the Champ de Mars.

没有人注意到贝丽尔手中的灵摆正在闪光。\
Not a single passerby seems to take notice of the glow coming from Beryl's pendulum.

车辆停泊的街道寂静无声。\
The car is parked on a silent street.

**阿黛拉**：我该怎么说呢……她总唱些我没听过的歌，所以我很难开口评价。\
**Adèle**: I never really understood any of the songs she sang; that's why I didn't bother to say anything.

**阿黛拉**：她的声调是很优美，我猜她一定有个有名的声乐老师。\
**Adèle**: But I could tell she had a beautiful voice—the kind any singer would envy.

驾驶座上的年轻女子垂下眼睛，看向手中的精致小盒。\
In the driver's seat, the young woman lowers her gaze to the ornate little box in her hands.

**阿黛拉**：她喜欢甜品，尤其是马卡龙，一天能吃掉一整盒。\
**Adèle**: She has a real sweet tooth, particularly for macarons. I've seen her eat a whole box in one go.

**阿黛拉**：而且她很挑剔，只愿意吃拉杜丽。所以我得经常绕路去香榭丽舍大街……\
**Adèle**: But not just any old macarons. Only Ladurée's will do. I often had to plan our trips around the store on the Champs-Élysées.

**阿黛拉**：那家店太早根本不开门，幸亏费利西安每天起床也很晚，不然那一路上我的油门都要踩冒烟了。\
**Adèle**: Lucky for me, Félicienne was a late riser, or else I'd have had to race all the way from the bakery to her place every morning.

她轻笑一声，无力地扯动嘴角。\
A weak smile tugs at her lips.

**阿黛拉**：但她吃的并不是马卡龙，对吗？\
**Adèle**: But what she was eating ... they weren't macarons, were they?

油纸衬上原本整齐码放的甜品变成了另一副模样。\
Inside, the once neatly arranged pastries have taken on another shape.

幼龙乖巧地躺在四方的小盒中，双眼紧闭。\
The little dragon lies within the box, its eyes closed.

它的身体被精细地切成了方便食用的大小，内馅从缺口处淌出，散发着诱人的甜美香气。\
Carved and cut into bite-sized pieces, filling oozes out from its little form, releasing a sweet, alluring scent.

**阿黛拉**：告诉我，贝丽尔女士……她究竟对我做了什么？\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, please, tell me. What did she do to me?

司机将幼龙的碎片仔细放进口袋里，疑问中有一丝难以察觉的颤抖。\
Adèle gathers her dragon's fragments into her pocket. Her voice trembling beneath her confusion.

**贝丽尔**：她窃取了你的命运。\
**Beryl**: She stole your fate.

**贝丽尔**：真正的她早已消融在迷思海深处，你遇到的不过是来自过去的一缕残影。\
**Beryl**: Her original self perished long ago within the Depths of Myth. The spirit that found you was only a remnant, a mere shadow clinging to a world in which she no longer belonged.

**贝丽尔**：但它同样渴盼着生的希望，因此依附于生者，汲取留存在阳光下的养分。\
**Beryl**: She longs to live again, even if it is only as a parasite.

**阿黛拉**：……所有那些记忆，都只是幻觉的一部分？\
**Adèle**: What about those memories we shared? Were they all just illusions?

**贝丽尔**：可能是费利西安与你交汇后产生的经历，也可能只是你们共同拥有的一段虚假记忆。\
**Beryl**: Some were true experiences you shared as your streams of fate merged; others were but fabrications.

**贝丽尔**：我无法断言，因为我没有看过这部分。\
**Beryl**: The nuance can be difficult to discern without careful observation.

司机沉默了半晌，再一次把手放在门把手上。\
Adèle stays silent for a long while before reaching for the handle again. The door doesn't move. She's been trying in vain for quite some time.

那扇门纹丝未动，她已持续了这样徒劳的努力许久。

**阿黛拉**：贝丽尔女士，我不明白。你究竟站在哪一边？\
**Adèle**: You've really confused me, madame. What side are you on?

**贝丽尔**：哪一边都不是。命运不偏袒任何一方，我能做的只是观看。\
**Beryl**: I am a watcher of the streams of fate, not a participator in them. I take no sides.

**阿黛拉**：可你不是已经都知道了吗？你告诉我，前方注定有牺牲……西莉亚已经死了！\
**Adèle**: But you can do more than watch! You already have! You were the one that told me about this inevitable death, and then, Célia really did end up dead!

**阿黛拉**：我即将遭遇什么、发生什么……这对你来说，不是早就十分清楚了吗？\
**Adèle**: You know exactly what's going to happen to me. You know everything, don't you?

司机的声音哽咽了。窗外，巴黎遥远地闪烁着。\
Her voice catches. Outside, the lights of Paris flicker erratically.

**贝丽尔**：我并非全知，阿黛拉小姐。\
**Beryl**: It is not nearly as simple as you might imagine, Adèle.

**贝丽尔**：一般我只是远远地看上一眼。只要知道结局和转折点，我就会跳过一些无关紧要的过程和前述。\
**Beryl**: To observe a stream is to see only its curves and eddies—the ripples of importance. I see the path, but not every moment along it.

**贝丽尔**：通常情况下，这并不影响命运的准确。\
**Beryl**: That is itself sufficient for me to ascertain one's eventual fate. There are rarely any exceptions.

**阿黛拉**：……在这之中从无例外？\
**Adèle**: You said "rarely," so there are exceptions?

**贝丽尔**：哦，是有这么一个人的。我对你说起过她。\
**Beryl**: An exception, yes. I told you about her, did I not?

**贝丽尔**：那时我决定仔细地沿着属于自己的水流前行，将它探查清楚……\
**Beryl**: I had been drifting along the streams of fate,

**贝丽尔**：于是我看见了那个与我相似的女孩儿，有一部分她源于我。这真奇妙。\
**Beryl**: when I saw a girl who resembled me—who in some part came from me. It was quite a revelation.

**贝丽尔**：先于她的出生，我就见到了我们的水流将在何处汇聚。我知道我会给她起名玛蒂尔达。\
**Beryl**: I saw where our streams merged long before she was born, and I knew I would name her Matilda—

**贝丽尔**：她将天赋异禀，她会变得善良且勇敢，她将表现得十分优秀。\
**Beryl**: That she would grow up to be kind, brave, and truly gifted.

**贝丽尔**：我沿着河流看到了她的终点，然后我挪开目光，不再关注流经她的一切。\
**Beryl**: I followed her through every turn and every ripple to the very end. Then, I looked away. I stopped watching.

占卜师简单地为叙述收尾。\
The diviner ends the story in her always even tone.

**阿黛拉**：这听起来很奇怪，甚至有些残酷……\
**Adèle**: The way you describe it ... It sounds strange, madame. A-Almost cruel.

**阿黛拉**：就像是……你为她还没有做过的事而忽视当下的她。\
**Adèle**: As if you've ignored her in the present because you're afraid of her future.

**贝丽尔**：我认真地看过了属于她的一生。这不够吗？\
**Beryl**: I studied the entirety of her stream. Every moment of her fate. It seemed enough.

车窗倒映出贝丽尔困惑的神情。\
The car window reflects the puzzled look on her face.

**贝丽尔**：不过，后来发生了一件有趣的事。\
**Beryl**: But then something peculiar happened.

**贝丽尔**：在1999年，那场雨落下后，我不再能像过去那样看清水流的去向。\
**Beryl**: In the final moments of this millennium, there was a certain kind of rain. Since that time, the streams of fate have lost their clarity.

**贝丽尔**：它们时而模糊，时而忽然中断，时而被搅乱成漩涡……\
**Beryl**: At times they are muddied, at others interrupted—twisted into vortexes.

**贝丽尔**：河道的走向开始变化，一切也随之混沌。\
**Beryl**: As they began to shift, so too did everything else.

**贝丽尔**：我曾见过的命运改变了。\
**Beryl**: The fates I had seen had taken a new form. Nothing was the same.

占卜师看向阿黛拉。\
She turns toward Adèle.

**贝丽尔**：很快罗西先生的仪式就会由费利西安完成。\
**Beryl**: Soon, Félicienne will complete Roseau's ritual.

**贝丽尔**：那之后，你的精神会在这辆车里永眠，一场灾难会降临巴黎。\
**Beryl**: Once that happens, your spirit will rest forever here in this car, and a calamity will fall upon Paris.

**贝丽尔**：我看到的“光景”，到此为止。\
**Beryl**: All the "visions" I saw end here.

**阿黛拉**：你是在提示我吗……？\
**Adèle**: You're implying something, aren't you?

**阿黛拉**：提示我这场命运仍可以改变？\
**Adèle**: Are you saying that my fate isn't set in stone?

**贝丽尔**：我只是说出了我见到的。\
**Beryl**: I am simply stating what I saw.

**贝丽尔**：有人在得知一切后不再行动，期待能避开原定的命运。有人则被激起抗争的勇气，最后只加倍落入陷阱。如何解读“预言”，只取决于你自己。\
**Beryl**: Many who learn of their fates become passive to them, hoping that by inaction, they might avoid their consequences. Others are driven to attempt, however vainly, to change it. How you interpret this prophecy is entirely up to you.

阿黛拉怀疑地注视着贝丽尔，没能读到任何额外的内容。\
Adèle examines her warily, but if there's anything being hidden from her, she can't detect it behind those glassy eyes.

**阿黛拉**：……我能从这辆车里出去吗？\
**Adèle**: Then there's still a chance for me to leave this car, right?

**贝丽尔**：这是你最坚固的精神港湾。一旦你离开，想从混合的河道中找回你自己的水流……\
**Beryl**: This is a spiritual haven. A place which belongs to you alone. Once you leave ...

**贝丽尔**：那么你可能会成功，但也可能迎来比永眠更糟的结局。\
**Beryl**: You may find salvation hidden within the currents or a fate far worse than death.

**阿黛拉**：我不需要知道这些。\
**Adèle**: *sigh* I don't want to know what lies in wait for me.

**阿黛拉**：我答应了西莉亚要把那钻石毁掉。我已经失约了一次，不能再失约第二次。\
**Adèle**: What I want is to get out of here and destroy the diamond, just as I promised. I won't fail again.

**阿黛拉**：你肯定有办法让我出去，是吗？不然你就不会出现在这里！\
**Adèle**: You know a way to let me out, no? You wouldn't be here otherwise.

**阿黛拉**：告诉我，贝丽尔！\
**Adèle**: Please, madame! Tell me!

**阿黛拉**：我不知道你究竟想看到什么……但如果我在这里放弃，你也什么都看不到了！\
**Adèle**: Whatever future you're hoping to see, it will never happen if I give up now!

她握紧了拳头，对准车窗。如果没有得到满意的答复，她就只有用最简单的手段毁掉这个笼子。\
She clenches her fist, ready to shatter the window if no answer comes.

直到现在，她仍不知道占卜师怀有怎样的目的。她既无法理解，也没有时间。\
Even now, she doesn't know what Beryl truly wants. She doesn't understand and has no time to attempt to.

这时，占卜师的笑容褪去了，取而代之的是她未曾见过的表情。\
Then, the diviner's smile fades, replaced by something unfamiliar.

那似乎是被冲淡的悲伤，也许更多是见惯失败后的乏味。\
It's a diluted kind of sorrow, perhaps just the weariness of someone used to failure.

**贝丽尔**：你已经知道了一切。如果仍然要去的话……\
**Beryl**: Even in the face of oblivion, you would try to change your fate.

副驾驶席上的乘客探出身，按下了对方的拳头，随后另一只手扶到门上，轻轻将其推开。\
She leans forward, presses down Adèle's fist, and gently opens the door.

**贝丽尔**：那就去吧。\
**Beryl**: Go then.

在对方惊讶的视线中，贝丽尔为司机撑住了车门。\
Beryl holds it there, steady, meeting Adèle's startled eyes.

**阿黛拉**：……谢谢您。\
**Adèle**: Thank you.

门外依旧是一片纯然的白色，巴黎依旧遥远。\
Outside, the lights of the city seem blindingly white, as near and as distant as the sun.

她突然感到一阵轻松。为自己的一无所见。\
A strange calm washes over her, despite seeing nothing at all.

**阿黛拉**：再见，贝丽尔女士。\
**Adèle**: I'll see you around, Madame Bouanich.

她迈入了那片纯白之中。\
She steps into the white.

**贝丽尔**：……\
**Beryl**: ...

副驾驶席上的乘客望着这一幕，闭上了眼睛。\
Beryl closes her eyes.

更为久远的一片碎屑在她的眼前重合。\
She recalls something from long ago.

**费利西安**：怎么样，看见你总在念叨的“命运”了吗？\
**Félicienne**: So, where is this so-called "fate" you've been waiting for?

**费利西安**：要是看不明白就算了。反正我会一切顺利。\
**Félicienne**: You've seen the end already, haven't you? The only one possible, anyway: my triumph.

**费利西安**：预言家？呵呵，我家曾经养过的那群预言家们，谁也没预见到那场革命！\
**Félicienne**: You prophets are all the same. Hah! My family bankrolled a dozen frauds like you, yet not one ever foresaw the Revolution.

**费利西安**：有这样的工夫，你还不如去多花心思考虑引导之人的指示……\
**Félicienne**: You ought to have dedicated yourself to the Guiding One instead.

贝丽尔竖起一根手指抵在费利西安的嘴唇前，提醒趾高气扬的同僚保持安静。\
Beryl raises a finger to Félicienne's lips, shushing her arrogant colleague.

**贝丽尔**：你的问题是，你想知道该怎样更好地完成那个任务，对吗？\
**Beryl**: You speak because you seek my direction.

**贝丽尔**：寻找起死回生的奥秘？\
**Beryl**: You wish to unravel the secrets of resurrection.

**费利西安**：没错。有几个门徒带回了某种传言，所谓起死回生的奇迹之术。\
**Félicienne**: You're clever for a prophet. Of course that's my goal. I wouldn't allow those bungling followers to take credit for such a discovery.

**费利西安**：我要去搞清楚是怎么回事，免得其他人抢先。\
**Félicienne**: I must determine the truth before anyone else.

**贝丽尔**：……那么，你要往北去。\
**Beryl**: North. That is where your path leads.

**贝丽尔**：但向北走很危险。你会得到你想要的，你也将不再是你。\
**Beryl**: But know that there are consequences to what you seek. You will not emerge from it the same.

**费利西安**：哼，你只需要告诉我，我要的东西在哪儿。\
**Félicienne**: Hmph, spare me the theatrics. I shan't be intimidated. You've pointed the way; I have no more need of you.

**费利西安**：结果如何不取决于命运，而是取决于我。\
**Félicienne**: Whatever consequences lie ahead depend on me, on my actions. Not some puddle of "fate."

**费利西安**：再见了，全知全能的贝丽尔小姐。\
**Félicienne**: Goodbye, madame. Let us see what the "All-Seeing Lady" has seen for us.

贝丽尔注视着她的身影。\
Beryl watches her silhouette.

穿过长廊，迈出门扉，这身影消失在门口刺眼的日光里。\
It passes through the corridor, out the door, vanishing into the blinding daylight.

**贝丽尔**：再见，阿黛拉小姐。我很期待。\
**Beryl**: Goodbye, Adèle. I look forward to seeing what comes of your actions.

**贝丽尔**：期待像你们这样的人，能证明我是错的。\
**Beryl**: To seeing another prove me wrong.

## AFF-16 应许的时刻 / Moment of Revelation

她在这片白中奔跑许久，不知道自己要寻找什么，也不知道终点在何处。\
She runs through the endless white, not knowing what she's searching for, nor where the path will end.

**阿黛拉**：河道……水流……这里没有飞鸟也没有植物。我该用寻水术去找吗？\
**Adèle**: Streams of fate ... But how can I find them? Dowsing might be a little on the nose.

**阿黛拉**：该死，在车里时她明明只和我隔了一条街！\
**Adèle**: Damn! She was just steps away from me when I was in the car!

脚步愈发沉重，但她不曾停下，直到“巴黎”出现在她面前。\
Her steps grow heavy, but she doesn't stop, until "Paris" appears before her.

**阿黛拉**：那是，什么……？\
**Adèle**: Wh-What's that?

一座城市突破云层倒映在天空中，所有人与野兽都在这一刻驻足，仰望起头顶永无止境的巴黎记忆。\
A city pierces the clouds, mirrored in the sky. People and beasts alike stop to stare up at the mirrored double above her.

**罗西教授**：看呐，这如果不是奇迹，那还有什么能算是奇迹？\
**Professor Roseau**: How spectacular! If this isn't a miracle, then I must ask what else could possibly qualify as one?

**罗西教授**：历史学家会嘲笑这座城市的时代错乱吧，建筑师会鄙视这座城市的规划排布吧。\
**Professor Roseau**: Let dusty historians scoff and rivals sneer! But there are none who would dare scorn this timeless, flawless vision of Parisian beauty across the ages!

**罗西教授**：但谁能否认这荒唐的空中城市就是巴黎？\
**Professor Roseau**: Who from this lofty perch would deny this is the truest form of Paris?

**罗西教授**：世博会馆、埃菲尔铁塔、凯旋门、圣母院、路易十五广场的方尖碑、吕特斯竞技场，还有那老旧的中世纪街区。\
**Professor Roseau**: The Palace of Optics, the Eiffel Tower, the Arc de Triomphe, Notre-Dame, the Luxor Obelisk, the Lutetia Arena, the medieval quarters—each piece woven together in perfect harmony!

**罗西教授**：思维才会构成现实，这座由世人意象构成的巴黎，才是真正的巴黎！\
**Professor Roseau**: As I've said, thought shapes reality. This Paris—born from collective imagination—is Paris at its most true and most real!

**罗西教授**：等到它完全降下！我们才能拥有真正的世界与生命！\
**Professor Roseau**: Only when it fully descends shall we finally possess a real world—a life worth living!

一人正在拥抱天空，一人正手握仪式的关键，最后一人仍沉默不语。\
One embraces the sky. One holds the key to the ritual. The last remains silent.

**“费利西安”**：罗西，你就不能安静一些？\
**"Félicienne"**: Must you hang over me like this, Roseau?

**“费利西安”**：如何，贝丽尔，你当时看到了这一幕吗？\
**"Félicienne"**: And you, madame, did you foresee this?

**“费利西安”**：现在整个巴黎的命运都被我捏在手中，而且我还是我，你的预言完全错了。\
**"Félicienne"**: The fate of Paris now rests in my hands, and yet I remain myself. What a pity it must be for you.

**贝丽尔**：……\
**Beryl**: ...

**“费利西安”**：哼，没有话说了？\
**"Félicienne"**: Hmph, no more tricks?

**阿黛拉**：那地之上的，终将等同那天之下的……所以这就是贝丽尔说的灾难。\
**Adèle**: "What lies below shall reflect what lies above"? So, this is what will befall Paris?

她朝着眼前的费利西安伸出手，指尖却穿过了对方。\
She reaches toward Félicienne, but her hand passes straight through her.

**阿黛拉**：果然碰不到……\
**Adèle**: I can't touch her.

她开始尝试各种方法，攻击，施展神秘术，掐自己的手臂，直到白色的光芒闪过。\
She tries everything—attacking, casting arcane skills, pinching her own arm—until a flash of white swallows her entirely.

**贝丽尔**：你回来了。\
**Beryl**: You have returned.

**阿黛拉**：什么？\
**Adèle**: What?!

**贝丽尔**：回过神来，她已经回到了出租车内。\
When she blinks, she's back inside the taxi.

**阿黛拉**：……我怎么又……回来了？\
**Adèle**: H-How am I back in here?

**贝丽尔**：你失败了。但你还能回到这里，说明你还可以去寻找道路。\
**Beryl**: You failed to take back your body. So long as you return here, though, there is still a chance.

**阿黛拉**：我刚才已经站到费利西安旁边了，但连她的头发丝都碰不到！\
**Adèle**: I found Félicienne! She—I was right next to her, but I couldn't reach her no matter how I tried!

**贝丽尔**：那么，你可以留在这里享受最后的时光，一边回忆过去一边等待仪式结束。\
**Beryl**: Then give up, and accept this as your final resting place.

**阿黛拉**：不可能。就算是为了西莉亚，我也一定要烧掉那颗钻石。\
**Adèle**: No, I won't sit here and do nothing. I will destroy that diamond. I must, for Célia.

**阿黛拉**：可我到底要怎么才能碰到她……\
**Adèle**: But how am I supposed to reach Félicienne?

**阿黛拉**：等等……为什么我需要碰到“她”？\
**Adèle**: Wait. I don't really need to reach her, do I?

**贝丽尔**：回到驾驶座的司机猛抬起头，她似乎想起了什么。\
She snaps upright, remembering.

**阿黛拉**：贝丽尔女士，你说过我和费利西安是交汇的水流。\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, you said before that the stream of my fate merged with Félicienne's.

**阿黛拉**：也就是说，不论如何，她都与我在一起，是吗？\
**Adèle**: So, in a sense, she and I are always together, right?

**贝丽尔**：她的手指掠过口袋中幼龙的脊背，然后是光滑的切面、无力的尾尖。\
Her fingers brush the dragon's spine in her pocket—the smooth cut, the limp tail tip.

**阿黛拉**：我根本不需要找到“她”。也不需要找到“自己”。她就是我……我就是她！\
**Adèle**: Then I don't need to "find her" nor even "find myself." Because she is me, and I am her!

**贝丽尔**：正如你所想的那样。\
**Beryl**: You have begun to understand.

**贝丽尔**：她会附着在你的躯体上，是因为你们的灵足够相似。\
**Beryl**: She only had the means to claim your body because your spirits are closely intertwined.

**贝丽尔**：而肉体的任何影响都会同时施加给你们双方，其中脆弱的一方未必承受得住。\
**Beryl**: Any impact to your body affects both souls. Though the weaker of the two spirits often cannot endure the strain.

**阿黛拉**：你说了“未必”。也就是说你根本没有预见到结果。\
**Adèle**: "Often," but not never, no? So even you can't see what comes next.

**阿黛拉**：你并不知道我和费利西安谁才是赢家！\
**Adèle**: You don't know whether Félicienne or I will win this fight!

**贝丽尔**：司机紧盯着无动于衷的占卜师。她抓住了机会——她找到了这个至关重要的漏洞。\
She locks eyes with the impartial diviner. And then she sees it—the flaw, the crack in the illusion.

而占卜师回望了她。那双眼睛少见地映出了跃动的火光。\
Beryl meets her gaze. For once, real fire flickers in those crystalline eyes.

**贝丽尔**：从抗拒到接受，你一直在试着找出方法推翻所谓的“命运”。\
**Beryl**: The currents of fate will bend to your actions. You will steer its course rather than be swept away.

**贝丽尔**：正是为了见证这一刻，我才始终注视着你的故事。\
**Beryl**: You have never once yielded before destiny, and that is precisely why I have followed you from the beginning.

此时此刻，她不再像是一块平静而无动于衷的、折射所有光彩的水晶了。\
She no longer looks detached and polished, no longer like a crystal reflecting every light but her own.

她的目光终于落在了当下的世界里。\
The diviner finally descends to the world as it is.

**贝丽尔**：——你会不会就是那个能成功的例外？\
**Beryl**: It is as you say. I do not know if you'll emerge victorious in this final trial.

**贝丽尔**：——你能向我证明吗？\
**Beryl**: Will you carry this through for me?

**阿黛拉**：既然你押注在我身上，就别问无聊的问题。\
**Adèle**: Do you even need to ask?

**贝丽尔**：散落的碎块被手指紧紧捏合，开始和她的心跳一同搏动。\
The fragments in her hand pulse in time with her heartbeat.

**阿黛拉**：好了，费利西安，如果你能听到的话，这就是塔沃尼尔家的诅咒了。\
**Adèle**: So, Félicienne. Time for you to experience the Tavernier family curse.

幼龙从口袋里探出头来，鼻息中开始冒出火舌。\
Her marvelous little dragon pokes its head from her pocket, sparks flaring from its nostrils.

**阿黛拉**：如果你与我的命运真的交织在一起，那么我也祝你，同样在赢得一切时遭遇不测。\
**Adèle**: If our fates are truly entwined, then this curse must bind your soul as well as mine. And in true Tavernier fashion, your end will come just as you lay hands on the treasure you desire most.

仪式的进展非常顺利，空中的巴黎逐渐靠近地上的巴黎，双方的埃菲尔铁塔即将交错。\
The ritual proceeds moment by moment as the Paris above them begins drawing closer to the ground, the twin Eiffel Towers nearing collision.

异样的闪光从钻石中流出，仿佛在牵引着二者靠近。\
Unnatural light emits brightly from the diamond, drawing the two worlds together.

**罗西教授**：太棒了！费利西安！只要再一会儿，人们意识中的巴黎就会降临现实！\
**Professor Roseau**: Incredible, Félicienne! Just a little longer, and Paris, as it should be, born from the collective unconscious, will descend into reality!

**罗西教授**：那真正的巴黎，每个人心中魂牵梦绕的巴黎，而不是这垃圾一般的现实！\
**Professor Roseau**: The true Paris—not like the garbage heap below us!

砰——\
*bang*

子弹擦过了钻石，费利西安下意识用手将其护住。空中的倒影在一瞬间变得稀薄。\
A bullet grazes the diamond. Félicienne instinctively shields it with her hand. The mirrored city above begins to fade.

**罗西教授**：西莉亚？你竟然回来了？\
**Professor Roseau**: Célia? How did you get here? How are you still alive?

教授的助手如今用枪指着他，但她身影稀薄，与空中的倒影并无区别。\
The professor's assistant stands with a gun aimed at him, but her outline wavers, ghost-like, just like the reflection above them.

**西莉亚**：我听见阿黛拉在叫我。\
**Célia**: Adèle called out to me.

**罗西教授**：有趣，你的灵应该已经被费利西安消灭了才对，感谢你印证了我的另一个猜想。\
**Professor Roseau**: Fascinating. Truly fascinating! Your soul should've been erased by Félicienne. I must thank you once again, my most brilliant student. Your existence confirms another of my theories:

**罗西教授**：迷思海不只能实现起死回生，或许死亡在迷思海也只是一种可剥离的迷思！\
**Professor Roseau**: The Depths of Myth promises more than just resurrection, but an end to death itself!

**“费利西安”**：呵，阿黛拉的朋友真是和她一样欠缺思考。\
**"Félicienne"**: Heh, a friend of Adèle's? No doubt you're as tactless as she was.

**“费利西安”**：你想阻止我？那就请吧。\
**"Félicienne"**: You intend to stop me? Be my guest.

她将手中的钻石端到左侧的胸口，正在心脏前。\
She lifts the diamond to her chest, right before her heart.

**“费利西安”**：我宽大地给予你这个机会。\
**"Félicienne"**: Go on. You should be grateful I've given you the opportunity.

**“费利西安”**：无论是打中我，还是钻石，你都可以阻止仪式，请吧。\
**"Félicienne"**: Whether you hit me or the diamond, you'll stop the ritual. Go on.

**西莉亚**：你用阿黛拉的身体威胁我？没有用的。\
**Célia**: You really think threatening Adèle's body will intimidate me? It won't work.

但她的手开始颤抖，她害怕自己打偏，害怕自己不小心真的打中。\
Her hand trembles. She fears missing the shot or, worse, hitting true.

**“费利西安”**：想想阿黛拉这时会怎么说吧，她一定会叫你开枪的。\
**"Félicienne"**: Yet, is that hesitation I see? Think about what our dear Adèle would say at a time like this—"pull the trigger." Sounds like her, doesn't it?

**西莉亚**：闭嘴、闭嘴！\
**Célia**: Shut up! Shut up!

**“费利西安”**：我说错了吗？还是说你和阿黛拉并不熟？\
**"Félicienne"**: My, my, have I said something wrong? Or perhaps you don't know Adèle as well as you thought.

**“费利西安”**：那我就展示一下慈悲，告诉你阿黛拉在这种时候会怎么想吧。\
**"Félicienne"**: Here, let me show you in a more vivid manner.

占据了阿黛拉身体的女性单手撑住歪过的头，像是要把脑中的思想抖出来。\
The woman inhabiting Adèle's body tilts her head with one hand, as if shaking loose her thoughts.

**“费利西安”**：“不用管我，开枪就是了，把我和费利西安一起干掉。”\
**"Félicienne"**: Don't worry about me. Just shoot. Take us both out. It's what you have to do.

**“费利西安”**：“这或许是破解塔沃尼尔诅咒的唯一办法呢？用我的死亡去成就冒险的结局。”\
**"Félicienne"**: It's the only way to break my family curse. You have to end the adventure with my death.

**“费利西安”**：“只要我死在终点之前，就不会迎来最后的凄凉末路，不是吗？”\
**"Félicienne"**: To fall at the height of a brilliant journey. That's better than fading into some bleak, ordinary end, no?

**“费利西安”**：“不过你放心，西莉亚，我不会需要你来成就我的死。”\
**"Félicienne"**: No, Célia. You don't need to do this! I'll end this myself.

**“费利西安”&西莉亚**：什么？\
**"Félicienne" & Célia**: Huh?!

拙劣的戏剧迎来一句意料之外的台词，演出者和观看者都对此感到震惊。\
An unexpected line is delivered in the clumsy play, stunning both the actress and her audience.

同时沉睡的龙从口袋中醒来。\
And at that moment, the sleeping dragon awakens in her pocket.

**费利西安**：啊——\
**Félicienne**: Aaagghh!

**费利西安**：这愚蠢的龙，居然要烧死自己的主人？！\
**Félicienne**: You irritating little lizard, how dare you harm your own master?!

**费利西安**：阿黛拉！看看你养的宠物！\
**Félicienne**: Damn you, Adèle! You and your wretched pet!

火焰的灼烧换来意识的清醒，混沌的记忆因痛楚来袭而消失。\
Flame sears through the haze, pain burning away the chaos of her memory.

只烧灼虚妄的高温为身体带回了上一任主人，它逐渐回到熟悉的动作习惯。\
The scorching heat, purging all illusion, returns the body to its rightful owner, finally allowing her to move freely.

**阿黛拉**：所以这就是灵魂被灼烧的感觉……我死后绝对不要下地狱。\
**Adèle**: So this is what it feels like for a soul to be scorched. I finally understand why so many fear hell.

**费利西安**：阿黛拉！你这蠢材！想和我一起死吗？快让你的宠物停下！\
**Félicienne**: Adèle, you fool! Tell your pet to stop at once! Do you wish to die with me?

**阿黛拉**：我确实也不想死，费利西安。不如你把钻石扔掉，我就只烧了钻石，怎么样？\
**Adèle**: No, I don't. Not right now, Félicienne. So why don't you drop the diamond?

**阿黛拉**：不过我很了解你，你的回答我心知肚明……\
**Adèle**: I can already guess your response.

**阿黛拉&费利西安**：把梦话留到梦里吧！这是我的法兰西之蓝，死亡也不能令我放弃它！\
**Adèle & Félicienne**: You keep dreaming! This diamond belongs to me! Not even death can steal it from me!

**阿黛拉**：呵，听听这永不放弃的精神，你真是个优秀的宝石猎人。\
**Adèle**: Heh, listen to you. You'd make an excellent Tavernier.

费利西安的怒骂声不曾中断，握着钻石的左手也不曾松开，火焰逐渐蔓延至全身。\
Félicienne's anger only grows, her left hand clutching the diamond tighter still as the flames crawl further up her body inch by inch.

**阿黛拉**：——现在来看看谁才是真货吧，费利西安！\
**Adèle**: Now let's see if fire can separate true from false, Félicienne!

## AFF-17 不必再会 / No Need for Promises

教授添加了最后一行记录，随即合上笔记本，伸手向外套之下摸索。\
The professor writes one last line, snaps his notebook shut, and reaches under his coat.

他找到了自己最信任的伙伴，“保护者”转轮手枪。\
His fingers grip his oldest friend—a "Le Protector" revolver.

**罗西教授**：阿黛拉的人格没有被覆盖，甚至重新夺回了肉体的控制权。\
**Professor Roseau**: Then Adèle's personality wasn't entirely consumed. She's managed to regain control of her body.

**罗西教授**：即使自负如费利西安，其个人意识的强度也与其他人无异，研究方向果然应该专注于呼唤集体的潜意识。\
**Professor Roseau**: Even a spirit as strong-willed as Félicienne lacks the ability to completely dominate another. Hmm, perhaps I was wrong to shift focus from the power of the collective unconscious.

**贝丽尔**：不必心急，罗西先生。\
**Beryl**: There is no need for that, Professor.

占卜者的精神也已落回躯体之中。\
Her spirit returns.

她抬起手，轻轻推开了瞄准阿黛拉的枪口。\
She raises her hand and nudges the barrel away from Adèle.

**贝丽尔**：即使你现在开枪，结局也不会改变。因为你并不是那枚能够阻碍水流的石子。\
**Beryl**: Even were you to interfere, the outcome would remain unchanged. You are but a pebble in the course of the stream of fate.

**贝丽尔**：我们不妨稍作等待。或许事情会迎来意想不到的变化。\
**Beryl**: Wait with me a little longer. Things may just take an unexpected turn.

**罗西教授**：……你看见了什么？\
**Professor Roseau**: You saw something, didn't you?

**贝丽尔**：恰恰相反，我阻止您，正是因为我突然“看不见”了。\
**Beryl**: Quite the contrary, I see nothing, and that is what fascinates me most of all.

**费利西安**：你被解雇了！阿黛拉！\
**Félicienne**: You're fired, Adèle!

**费利西安**：你这成天扮演英雄的小丑……不要命的疯子！\
**Félicienne**: You reckless, foolish would-be Joan of Arc!

费利西安的身形剧烈地晃了晃。失去了可以依附的躯壳，她就只是一个飘荡而出的游魂，一道影子。\
Félicienne's form convulses violently. Without a vessel to cling to, she's nothing but a drifting soul—a shadow.

一个被赶下舞台的失败者。\
A failed actress, dragged offstage.

**阿黛拉**：多谢你的夸奖。\
**Adèle**: That's almost flattering.

**阿黛拉**：比起你对西莉亚做的，这根本不算什么。\
**Adèle**: But this is nothing compared to what you did to Célia.

她捡起在挣扎中滚落的钻石。\
She picks up the diamond that rolled away during the struggle.

**西莉亚**：阿黛拉，快！快烧掉它——\
**Célia**: Adèle, hurry! Turn your fire on the diamond.

**费利西安**：闭嘴！\
**Félicienne**: Silence!

**西莉亚**：呃……\
**Célia**: Ugh ...

西莉亚的影像更加单薄，费利西安扬起手，她的轮廓便融化、消散。\
Her figure flickers as Félicienne lifts her hand. Then, with only a twist of her wrist, Célia's outline melts away.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安，住手！\
**Adèle**: Stop this, Félicienne!

来不及确认西莉亚的状况，她握紧了手中的蓝钻。\
There's no time to check on her friend. Instead, she grips the blue diamond so hard she imagines it could break.

唯有真实存留，一切虚假的化为灰烬。\
Only the real remains. All falsehood will burn away to ash.

这场荒诞不堪的闹剧终于可以落幕。\
This charade must finally be put to rest.

**阿黛拉**：唯以真知——\
**Adèle**: By fire, what is false—

**费利西安**：呵。\
**Félicienne**: Heh.

**阿黛拉**：——！\
**Adèle**: ...!

**费利西安**：你这令人作呕的蠢货、厚颜无耻的骗子——你想把一切都推到我身上？\
**Félicienne**: You disgusting hypocrite! Don't you dare wag that finger at me!

**费利西安**：你骗得了任何人，但你骗不过我——我比任何人都了解你。包括你那自欺欺人的底色……\
**Félicienne**: You may fool everyone else, but not me. I know you better than anyone. I know your true colors!

**费利西安**：你一生中最光荣的事就是能被我认作同类。阿黛拉！\
**Félicienne**: Deny it all you want, but our souls are entwined, because deep down, you and I are just alike! Take pride in it, girl! Hosting me will be your greatest achievement!

**费利西安**：你早就知道那些信都是西莉亚写的，还要装作不知情的样子对她提起！\
**Félicienne**: Be honest, now! No need to play pretend as you did with Célia. All that time, you let her keep writing those letters, knowing full well that your parents were long dead. How wickedly false indeed!

你早就知道你的父母已经过世，却默许了她出于好心玩这过家家酒的游戏……

**阿黛拉**：不……我只是……\
**Adèle**: N-No ... I just ...

冰冷的手指逐渐收紧，生者与死者的界限变得模糊不清。\
Cold fingers tighten, blurring the line between the living and the dead.

**费利西安**：看到她憧憬那些冒险，你既哀伤又愤怒……一个结局注定不幸的诅咒，又有什么好羡慕的呢？因此失去双亲的人又不是她……\
**Félicienne**: She shared her deepest hopes and dreams with you through those make-believe adventures. But you ignored them. What's there to envy about a cursed bloodline?

**费利西安**：可如果没有西莉亚的这份憧憬，你的生活还剩下什么？一个随波逐流的出租车司机？这真的是你想做的吗？\
**Félicienne**: Hmph. I suppose you kept her as a salve to your dreary, miserable life. You really thought you could fool the world into thinking taxi driving was your highest ambition? Deep down you've always craved more.

**阿黛拉**：咳……你少自以为是了……！\
**Adèle**: *cough* Don't act like ... you know me ...

她拼命汲取着所剩无几的空气，从喉咙里挤出一句反驳。\
She gasps for breath, forcing out a strained protest.

**费利西安**：自以为是？我什么都清楚——我比你更清楚你脑子里那点念头！\
**Félicienne**: But I do know you! I know each and every one of your wicked thoughts better than you do!

**费利西安**：西莉亚让你烧掉宝石，她把你强行拖进这片混乱。你惊慌失措，却也暗自期待——因为你将不费任何力气，以一个全然受害者的模样获得这一切！\
**Félicienne**: She told you to burn the diamond, but you ... you secretly desired it! You craved your place in this adventure—your death!

**费利西安**：谁也不会为你开启了“诅咒”而埋怨你，就像你埋怨你的父母那样！\
**Félicienne**: Who could blame you for "triggering the curse"? You weren't chasing treasure—not by choice. Not like your parents.

**费利西安**：你只是被卷入了，不会有任何人因你的冒险受到伤害，甚至你还要扮演一个拯救者……哈。\
**Félicienne**: All of this to pretend you were "unwillingly" caught up in this adventure. You even get to play the savior, haha!

**费利西安**：你那天真无邪的青梅竹马，扮演一个公主真是再合适不过了！那么，怎么能没有加害者呢？\
**Félicienne**: And, oh, how your dear little friend fits the role of a damsel in distress. All you need is a villain.

**费利西安**：于是我出现在了那里，如你所愿。一如最初。\
**Félicienne**: And that's where I came in, just as you wished.

**费利西安**：——全巴黎有这么多人，为什么独独是我出现在你身边？你想过这个问题吗？\
**Félicienne**: Of all people in Paris, why did I come to you? Have you given it even the slightest thought?

肌肉与骨骼在她狠狠收拢的手掌下挤压、摩擦、变形。\
Muscle and bone grind and twist beneath her crushing grip.

**费利西安**：承认吧，阿黛拉！是你期望我对西莉亚出手，是你想要杀了她！\
**Félicienne**: Admit it, Adèle! You wanted me to hurt Célia! You wanted to kill her!

阿黛拉拼命地转过头，她切实地看到了西莉亚满脸惊愕。\
Adèle uses all her strength to turn toward Célia's face, finding it frozen in shock.

**阿黛拉**：咳……这只是、谎……\
**Adèle**: *cough* You're ... lying ...

**费利西安**：啊，谎话。对，她也向你撒谎了，阿黛拉。\
**Félicienne**: Ah, yes, lies. She lied to you too, Adèle.

**费利西安**：你们真是相称的好友，一对互相掩饰的小骗子……\
**Félicienne**: You really are a perfect duo—two little liars keeping secrets from one another.

**费利西安**：她没告诉你，烧掉这颗钻石，我和她——这两个麻烦，就会一起消失得干干净净。\
**Félicienne**: Allow me to reveal another secret. Destroying this diamond will bring an end to more than just me. It will end her as well.

**费利西安**：你也会得到轻松和自由。\
**Félicienne**: Though perhaps, without her, you might at last be free.

**阿黛拉**：你说……谎……\
**Adèle**: That's not ... true ...

她再一次望向西莉亚，只得到听了无数遍的请求。\
She looks at Célia again and hears the same plea she's heard a hundred times before.

**西莉亚**：别听她的，阿黛拉！迷思海不能彻底打开！\
**Célia**: Don't listen to her, Adèle! You must destroy the diamond! The Depths of Myth must not be unleashed!

立刻把宝石烧掉！

**费利西安**：是看这座城市毁掉，还是再一次送你的朋友去死？塔沃尼尔的大英雄？\
**Félicienne**: Lose your friend or lose the city—what will it be, Ms. Tavernier?

**费利西安**：我可不会给你做选择的机会，因为我还不想死呢。\
**Félicienne**: What am I saying? I have no intention of giving you the chance to decide. I'm not about to die again.

为了更好地欣赏阿黛拉窒息的痛苦，她稍稍低下头。\
She lowers her head for no other reason than to indulge in her suffering.

于是，她得到了一个歪歪扭扭的笑容与狠命咬紧的牙齿。\
But what she sees instead is a crooked smile with teeth clenched in defiance.

**费利西安**：啊！该死——\
**Félicienne**: Argh! Damn it!

Félicienne recoils, shoving Adèle away.\
Adèle, anticipating the next play perfectly, rolls twice and lands on her feet.

**旁白**：在几近本能的撕咬之下，她反射性地松开手，将阿黛拉狠狠推远。\
**旁白**：而后者早有准备。两三个翻滚后，阿黛拉站直了身子。

**阿黛拉**：真巧、我也……还……不想死！\
**Adèle**: Funny that. I'm not ready to die either.

她没有再望向西莉亚。那双焦急的眼睛比能检验真伪的火焰更加灼人。\
She doesn't look back at Célia. Those anxious eyes burn hotter than any flame of truth.

属于“费利西安”的外壳剥落殆尽，毫无先兆的巨大暗影于这个瞬间显现在铁塔的尖端。\
The shell of "Félicienne" peels away completely, and without warning, a massive shadow takes form at the tip of the Eiffel Tower.

**"Félicienne"**: I won't let you get away!

**“费利西安”**：别想摆脱我。

**罗西教授**：再等下去，她就要把那枚钥匙毁掉了，贝丽尔。\
**Professor Roseau**: She's going to destroy the key, Beryl.

**罗西教授**：如果你不能拿出一个足够好的理由，三秒钟后，我立刻开枪。\
**Professor Roseau**: If I don't intervene, all I've worked for will come to nothing. Give me one good reason I shouldn't shoot.

**贝丽尔**：“意象宝库”的裂口从未合上，罗西先生。\
**Beryl**: The rift of the Archive of Imagery has shown no signs of closing, Professor.

**贝丽尔**：再抬头看看吧。\
**Beryl**: Look up again. Watch closely.

劳伦·罗西抬起头，空中的城市越来越近，边缘的建筑正逐渐延伸到地平线边缘。\
Laurent Roseau lifts his head. The city in the sky drifts closer, its edge scraping the horizon.

**贝丽尔**：钻石只是将裂缝撕扯得更大、更壮观，加快它泄露的进程。\
**Beryl**: The diamond has already served its purpose. It has torn the rift open; the Depths of Myth is trickling down over us as we speak.

而我们都有足够的时间……

**贝丽尔**：不如看看这枚小石头在她手上会有怎样的效果。\
**Beryl**: Let's see what more the little gemstone can do in her hands.

阿黛拉注视着手中的蓝钻，用指腹抹去其上的血迹。\
Adèle wipes the blood from the blue diamond with her thumb.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

在做出最终的决定前，她还要确认一件事。\
Before she decides, she has to be sure of one thing.

**阿黛拉**：西莉亚，你说过等研究成果出版之后，就用稿费送我一条“好运项链”……\
**Adèle**: Célia, you said you'd buy me a good-luck necklace after you publish your paper.

**阿黛拉**：还有机会吗？\
**Adèle**: Will you keep that promise?

她低着头。被冲淡的血水从她脸上滴落到那枚钻石上。\
She lowers her head. Blood diluted with tears and sweat runs down her face, dripping onto the diamond.

**西莉亚**：你真过分，阿黛拉。\
**Célia**: You're too cruel, Adèle.

**西莉亚**：应该早点告诉我……这样我就不用挤时间偷偷写那些信啦。\
**Célia**: Why didn't you just tell me? I wouldn't have had to write all those silly letters.

一个有点难看的、艰难挤出的笑容浮现在她脸上。\
A strained, awkward smile twists her lips.

**阿黛拉**：……我们还会再见面吗？\
**Adèle**: Will I see-see you again?

**西莉亚**：可能……\
**Célia**: I'm not sure.

她的目光扫到一旁昏迷的费利西安。时间不多了。\
Her eyes land on Félicienne, unconscious beside her. Time is running out.

最终，西莉亚上前一步。\
At last, Célia steps forward.

像小时候玩耍那样，她的手掌覆上阿黛拉的手掌，帮助对方握紧了拳头。\
Like when they were children, she places her hand over Adèle's, helping her close her fist.

**西莉亚**：死者复活只是一个传说。\
**Célia**: The art of resurrection is elusive and unknown.

**西莉亚**：没人知道烧毁宝石之后会发生什么，那些……都只是猜测。\
**Célia**: I don't know what will happen after the diamond is destroyed. What Félicienne said—it was just speculation.

**西莉亚**：就是现在了。做决定吧，阿黛拉。\
**Célia**: There's no more time, Adèle. Make your decision, now.

阿黛拉听着这番话，迟迟没有动作。几次尝试后，她艰难地开口了。\
Adèle listens, motionless. After a few failed attempts, she forces out the words.

**阿黛拉**：费利西安是对的。我是个狡猾的骗子、自欺欺人的蠢货。\
**Adèle**: You know what? Félicienne was right. I am a foolish, pathetic hypocrite.

**阿黛拉**：可她有一点说错了。\
**Adèle**: But she still doesn't know all that much.

她终于调整好了呼吸。接下来的句子几近不受控制地涌出。\
She steadies her breath, but her next sentences spill out without any filter.

**阿黛拉**：你不需要谁的拯救……你才是真正的冒险家。\
**Adèle**: You were never the damsel in distress. No, you're the hero, the adventurer.

**阿黛拉**：至关重要的线索来自你，最先踏上这场冒险的也是你。你比我更有资格站在这里……\
**Adèle**: You were the one who uncovered all the clues. You were the first to embark on this journey.

**阿黛拉**：你比我更像塔沃尼尔。\
**Adèle**: You're more of a Tavernier than I'll ever be, Cici.

**西莉亚**：……\
**Célia**: ...

握住阿黛拉的那只手紧了紧。如同此前的许多次对话，西莉亚有点无奈地轻轻叹了一口气。随后，阿黛拉听到好友笑了笑。\
The hand holding Adèle's tightens once more. Célia sighs softly, helplessly. Then Adèle hears her laugh.

**西莉亚**：不是的，阿黛拉。那不重要。\
**Célia**: Don't be silly, Adèle. That never mattered to me.

**西莉亚**：我对塔沃尼尔家的事迹感兴趣，只是因为你。因为你是我的朋友。\
**Célia**: It wasn't the tales of gemstones or adventures that drew me to the Tavernier family. It was you.

**阿黛拉**：……我？\
**Adèle**: Huh ... Me?

**西莉亚**：从小到大，你总能在关键时刻做出选择，从没有后悔过……\
**Célia**: You've always been so driven and sure of yourself. Even when we were kids, you never hesitated, never looked back.

**西莉亚**：我也想学会像你那样活着，阿黛拉。\
**Célia**: I wish I could live without regrets like you do.

西莉亚的笑容轻易地撕碎了那颗颤抖的心。\
That laugh tears through her trembling heart.

但它总要跳动下去，带着一些难以弥合的痕迹。\
But it keeps beating—scarred, but alive.

**西莉亚**：你总是从不后悔，你应该那样。\
**Célia**: Stay that way, Adèle, just as you are.

她把那几个字眼咬得很重。像一个郑重的约定，或者要求。\
She bites out the words like an oath or a demand.

**西莉亚**：好吧，可能……最后只是有些遗憾。但你现在动摇的话，我会失望的。\
**Célia**: Well, maybe not completely without regrets. That's asking the impossible. But if you hesitate now, I'll be disappointed.

西莉亚露出最后一个笑容。\
Célia smiles one last time.

**西莉亚**：做你想做的吧，我伟大的冒险家。\
**Célia**: So go on. Follow your heart, my dear friend.

**西莉亚**：我相信你。\
**Célia**: I believe in you.

她拍了拍阿黛拉的肩膀，而后松开了手。\
She pats Adèle's shoulder and lets go.

**阿黛拉**：……\
**Adèle**: ...

声音消退了。呼吸也随之退去。唯有心脏仍在震颤。\
The sound fades. So does her breath. Only the heartbeat remains.

一切的等待、煎熬、追逐与挣扎都已至尾声。\
All the waiting, torment, pursuit, and struggle have come to an end. Every ounce of hope, hatred, sorrow, and forgiveness has been poured out.

期望、仇恨、悲痛与谅解都已被倾吐殆尽。\
She has no other choice.

她别无选择。

**阿黛拉**：唯以真知炼化虚妄。\
**Adèle**: By fire, what is false is purged.

燃烧的火焰只是一种变化时产生的现象，此刻却要揭露实在之物的真相。\
Flame is just another means of transformation, but now it must expose what's real.

无论何种伪装，都会在这种剧变中显露出本质，质与量应当在此刻产生变化。\
Whatever the disguise, their true natures are revealed. As both substance and form change.

火焰自下而上，掠过整颗法兰西之蓝。阿黛拉感到手中一沉，那枚被意象侵蚀、化为法兰西之蓝的烟晶出现在她的手中。\
The consuming flames surge upward, devouring the French Blue. Adèle feels her hand grow heavy, as a familiar smoky quartz reappears in her palm.

然而法兰西之蓝并未消失，手中的一枚宝石变成了两枚，意象离开了物质，却没有回归来时的世界。\
But the French Blue doesn't vanish. The single gem becomes two. Image and matter part ways, yet neither returns to its origin.

**阿黛拉**：怎么……\
**Adèle**: How ...?

**阿黛拉**：为什么它还在……？\
**Adèle**: How can it still be here?

**阿黛拉**：——唯以真知炼化虚妄！\
**Adèle**: By fire, what is false is purged!

在火光之中，虚假的破灭，真实的存留。\
In the blaze, falsehood crumbles and truth remains.

这枚纯粹的、略显透明的蓝钻，在不灭中证明了自己无可抵挡的真实。\
The translucent blue diamond endures, proving its unshakeable reality.

**阿黛拉**：“热沃当的野兽”会被焚烧，连费利西安也会！\
**Adèle**: I burned the Beasts of Gévaudan; I even burned Félicienne.

**阿黛拉**：它也来自那片潜意识海洋——凭什么它能毫发无损？！\
**Adèle**: So why can't I burn this diamond? It is from the Depths of Myth, isn't it?

**西莉亚**：这不应该……它明明只是一个象征……\
**Célia**: Surely it can't survive your fire. It isn't possible. It's only a symbol.

**贝丽尔**：正因为它是纯粹的象征。\
**Beryl**: A primordial symbol, yes. That is precisely why it survives.

占卜师肯定了她的措辞。\
The diviner affirms her words.

**贝丽尔**：它是实在的意象，世人的记忆构成了它，就好像一幅画作。\
**Beryl**: The French Blue is both abstract and concrete, an iconic symbol held deep in the collective imagination of our society.

**贝丽尔**：不论有多少赝品与模仿者，画中的宝石都会永远享有独属于它的名字。\
**Beryl**: No matter how many imitations or counterfeits may exist, none will ever take its place.

**贝丽尔**：不会劣化，没有任何杂质，永远保持纯粹。因而也不会被烧毁，得以永久地留存。\
**Beryl**: It is eternally transcendent—unconditionally pure. Its existence can never truly be destroyed.

**贝丽尔**：你做得很好，阿黛拉。\
**Beryl**: You have done all you can, Adèle. Bravo.

阿黛拉困惑地听着这句赞赏。她分明什么也没能改变。\
Adèle listens, confused. She's changed nothing, and yet she's praised.

天上的巴黎仍在降下，两座埃菲尔铁塔的尖端已经开始交错。\
Paris continues to descend. The twin Eiffel Towers crossing at their tips.

犹如一架梯子被逐渐收起，天与地的差距正在弥合。\
Like a ladder folding away, heaven and earth draw closer.

而西莉亚与费利西安的形影都愈发趋于透明，被风一缕缕切削，消散。\
Célia and Félicienne grow transparent, stripped away by the wind.

**阿黛拉**：我没能毁掉钻石，可是她们……\
**Adèle**: But I failed to destroy the diamond. Célia and Félicienne are ...

她无法再说下去。她看到了贝丽尔的微笑。

她无法再说下去。她看到了贝丽尔的微笑。\
Adèle can't go on, but she sees Beryl's smile.

在故事的最初，在占卜沙龙之中，贝丽尔朝着她——此时此刻的她，露出的笑容。\
The same smile she gave her long ago in that divination salon—the version of her in that moment, smiling now.

**贝丽尔**：正如我所见的那样，人们在命运中挣扎，无数水珠在此汇聚，终于变成了滚滚向前的洪流。\
**Beryl**: Countless streams converge and intertwine here in this moment. An unstoppable downpour is coming.

**贝丽尔**：而你是其中格外倔强的一滴水珠，你的挣扎得到了回应。\
**Beryl**: And in it, you are a remarkably stalwart droplet. Your struggle has at last reached its conclusion.

**贝丽尔**：我想……那洪流将要落下了。\
**Beryl**: The rain ... It is about to fall.

## AFF-18 雨 / Rain

毫无半点犹豫，阿黛拉快步奔向西莉亚，试图扶稳好友。\
Without hesitation, Adèle rushes to Célia, trying to steady her friend.

后者虚弱地摇了摇头，制止她徒劳的努力。\
Célia weakly shakes her head, stopping her.

**西莉亚**：……\
**Célia**: ...

占卜师的视线越过了众人，投向逐渐昏沉的天幕。\
The diviner looks past everyone, toward the darkening sky.

**贝丽尔**：没有用。这只是必然。\
**Beryl**: Just as it was meant to be.

**阿黛拉**：……您在说什么？\
**Adèle**: What?

**阿黛拉**：这究竟是怎么回事？您打算告诉我，眼前的这一切……\
**Adèle**: This ridiculous sight ... This distorted "Paris" ...

她也笑了。然后将视线投向塔下的世界。\
She smiles too, then lowers her gaze to the world below the tower.

游行中的野兽穿上奇装异服，再次伪装起人类，罢工游行化为了狂欢节。\
The beasts below have donned new costumes, masquerading as humans. The strike becomes like a carnival parade.

又接连有人从巷子和建筑中走出，披上野兽与人的外衣，加入这场狂猎。\
More figures pour out from the alleys and buildings, half-beast, half-human, joining the wild hunt.

**阿黛拉**：整座城市乱七八糟，巴士底柱变成比尔博凯特玩具，维尔特-加朗广场的石雕被换成一只滑稽的龙虾……而我的朋友正在消失。\
**Adèle**: The July Column just turned into a bilboquet, the Vert-Galant statue replaced with some bizarre lobster, and my friend is disappearing before my eyes.

**阿黛拉**：您要说这些都是注定的命运？！\
**Adèle**: And you're telling me that all this was meant to happen?!

**阿黛拉**：如此可笑……如此荒谬，毫无意义……\
**Adèle**: It's all so-so meaningless, hah, so absurd.

**贝丽尔**：是吗？\
**Beryl**: Is it?

某个词语触动了贝丽尔，她从恍惚中回过神。\
A single word pulls Beryl from her trance.

**贝丽尔**：啊……对。是这样。我要感谢你，阿黛拉。\
**Beryl**: Hm. Perhaps you are right, Adèle. Thank you for showing me what I could not see.

**贝丽尔**：我得到了答案。所谓的命运现在只是一团荒谬的、混乱的、发了疯的东西。\
**Beryl**: Fate, destiny—it has become nothing more than an absurdity. A tangled mess.

**贝丽尔**：这场“暴雨”本不该到来的。\
**Beryl**: This "Storm" should never have come to pass.

**阿黛拉**：“暴雨”……？\
**Adèle**: "Storm"?

她茫然地重复，望向四周。\
She repeats the word faintly, glancing around.

虚弱到吐不出哪怕一个字的西莉亚，昏迷的费利西安，静静注视着她们的贝丽尔。\
Célia, too weak to speak; Félicienne, still unconscious; and Beryl—watching them both in silence.

众人皆已疲惫不堪，舞台上仅剩下一位狂喜的演员。\
Everyone is spent. Only one delirious actor remains on the stage.

**罗西教授**：这场雨……不在我们的预测里……\
**Professor Roseau**: This "Storm" is quite the delightful surprise!

**罗西教授**：“癔症”在发生变化……它们变得更一致了……\
**Professor Roseau**: Look at this mass hysteria. It's becoming ever more unified!

**罗西教授**：有什么在“统一”并“修正”它们……\
**Professor Roseau**: As if some force—some will—is drawing them together, controlling them.

他踉跄了一步，在笔记本上写下最后一笔。\
He stumbles, penning the last stroke in his notebook.

**罗西教授**：原来如此！原来如此！就像一个自由演出的剧场，现在已经发展到不得不更换幕布的时候——\
**Professor Roseau**: Yes! Yes, I see it clearly now! The world is a stage—a performance with no script—and we have arrived at the moment when the curtain must fall and the scene must shift!

**罗西教授**：而本不存在的剧变加快了时代的动荡！\
**Professor Roseau**: This upheaval—this shift we've ushered in—has been intensifying the turmoil of the era!

**罗西教授**：只要用同样的方式，只需要稍加推动，只是点一把火而已！\
**Professor Roseau**: What a marvelous device! It's just the spark we need to ignite a cleansing fire.

**罗西教授**：“暴雨”可以被我们操纵——它可以被提前引发！\
**Professor Roseau**: With this power, we can manipulate the appearance of the "Storm" as we please!

**罗西教授**：而这些癔症，是的，物质世界不过是精神的臆想，所有的变化都来源于演员们的集体潜意识……\
**Professor Roseau**: The changes to the mass hysteria ... Yes, it's all obvious now. They were born from the collective subconscious. We are mere actors on this stage! For the material world is nothing but a projection of the mind!

**罗西教授**：哈哈哈……哈哈！\
**Professor Roseau**: Hahaha ... Hahahahahaha!

**罗西教授**：所有的话语不过是对旧作的引用，对生命的爱也不过是演员的职业道德！这出连编剧都没有的戏剧，所演出的不过是众人的自我幻想！\
**Professor Roseau**: Their dialogues are but borrowed lines from ancient scripts! Their passion—their love for life—an oblivious repetition of the same narratives! The play has no script yet tells the same story! This material world—it is nothing more than a flicker on a cave wall!

**罗西教授**：这才是世界的真相——连至高规律都要掩饰这一点！\
**Professor Roseau**: I've seen it—the ultimate truth! The truth that even the transcendental Law feigns to hide!

**罗西教授**：却是我发现了……哈哈哈！却是我发现了……\
**Professor Roseau**: But I've seen it now, hahahaha! I've seen it!

**罗西教授**：迷思海会被修正，一如世界所有的错误……可谁说错误不是正确？正确只是一个连绵不绝的错误……\
**Professor Roseau**: The Depths of Myth itself will also be corrected, just as all the errors of the reality. But who decided which of these errors are "wrong" to begin with? Or perhaps, what is "right" is essentially an endlessly repeated chain of errors?! Hahaha ...!

劳伦·罗西几乎要把后仰的腰给折断。空中的建筑折射着他眼中欣喜若狂的光彩。\
Laurent Roseau bends backward, so sharply it seems as if he would snap in two. The reflected light of the sky-city shimmering in a reflection of his manic joy.

贝丽尔看向他，神情中多少掺杂有一点儿怜悯。\
Beryl looks at him. Pity flickering across her tired face.

**阿黛拉**：他怎么回事……？\
**Adèle**: What's wrong with him?

**贝丽尔**：罗西先生只是正被他毕生追求的事物吸引。或者，你可以认为他疯了。\
**Beryl**: He has seen the fruition of his life's work, and it has driven him mad.

**贝丽尔**：但很快，清醒还是疯癫，这些都不再重要。\
**Beryl**: But mad or not, none of it will matter soon.

**贝丽尔**：我们所熟悉的巴黎，以及这个无序的浪漫时代，都将被冲刷殆尽。毁灭它的雨即将到来。\
**Beryl**: This whimsical era—along with the Paris we know—will be washed away in the coming rain.

**阿黛拉**：这太荒谬了！您竟然开这种玩笑！这根本……\
**Adèle**: Is this some kind of joke? Am I missing something?

**阿黛拉**：不可能……一场雨会带走一个时代……这种毫无道理的解释……\
**Adèle**: An era wiped out by a little rain? It doesn't make any sense.

**西莉亚**：……\
**Célia**: ...

**阿黛拉**：不，西莉亚……！\
**Adèle**: No, Célia!

**贝丽尔**：巴黎。\
**Beryl**: Paris—

**贝丽尔**：光之城，浪漫之城，充满象征与寓言的城市。\
**Beryl**: The city of light, of romance, and a tapestry of symbols.

**贝丽尔**：它不吝于展示其中混乱的激情、不同立场之间的倾轧、\
**Beryl**: Never shy in showing all manner of emotions—the chaotic passions of conflicting views, the conspiracies staged in her ancient alleys ...

在古老拥挤的巷子里上演的阴谋。

**贝丽尔**：因为它捍卫选择的权利。\
**Beryl**: Because she defends your right to choose. To scream or fall silent. To look back or forward. To live under a monarchy or republic. And all manner of thought ...

呼喊或沉默，怀旧的与现代的，君主制、共和制、令人眼花缭乱的主义……

**贝丽尔**：你尽可以投身其中，或一无所信。\
**Beryl**: You may throw yourself into the maelstrom or conjure up a new one yourself.

**阿黛拉**：那些学说、那些复杂的历史……她都记得很清楚，她比我更喜欢这片地方……\
**Adèle**: Célia loves this city so deeply. She knows everything about Paris, from the catacombs to the top of every tower.

**阿黛拉**：她那么认真……是最应该活下来的人……\
**Adèle**: Célia deserves to live, not me!

**阿黛拉**：为什么是西莉亚……？\
**Adèle**: Why? Why does Célia have to vanish?

**贝丽尔**：一座小径交叉的花园，它包容无数选择，允许每条岔路存在。\
**Beryl**: We stand in a vast garden surrounded by innumerable intersecting paths, welcoming endless forks, endless choices.

**贝丽尔**：那些思想流经每个人，变得具体可感。\
**Beryl**: Hernani, Notre Dame, the hot air balloons drifting above the Palais Saint-Pierre ... Philosophies find their form, passing lip to lip and heart to heart through all her residents.

《艾那尼》，圣母院，飘浮在圣皮埃尔宫上空的热气球……\
To regard fate and life with elegance and levity—that is the very spirit of Paris.

这是巴黎的灵魂，对命运和生活报以优雅而戏谑的审视。\
Where dreams and imaginings never fade—they stay with you across all times and eras, like a moveable feast.

它承载了过多的想象与幻梦，是一席流动的盛宴。\
Immortal. Indestructible.

绝不腐朽，无法焚毁。

**阿黛拉**：不……\
**Adèle**: No ...

**罗西教授**：我还需在这毫无意义的劣等世界里寻找什么呢？真正的世界已经降临！\
**Professor Roseau**: What more is there for me to seek in this meaningless, inferior world? The "true" world—the one that matters—has already descended!

**罗西教授**：那沉在宝库底部的湖水……令一切趋于完美……\
**Professor Roseau**: Voilà, see that? The clearest, most perfect water at the bottom of the Archive!

**罗西教授**：它就在……意识深处……在所有人的脑袋里！\
**Professor Roseau**: Now so close, almost within reach! In the deepest, most pristine layer of our joined consciousness!

Eternally real.\
Eternally imprinted in the mind.

**贝丽尔**：永恒真实。\
**贝丽尔**：永在你的脑海之中。

**贝丽尔**：迷思海的裂隙要关上了。“暴雨”正在修正谬误。\
**Beryl**: The rift is closing. The "Storm" will now correct the faults of this era.

**贝丽尔**：自天而降的光之城、不属于人世的幽灵、徘徊的野兽都会消失。\
**Beryl**: The City of Light descending from the sky, the phantoms walking among the living, and the legendary beasts roaming the streets—they will all vanish.

**贝丽尔**：疯人得偿所愿，剧目已至尾声，而失控的一切重归秩序的统治。\
**Beryl**: The mad have fulfilled their wish. The play has come to an end. Everything once in chaos will be brought back to order.

**？？？**：……不。\
**???**: No ...

**？？？**：贝丽尔……\
**???**: Beryl ...

一只手死死抓住了贝丽尔的脚踝。\
A hand clamps tight around Beryl's ankle.

**贝丽尔**：噢，你醒了。\
**Beryl**: Ah, you have awakened.

**贝丽尔**：也许你就这样睡着更好。能够躲开精神的痛苦。\
**Beryl**: Though perhaps it would be better to remain asleep. It may spare you some pain.

**费利西安**：我什么时候……躲躲藏藏……过！\
**Félicienne**: I ... I am no coward, Beryl!

她艰难地抽气，尽管空气与风都已无法从她消散的身体中灌进胸腔。\
She gasps, though no air, no wind, can fill what's left of her fading chest.

**费利西安**：贝丽尔，你必须——解决这些，快想办法！\
**Félicienne**: But you have to fix this! You have to do something!

**费利西安**：告诉我要怎么做？！\
**Félicienne**: Tell me how to change this, just a hint!

**费利西安**：我绝对不会为这种莫名其妙的——理由——消失！\
**Félicienne**: I refuse to vanish like this—to disappear after finally clawing my way back!

贝丽尔轻松地抬起脚，迈开步子。费利西安的手指猛然攥紧了一团空气。\
Beryl lifts her foot and steps forward without concern. Félicienne's fingers close desperately on empty air.

**费利西安**：应该去死的不是我，是那群蠢货！那群只知道舔统治者脚趾的庸人，甚至用不了神秘术的废物——\
**Félicienne**: Those worthless grovelers who can't even use arcane skills! They deserve to die, not me!

**费利西安**：这个世界本该属于我们——活下来的本该是我！\
**Félicienne**: This world belongs to us!

**费利西安**：贝丽尔·布翁尼！滚回来、别走——\
**Félicienne**: Don't you dare turn your back on me, Beryl Bouanich!

**费利西安**：我会向引导之人上报所有事！\
**Félicienne**: I will report every moment of this to the Guiding One!

远去的脚步声顿了顿。\
The retreating footsteps pause.

**费利西安**：你让劳伦·罗西去送死，我看到了……你别想装傻——\
**Félicienne**: I saw what you did to Laurent Roseau! You drove him to his death!

**费利西安**：你根本没有对任何人忠诚过，你是个见鬼的商人……贝丽尔……\
**Félicienne**: You've never been loyal to anyone! You're nothing but a soulless profiteer.

**费利西安**：除了自己的利益，你什么都不在乎……你从来没有真正认可过重塑之手的理念，也不想将世界带回那美好的时代——！\
**Félicienne**: You care for nothing! You never believed in any of the principles of Manus Vindictae! You never wanted to bring back the beautiful world we once had, did you?!

熟悉的脚步停在了她面前。\
The sound of familiar steps approaches again, stopping right in front of her.

**贝丽尔**：你真有趣。\
**Beryl**: How amusing.

**贝丽尔**：你有求于我，却选择威胁我。\
**Beryl**: You seek my help, yet accuse and threaten me in the same breath.

**贝丽尔**：如果对方想让你就此永远闭嘴呢？你怎么办，费利西安小姐？\
**Beryl**: Do you think you speak to me from a position of strength? What would you do if our positions were reversed, dear Félicienne?

她俯视着费利西安，像打量一只狼狈挣扎的珍稀动物。\
Beryl looks down at Félicienne as if examining a rare creature writhing in a deadly trap.

**费利西安**：……\
**Félicienne**: ...

**贝丽尔**：那么，就是这样了。\
**Beryl**: There is nothing more to say.

**贝丽尔**：能认识你，我十分荣幸。\
**Beryl**: It has been a pleasure, madame.

在贝丽尔起身前，费利西安终于颤抖着挤出微不可闻的句子。\
Before Beryl can move, Félicienne trembles out a faint, broken sentence.

**费利西安**：……\
**Félicienne**: ...

**贝丽尔**：嗯？\
**Beryl**: Hm?

**费利西安**：咕……\
**Félicienne**: Ugh ...

她低下头，喉头艰难地移动着。水珠从她的发梢上滴落，一直落到尘埃里去。\
She lowers her head, throat straining. Droplets slide from her hair and vanish into the dust.

**费利西安**：求……\
**Félicienne**: Please ...

**费利西安**：求你……贝丽尔……\
**Félicienne**: Please help me ... Beryl ...

**费利西安**：我不想……我不想死……！\
**Félicienne**: I ... I don't want to die ...!

**贝丽尔**：好的。\
**Beryl**: Very well.

贝丽尔点了点头，站直身子，提出了最后的问题。\
Beryl nods, straightens, and asks her final question.

但这次，她望向的是怔在原地的阿黛拉。\
But this time her translucent gaze settles on Adèle.

**贝丽尔**：你怎么想，阿黛拉？\
**Beryl**: What do you think, Adèle?

**贝丽尔**：你是否希望她以死偿还自己的过错？\
**Beryl**: Should she be saved or pay for what she has done with her life?

## AFF-19 英雄之旅 / The Hero's Journey

**阿黛拉**：看来您不想为其他人的性命负责。\
**Adèle**: Sounds like you're just trying to pass the burden onto me.

**阿黛拉**：您让我来决定，如果我拒绝，就是我杀了她。\
**Adèle**: Whether she lives or dies ... The weight ends up on my shoulders, doesn't it?

这个问题比预料中来得更直接。贝丽尔稍作思考，再次点头确认。\
The question is more direct than expected. Beryl thinks over the words, then nods again.

**贝丽尔**：你们的确很相似。关于那份求生的意志，以及一些面对命运的有趣反应。\
**Beryl**: In many ways you two are alike; neither of you can stand by as fate attempts to pull you down its path. You fight.

**贝丽尔**：正因为相似，费利西安才能持久地借用你的躯体，影响你的意识。\
**Beryl**: It is no wonder that she could reach into the depths of your mind.

**贝丽尔**：这样合适的机会再没有第二次了。\
**Beryl**: Now, her very existence is in your hands. You will not have another chance like this.

她向阿黛拉伸出手。\
She reaches out her hand.

**贝丽尔**：如果我没有猜错，你的朋友和曾经的费利西安死于同一个原因。此刻她应当回到了迷思海之中。\
**Beryl**: Your friend and the original Félicienne perished in the same way. It is likely, then, that she has returned to the Depths of Myth.

**贝丽尔**：留下费利西安，她会成为一个合适的研究对象，也许你能找到带回朋友的办法。\
**Beryl**: Should Félicienne live, she may become the key to discovering the truth of that realm. And in time, you may even find a way to bring your friend back.

**贝丽尔**：或让她以凶手的身份死去。往后的日子，你不必再受折磨。\
**Beryl**: Yet, should she die, you will have taken a fitting revenge, and her torment of your body will end at last.

**阿黛拉**：那……请您发誓吧。您承诺这些话都是真的。\
**Adèle**: Swear it, then. Swear that every word you just said is true.

一双恳切的眼睛，对上另一双平静而纯粹的眼睛。\
One pair of earnest eyes meets another, calm and unflinching.

**贝丽尔**：我无法承诺。\
**Beryl**: You ask for something beyond what I am capable of.

**贝丽尔**：你应该清楚，神秘术的能力是有限的。你无法鉴别一句话或一颗心的真伪，正如我此刻看不清命运的流向。\
**Beryl**: As you know, arcanum has its limits. There is no absolute way to prove one's intentions or words, just as I cannot see all ends as clearly as I once did.

**贝丽尔**：抓紧时间。把那颗钻石给我，或抛弃它。\
**Beryl**: Time is ticking. Give me the diamond now, or lose this opportunity forever.

阿黛拉犹豫着抬起胳膊。

费利西安没有再说话。也许她现在已不能开口。\
Adèle hesitates, then raises her arm.

她低着头，阿黛拉第一次见到她垂下头颅。\
Félicienne is silent, or perhaps she can no longer speak.

熟悉的、趾高气昂的神采从她身上消退了。\
She lowers her head. That proud defiance she once carried is gone.

烦躁、疲倦与无处着落的愤怒席卷而来。\
Irritation, exhaustion, and aimless rage wash over her. And in the end, it all becomes a sigh.

最终，它们变成一声叹息。

**阿黛拉**：……拿去吧。\
**Adèle**: ... Take it.

她能确信自己怨恨费利西安。但她也并不期望看到这样的屈服。\
Her resentment is still there, but somehow looking at her broken and pathetic, it awakens some pity in her.

**阿黛拉**：请您救她。\
**Adèle**: Save her.

钻石落入手心，贝丽尔合拢手掌。\
The diamond drops into Beryl's palm.

**贝丽尔**：多谢。\
**Beryl**: Thank you.

**贝丽尔**：你们为我找到了答案。我会拿出相应的诚意。\
**Beryl**: You have led me to the answer. I will respond with the sincerity it deserves.

**贝丽尔**：我说过很多次，你们的命运正在交汇。\
**Beryl**: As I have said before, your fates have converged.

**贝丽尔**：你在精神王国的旅途已经到了尽头……但仍然可以留在物质世界的王冠之中。\
**Beryl**: Félicienne, your journey through the spiritual realm has reached its end. But you still have a place in the crown of the material world.

**贝丽尔**：现在，到达世界尽头的灵性，该前往下一个世界了。\
**Beryl**: Now, the pneuma that has reached the edge of one world must begin anew in the next.

**贝丽尔**：收下它。\
**Beryl**: Take this, Adèle.

**贝丽尔**：作为你冒险之旅的勋章。\
**Beryl**: An accolade for your adventure.

**阿黛拉**：是吗……勋章。\
**Adèle**: Hah. An accolade?

钻石重新回到她的手中。\
It's back in her hand.

它带着血迹、温度、泪水。它是她最后唯一拥有的东西。\
Stained with blood, warm with tears, the last thing she still owns.

**阿黛拉**：谢谢您。\
**Adèle**: Thank you.

**阿黛拉**：但您的眼睛……\
**Adèle**: But your eyes ...

**贝丽尔**：不必担心。\
**Beryl**: Please do not worry yourself.

**贝丽尔**：就像你之前说的，我走在岸上太久，对这份注视水流的能力习以为常。\
**Beryl**: It seems I have walked this shoreline too long. I have grown too accustomed to watching its flow.

**贝丽尔**：自以为能看清命运，可能比他人更容易受命运摆弄。\
**Beryl**: The more I think I see through fate, the more vulnerable I become to it.

**贝丽尔**：所以我决定尽可能地看最后一次。就是这次了。\
**Beryl**: Still, I chose to watch one final time—just this once.

她笑着指了指阿黛拉握紧的钻石。\
She smiles and points to the diamond clutched in Adèle's hand.

**贝丽尔**：一个小小的“仿制品”。\
**Beryl**: It makes for a fine "imitation."

**贝丽尔**：你的火焰将法兰西之蓝与它暂时寄身的烟晶分离。\
**Beryl**: Your flame separated the French Blue from the smoky quartz it had inhabited.

**贝丽尔**：我只能为它另寻一副可寄宿的壳，希望你不介意白水晶制成的仿钻。\
**Beryl**: I simply gave it a new vessel—a clear quartz. It was the best that I could manage. I hope it will suffice.

**贝丽尔**：也希望你和费利西安都会满意它。\
**Beryl**: And I hope both you and Félicienne will be satisfied with it.

**阿黛拉**：她还会醒来吗？我还会像之前那样产生幻觉，看见她和我说话吗？\
**Adèle**: Will she wake up soon? And when that happens, will I still see her image in my hallucinations like before?

**贝丽尔**：不再有幻觉了。\
**Beryl**: You will suffer no more hallucinations.

**贝丽尔**：她会醒来，只是需要些时间。\
**Beryl**: And she will awaken again—in time.

**贝丽尔**：现在你是躯体，她是偷偷依附于你的精神。你们待在一起，她也许不会因灵与肉分离而被抹去。\
**Beryl**: Yet you will be the sole master of your body. She is but a soul quietly bound to it.

**贝丽尔**：所以别让她离你太远。否则这个小漏洞早晚会被发觉。\
**Beryl**: So long as neither of you strays too far from the other, her soul should remain whole.

钻石的棱角刺痛了手指。阿黛拉感到指尖的血管在抽动，连带着心脏一同拧紧。\
Its edges cut into her fingers. She feels the veins in her fingertips tighten, pulling at her heart.

一切诚如预言所示。\
Everything unfolds as foretold.

连这颗蓝钻也很好地履行了它命定的职责，纠缠着它的所有者，成为一个如影随形的诅咒。\
Even the French Blue fulfills its destined curse, entangling its bearer like a shadow.

**贝丽尔**：雨很快就会落下。该离开了。明天它的清洗便会完成。\
**Beryl**: The rain is about to fall. We must go. By dawn tomorrow, this world will be washed clean.

**贝丽尔**：我很喜欢你的结局。但是否要跟上，这是你的自由。\
**Beryl**: I must admit, I enjoyed this ending of yours. But whether you continue to the next chapter is up to you.

当戏剧落幕，观众也该适时离场。\
But when the show ends, the audience must leave.

贝丽尔一直遵守着这套规则，她不打算为谁改变习惯。\
Beryl has always obeyed that rule, and she is not about to change.

**阿黛拉**：——贝丽尔女士！\
**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich!

**阿黛拉**：贝丽尔女士，您知道那个说法吗？\
