**Adèle**: Madame Bouanich, forgive me, do you know the theory of evolution?

**阿黛拉**：人类的祖先是猿猴。我们都是由猴子进化而来。\
**Adèle**: Humankind evolved from apes. I don't understand the science, but, in short, we all came from monkeys.

**阿黛拉**：那么世界上第一只猴子从何而来？它最远的祖先是谁？\
**Adèle**: But then, where did that monkey come from? Are we all just a copy of a copy of some ancient thing?

**阿黛拉**：再往回推算呢？世界上最早的生命是如何诞生的？\
**Adèle**: And if we keep tracing back, how did life even begin on Earth?

**阿黛拉**：像这样不断溯源，能找到“最初的生命”吗？\
**Adèle**: Can we ever find that original spark of life? Is it even possible?

**贝丽尔**：……\
**Beryl**: ...

**阿黛拉**：您看，有许多事情都无法找出那个所谓的、唯一的、完全准确的决定因素。\
**Adèle**: What I'm trying to say is, things rarely have a single clear cause.

**阿黛拉**：生命的诞生很复杂，受到许多条件的影响。\
**Adèle**: The birth of life is complex. It can be influenced by all kinds of factors.

**阿黛拉**：我觉得命运也是同样。\
**Adèle**: Maybe that applies to fate as well.

**阿黛拉**：还没到结束的时候呢。\
**Adèle**: So, whatever happens, I don't intend for my story to end any time soon.

朋友、家乡、诅咒或预言，她曾有的期待与抗拒，都被一场雨变得不再重要。\
Friends, home, curses, prophecies ... Everything she's ever hoped for or fought to achieve means nothing against the rain.

如果眼前只剩这个解释，只有先抓住它。\
If only one explanation remains, she'll seize it.

即使这只是一根轻飘飘的蛛丝。\
Even if it's just a fragile thread of silk.

**阿黛拉**：请您带上我。告诉我该怎么躲过您口中的“暴雨”！\
**Adèle**: Please, take me with you. There must be a way to avoid this "Storm" you spoke of!

她喊出了这句话——塔沃尼尔的诅咒或许已经触发。\
She shouts—the Tavernier Curse may already be in motion.

这就是命运安排的目标。一个值得为之而死的目标。\
This is the goal fate intended. A goal worth dying for. The rain washes everything away, ending her long wait.

雨水带走了一切，也终止了漫长的等待。\
As ordinary life fades away, her adventure truly begins.

在熟悉的生活被碾磨殆尽之后，她的冒险真正开始了。

**阿黛拉**：我可以为您寻找您想要的宝石、答案、一切东西！\
**Adèle**: I'll help you find jewels in return—answers, anything! Whatever it is you seek!

**贝丽尔**：作为报酬，你想从我这儿得到什么呢？\
**Beryl**: A generous offer. To honor your sincerity, I shall give you an answer. What is it you wish to know?

**阿黛拉**：“暴雨”的真相。\
**Adèle**: The truth about the "Storm."

她立刻给出了答案。\
She answers without hesitation.

**阿黛拉**：我只想弄明白它，让我的朋友和……费利西安回来。\
**Adèle**: I need to understand it so I can bring back my friends.

**贝丽尔**：费利西安？\
**Beryl**: Including Félicienne?

**阿黛拉**：她的结局不该在这里。只是消失，对她来说……太轻松了。\
**Adèle**: I wouldn't call her a friend. But for her to simply vanish, hmph, that's just too merciful for her.

占卜师听完了每一个字，点了点头。\
The diviner listens to every word, then nods.

**贝丽尔**：即使最后可能一无所获，你也要和我一起离开吗？\
**Beryl**: Would you still accompany me, knowing we may gain nothing in the end?

**阿黛拉**：是的。\
**Adèle**: I would.

**阿黛拉**：总不能干等着糟糕的事发生，对吧？\
**Adèle**: You can't just sit around waiting for something terrible to happen, can you?

那条躲藏许久的小龙攀上她的肩膀，吐出一枚火球。\
The little dragon climbs onto her shoulder and spits out a fireball.

**贝丽尔**：是。而且，每个时代都不会缺少追逐宝石与水晶的客人。\
**Beryl**: Indeed. I suppose there will never be an age lacking those who chase gemstones and answers about their fate.

**贝丽尔**：我的店里还缺一名能找到珍贵宝石的员工。\
**Beryl**: Perhaps a jewel hunter is exactly what my little establishment needs.

**阿黛拉**：我们该往哪儿去，贝丽尔女士？\
**Adèle**: Which way do we go, Madame Bouanich?

**贝丽尔**：往前开。穿过人群，离开这里。\
**Beryl**: Forward. Through the crowd.

**贝丽尔**：我会为你找出那条正确的道路。\
**Beryl**: Allow me to guide you.

**阿黛拉**：为您服务，女士。\
**Adèle**: I'm just glad to be of service, madame.

**阿黛拉**：旅途愉快。\
**Adèle**: I hope you have a pleasant journey.

贝丽尔最后望了一眼狂欢的人群。\
Beryl takes a final wistful look at the revelers.

这座城市只是她用于安放自己的地方，一个盛放珍贵水晶的珠宝盒。\
This city is just the place where she keeps herself, a jewelry box made to hold a precious crystal.

但她还是愿意再花些时间记住它——这一点儿时间，已经足够了。\
Still, she decides to remember it—just a little longer. That's enough.

她靠在副驾驶，闭上眼睛。\
She leans back in the passenger seat and closes her eyes.

**贝丽尔**：接下来的很长时间里，我应该无法提供过去那样详细准确的占卜了。\
**Beryl**: For a long while going forward, I may not be able to divine with the same precision I once had.

**贝丽尔**：但“看不见”的感觉比想象中要好。\
**Beryl**: Yet this feeling of "not seeing" has a comfort of its own.

**贝丽尔**：如果的确有某个掌管命运的存在，我想祂也许是个瞎子。\
**Beryl**: If our fate truly is guided by a higher being, I must imagine they are blind.

车载收音机的歌声开始流淌。\
The radio begins to play.

**贝丽尔**：希望我醒来的时候，你已经到达了目的地。\
**Beryl**: I hope that, when I awake, you will have reached your destination.

## AFF-20 平凡的日子 / In Ordinary Times

**执夜人**：让我确认一下，也就是说……第五次“暴雨”是重塑之手导致的灾难。你就是他们罪行的证人。\
**Vigil Officer**: So, let me get this straight: The fifth "Storm" was brought forth by Manus Vindictae, and you witnessed the process firsthand.

**执夜人**：但贝丽尔·布翁尼与重塑之手没有任何关系。\
**Vigil Officer**: Based on your testimony, Ms. Beryl Bouanich wasn't an accomplice of the Manus, and she even saved your life.

她是救了你的恩人。

**灰调蓝**：没错。\
**Brume**: Yes.

黑镜中雾气退去，露出了受审者清晰的模样——她所言非虚。\
The mist clears from the black mirror, revealing the witness beneath—it was never a lie.

**执夜人**：……\
**Vigil Officer**: ...

**执夜人**：之后发生了什么？\
**Vigil Officer**: And after that? What happened?

**灰调蓝**：我按布翁尼女士说的，来到了能够躲避那场“暴雨”的避难所。\
**Brume**: I followed Madame Bouanich's advice and made it to a shelter that could resist the "Storm."

**灰调蓝**：路上雨越下越大，但幸好我们及时赶到了。\
**Brume**: The rain got heavier and heavier along the way, but thankfully, we made it there just in time.

**灰调蓝**：只是我那辆小车里来不及、也没办法装下更多人。\
**Brume**: It's such a shame my little cab didn't have room for anyone else.

**灰调蓝**：……现在远方仍有一座巴黎城，但那里已经不是我的故乡了。\
**Brume**: I know that there's still a Paris out there, but it's no longer my Paris.

**灰调蓝**：我珍视的一切都被命运的洪流吞没……哈，就和那个预言一模一样。\
**Brume**: Everything I loved there was washed away in the rain. Heh, just as the prophecy said.

她用一声轻笑为这场讲述画上了句号，小房间内安静了一会儿。\
The storyteller caps her story with a bitter laugh, leaving the room quiet.

**灰调蓝**：接下来的事情你们已经都知道了。\
**Brume**: And the rest ... you already know.

**灰调蓝**：多亏布翁尼女士的帮助，我才没有流落街头。\
**Brume**: Thanks to Madame Bouanich, I wasn't left on the streets alone.

**灰调蓝**：那些我曾熟悉的街道和人都变了，但幸好我的车还在身边。\
**Brume**: The neighborhoods I knew, the people I once recognized—they've all changed. But at least I have my car.

**灰调蓝**：比起呆在安全的住处里悠哉度日，我还是更喜欢上街兜兜风。\
**Brume**: In any case, I still prefer driving the streets to staying in some cozy room.

**灰调蓝**：布翁尼女士因为工作关系，常需要到处跑，我在那之后就一直跟在她边上帮忙。\
**Brume**: Madame Bouanich's work keeps her on the move, so I've been helping her since then.

**灰调蓝**：前段时间我还和她一起去了一趟德里，帮她卖掉手里的黄水晶……对了，我还在那里认识了她的女儿玛蒂尔达。\
**Brume**: We even went to Delhi to sell her topazes. Oh, and I met her daughter there—Matilda.

**灰调蓝**：她们母女的性格真是完全两样，玛蒂尔达小姐把什么都写在脸上。必须说，我和她更合得来。\
**Brume**: She's nothing like her mother. Everything she feels is written plainly on her face. To be honest, I get along better with her.

**灰调蓝**：不过布翁尼女士和我刚认识她那时候相比，也有了不小的变化。\
**Brume**: Madame Bouanich ... She's changed, too.

说到这里，她顿了顿。\
She pauses.

**灰调蓝**：我觉得……她变得更像是个活人了。\
**Brume**: She feels more real now. More alive.

谈话又持续了一段时间才宣告结束。待节奏匀整的脚步声远去，房间内归于寂静。\
Their conversation continues for some time before ending, until, after the sound of departing footsteps, silence returns.

**副手**：……看来贝丽尔·布翁尼没有问题，至少她亲自带回来的这位幸存者一无所知。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: It seems Ms. Bouanich is in the clear, based on the witness's testimony.

**副手**：她这几年一直跟在布翁尼的身边，如果布翁尼有什么可疑的地方，不太可能瞒得过她。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: She claims Beryl Bouanich saved her and has remained at her side for years. If there were anything suspicious going on, she would've noticed.

**黑鹮**：这可不好说。\
**Black Ibis**: Hmm. I wouldn't be so sure.

声音来自房间中被阴影笼罩的角落，整场问询中，他的这位上司都始终保持着沉默。\
A voice comes from the shadowed corner. Throughout the inquiry, his superior has kept silent.

**副手**：你不相信测谎仪的结果？这可是最新的仪器。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: You don't trust the lie detector results? Isn't this the most advanced, top-of-the-line model?

**黑鹮**：机器总会出错，我更相信自己的直觉。\
**Black Ibis**: Advanced or not, machines can fail. I prefer to trust my instincts.

执夜人从阴影中走出，来到方桌旁，伸手敲了敲桌面上那台价格不菲的“最新仪器”。\
Black Ibis steps out from the dark, rapping her knuckles on that costly "top-of-the-line model" on the table.

**黑鹮**：她一定有所隐瞒。\
**Black Ibis**: And mine are telling me—she's hiding something.

**副手**：关于第五次“暴雨”中发生的事吗？\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: About the fifth "Storm"?

**黑鹮**：也包括如今布翁尼忽然旧事重提的原因。\
**Black Ibis**: That, and the fact that Madame Bouanich returned so abruptly.

**黑鹮**：第九次“暴雨”后，她毫无征兆地失踪，谁也找不到她的下落……可谁能想到呢？\
**Black Ibis**: After the ninth "Storm," she vanished without a trace. Who would've thought—

**黑鹮**：她居然就这样若无其事地回来了——带着一条“不得了的消息”。\
**Black Ibis**: She would stroll back in out of nowhere, acting as if nothing happened, with some "big revelation" in hand.

空洞的走廊里徒立着一个人，本该一片寂静。\
The corridor is empty but for one still figure.

**耳畔的声音**：太蹩脚了，你犯了不止一个错误。\
**Voice in Head**: Unbelievable. One sloppy mistake after another.

**耳畔的声音**：你简直就要把“我在说谎”写在脸上了。要不是我，你早就被抓包了。\
**Voice in Head**: You'd have been less conspicuous if you'd just written "liar" all over your face. You should count yourself lucky I covered for you.

灰调蓝本不打算理会，但那个声音喋喋不休。\
Brume hadn't planned to answer, but the voice is incessant.

**灰调蓝**：……你是要我感谢你吗，费利西安？\
**Brume**: Are you expecting a thank you from me, Félicienne?

**灰调蓝**：别以为我不知道，你只是不想自己的事暴露给基金会而已。\
**Brume**: Don't think I don't know. You just don't want your own secrets exposed.

**灰调蓝**：不要在圣洛夫基金会的设施里和我说话，谁能保证没有人在监视我们？\
**Brume**: And didn't I tell you to stop talking to me like this while we're on Foundation grounds? Who knows who might be eavesdropping on us?

**费利西安**：你不把话说出口我也能够听到，就像现在这样。\
**Félicienne**: And I told you that I can hear you perfectly well without you mouthing the words. Is that really so hard to understand?

这是什么很难的事吗？

**灰调蓝**：万一我下意识地露出破绽了呢？\
**Brume**: And if I slip up subconsciously?

**灰调蓝**：毕竟我不像你，压根就没有嘴了，所以没有这个烦恼。\
**Brume**: I suppose you might have forgotten what it feels like to have a mouth.

左手处传来一声冷哼，沿着骨骼攀至脑中。\
A cold snort crawls from her left hand up through her arm and rattles around her skull.

**费利西安**：我发现你对我越来越无礼了，但对那个女人倒是乖顺得很。\
**Félicienne**: Always so rude to me, while you offer nothing but praise and fawning to that woman.

**费利西安**：我告诉过你，和我一起去面见引导之人才是你最好的归宿——你不听。\
**Félicienne**: You ought to have listened to me—gone to meet the Guiding One and pledged your loyalty. But you didn't because you are, and always have been, a stubborn fool.

**费利西安**：如果你选择投靠基金会也就罢了。最多是见识浅薄，看不清局势，犯了和所有乌合之众一样的错误。\
**Félicienne**: Fine. Side with the Foundation if you want. Call it ignorance, call it shortsightedness—should I expect anything less from such rabble?

**费利西安**：——可你偏偏把所有注都下在那个女人的身上！\
**Félicienne**: But staking our lives on that woman? That is something far more than simply foolish! Do you really trust her so much?

真是个疯子，你就那么相信她？

脑海中的怒骂未能激起预想中的激烈辩驳。\
The complaining voice in her head receives a curt reply.

**灰调蓝**：……我相信贝丽尔女士，因为她是我最好的选择。\
**Brume**: I do. I believe in Madame Bouanich.

**灰调蓝**：她的判断是对的，时机到了。\
**Brume**: She'll prove I made the right choice.

房门被敲响。间隔几秒后，门内传来幕僚长的回应。\
A knock on the door. A pause. The chief of staff's voice from within.

**Z**：哪位？\
**Z**: Who is it?

**维尔汀**：是我，维尔汀。我想询问外勤申请的审批进度。\
**Vertin**: It's me, Vertin. I've come to check on the status of my field mission application.

**维尔汀**：能耽误您一些时间吗？\
**Vertin**: Is now not a good time?

往常这扇门总是会第一时间为她打开，但这次她却等待得稍久了些。\
Usually the door opens right away, but this time she waits a little longer.

**Z**：请进，维尔汀。\
**Z**: Please. Come in, Vertin.

推门而入，来宾用的革质沙发上正坐着一个陌生的身影。\
She pushes it open. A stranger sits on the guest sofa.

**贝丽尔**：我们终于见面了，维尔汀。玛蒂尔达常提起你。\
**Beryl**: We finally meet, Ms. Vertin. Matilda has told me much about you.

同窗的名字唤起了记忆，面前女子精致的五官与另一张更加生气勃勃的面孔重叠在了一起。\
The name of an old classmate resurfaces. The woman's refined features blur with another livelier face.

**维尔汀**：您是……贝丽尔·布翁尼女士？\
**Vertin**: Then you must be Madame Beryl Bouanich?

**贝丽尔**：看来我们能省去自我介绍环节了。\
**Beryl**: I see we can skip the formalities.

她的笑容柔和而亲切，眼里却没有带上同样的笑意。\
Her smile is warm and gentle, but her eyes don't match.

**贝丽尔**：你也曾见过金色的纺线，对吗？\
**Beryl**: You have seen the golden thread, have you not?

迁 流 的 盛 宴

A F l o w i n g F e a s t
